许昌

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　苏籀从祖父习《春秋》，颇通义例，亦曾闻祖父《易》论，苏辙作诗示诸孙，赞苏籀等少年力学。<br /><a href="javascript: 陕县

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　张耒卒，苏籀有诗留题张诗卷。作品：《题张公文潜诗卷一首》<div id='poem_139794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139794'>杕杜尝嗤点，椒兰足陷倾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139794'>穷途乖党侣，陋屋挂冠缨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139794'>彰炳流千载，嗟咨奠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>两楹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139794'>桑枌堕兵火，简札落寰瀛。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139794'>态度云霞蔚，瑰奇珠玉生。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139794'>渊停真可挹，川驶不留行。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139794'>机杼班扬旧，笙竽陶谢并。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139794'>百末芳蜂采，千岐理刃迎。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139794_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139794'>斧斤皆阁束，凿枘自天成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139865'>乃公振旅来，河湟新奏捷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139865'>诗礼壮斋坛，荆州初妥帖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139865'>王郎赋缁衣，旦暮刷燕越。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139865'>从容挽六钧，邂逅记三箧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139865'>赏奇必先睹，语怪尤欣惬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139865'>樵径曳斑杖，僧窗敷白氎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139865'>解颐千虑却，爬痒众宾厌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139865'>辕门熊虎士，铁面竦长鬣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139865'>椎牛赴大釂，割肉挥长铗。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139865'>酸寒商公邑，会我萦仕牒。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139865'>儿嗥羹不糁，女瘦裙剩摺。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139865'>嫉邪发冲冠，忧国须屡镊。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139865'>侯家有美载，寒冬相煖热。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139865'>騕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>袅带青萍，于菟包璅甲。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139865'>风磴好扶轮，冰溪多病涉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139865'>凄凉熊耳下，小雪轻尘浥。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139865'>升堂语君公，浚治千楼堞。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139865'>勉勉足兵食，孜孜抚疲苶。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139865'>政成在简易，可大贤人业。<div id='poem_sentence_18_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_139865'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_139865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_139865'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_139865_0'>⑴ 原作偠，据粤雅堂本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_139865_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　在陕州任仪曹掾。作品：《二松赋》《牡丹赋》<div id='poem_1236917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二松赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236917")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236917'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236917'>商邑岩岩，群山环中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236917_comment'></div>膏液外凑，英灵内钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236917_comment'></div>其人黄绮，其植曰松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236917_comment'></div>翘翘我室，契阔朋从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236917_comment'></div>二友忘言，冉冉秋冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236917_comment'></div>古之遗直，本钜末丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236917_comment'></div>尺寸非可较量，绳墨非可究穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236917_comment'></div>凛凛乎其可严惮也，如见大宾，如承大祭，形魄竦动，圭璋卬颙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236917_comment'></div>矫矫乎其能励操也，如首阳之二贤，齐鲁之两翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236917_comment'></div>石忘其坚，山失其穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236917_comment'></div>确乎其不可拔也，如辞位之泰伯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236917_comment'></div>邈乎其不可攀也，如忧世之元龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236917_comment'></div>炎曦郁攸，金铁销镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236917_comment'></div>冰合九河，雪屯万峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236917_comment'></div>毛发磔磔，不改声容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236917_comment'></div>如蔺子完璧，怒发冠冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236917_comment'></div>睢阳蔽江，张髯乘墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236917_comment'></div>天籁嗥鸣，非鼓非钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236917_comment'></div>生三伏之栗冽，时一警于昏聋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236917_comment'></div>若洞庭之乐，钧天之奏，均节跌荡，他乐莫同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236917_comment'></div>斲而支太室之坏，辑而营灵台之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236917_comment'></div>如良弼之用舍，系此邦之替隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236917_comment'></div>虽然，待雨露而茂遂，积岁月而强雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236917_comment'></div>世俗尚得而企仰，蛇鼠谬托于蔽蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236917_comment'></div>孰知其筋干鳞甲，非特据地而摩空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236917_comment'></div>犹龙变化，乘云高踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236917_comment'></div>排阴助阳，追日回风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236917_comment'></div>超乎六合之表，出乎造化之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236917_comment'></div>遗琥珀与茯苓，贻俞跗与仓公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236917_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236917_comment'></div>世人欲速，种柳与枫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236917_comment'></div>菌生朽壤，蔓延楚丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236917_comment'></div>惟二友之不凡，爱正命于厥躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236917_comment'></div>相与吟啸而作，殆其莫逆于胸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1236917_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>牡丹赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236915")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236915'>河洛之神，权舆此奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236915_comment'></div>何夜半之有力，刻朝新之琼枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236915_comment'></div>麟角凤觜之续，不足以为固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236915_comment'></div>投觚削鐻之割，不足以为机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236915_comment'></div>砂点铁以成金，青出蓝而过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236915_comment'></div>何造物之钩距，盖三昧之密施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236915_comment'></div>候琯裁动，枯蘖先知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236915_comment'></div>巉然擢珊瑚之巨，郁然饮沆瀣之滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236915_comment'></div>无揠苗以助长，忌蚤华而中衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236915_comment'></div>丛干渐老，开花及时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236915_comment'></div>挥琼尺以裁绡，缕金钿而镂衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236915_comment'></div>妆未了而半就，情欲吐而犹疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236915_comment'></div>发精神于雨露，借光气于虹霓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236915_comment'></div>凤刿羽而初下，鹤敛翅而未飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236915_comment'></div>如误入于金谷，似迩沿于芗溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236915_comment'></div>候晨光而洁鲜，怯午景而低徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236915_comment'></div>初含喜以浓笑，忽微怒而自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236915_comment'></div>缭以画阑，障以罗帏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236915_comment'></div>暗淡月采，空濛烟霏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236915_comment'></div>有美一人，艳无等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236915_comment'></div>缥缈金菊之裳，娟婵蛾绿之眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236915_comment'></div>若夫紫殿龙楼，金台彤池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236915_comment'></div>封黄蜡以入贡，乘汗血而绝驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236915_comment'></div>天颜一解，四海光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236915_comment'></div>念其向日，远过蜀葵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236915_comment'></div>太平佳瑞，许配灵芝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236915_comment'></div>至于箕、颍之间，林下水湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236915_comment'></div>晔乎满目，野夫所窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236915_comment'></div>我方铁石其肝胆，枯槁其形仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236915_comment'></div>岂造物之见试，示绰约之妍姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236915_comment'></div>为汝一笑而引满，心亦无成而无亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236915_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1236915_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='52e7d520a42e473eb253579bad26db51_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("52e7d520a42e473eb253579bad26db51");'><span id='52e7d520a42e473eb253579bad26db51_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>任谅为陕西转运副使，荐苏籀入幕。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在陕西转运司幕中。与咸阳令、何子应、陈叔易等人游。作品：《咸阳令求清渭楼诗，和何子应长句》<div id='poem_139858' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139858' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139858?labeling=true' target='_blank'>咸阳县令求清渭楼诗和何子应长句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139858")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139858_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139858'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139858'>秦如蒹葭未饱霜，四维不举空豪强。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139858'>神疲鬼乏赴功利，兆自襄公终始皇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139858'>富极薰天力斡地，诸侯西来谁敢当。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139858'>范雎李斯乘利势，蒙骜白起先戎行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139858'>韩卢前奔宋鹊举，角逐海内如驱羊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139858'>干戈取之刑法治，举事夸淫惟快意。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139858'>时移数尽非徒然，直笔汗青遭唾毁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139858'>咸阳宫殿无尺瓦，直抵南山是禾稼。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139858'>山巅观<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>阙总成尘，清渭东流无昼夜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139858'>昔时此水贯宫垣，今日沦涟县楼下。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139858'>无复秦娥洗妆水，时有村童饮牛马。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139858'>秋波泠泠泛红叶，春天波荡桃花节。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139858'>清名不与世荣辱，混浊何尝妨至洁。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139858'>八川分流皆异态，七泽胸中无芥蒂。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139858'>直须面面倚危栏，殚睹雍州原野火。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139858'>楼中有客雍门弹，坐上悲歌击樽坏。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139858'>何侯精采如琳琅，携诗揖我谓我臧。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139858'>我今为子登楼赋，书版一讽悲兴亡。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139858'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_139858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_139858'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_139858_0'>⑴ 原作冠，据粤雅堂本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_139858_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b4b59d8e13d745c4ae5acb3e87d8e8cd_label'><a href='javascript: -----title
咸阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8cab5494c8d4455791810f3a6adb6c62_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8cab5494c8d4455791810f3a6adb6c62");'><span id='8cab5494c8d4455791810f3a6adb6c62_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　与咸阳令、何子应、陈叔易等人游。作品：《次韵陈叔易远别离三首》<div id='poem_139827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵陈叔易远别离三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139827")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139827'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139827'>昼短宵未明，何朝妾觌君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139827'>泪滴九霄雨，愁凝千古云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139827'>凤藏丹霄晚，鸿遵沙碛远。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139827'>楼迥眼波穷，轴折离魂断。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139827'>安得葛陂龙，肉骨丹九转。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139827'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_139827_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139826' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139826' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139826?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139826'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139826'>妇慧弗谙事，谓世无离索。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139826'>洋洋旧依蒲，逐逐难翳藿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139826'>冲风递弱羽，烂漫何乡落。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139826'>忧端埒南山，那堪鲁酒薄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139826'>人力末如何，天公良可托。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139826'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_139826_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139825?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139825'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139825'>别情荼无苦，诀语若为道。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139825'>日近长安遥，山围烟浪绕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139825'>星河通故都，冰雪迫凋槁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139825'>回辕尚茫茫，延颈空矫矫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139825'>卜归付乾策，此策何人抱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139825'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_139825_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
临潼
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='183aacea71f94d44afd357cd4abbc187_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("183aacea71f94d44afd357cd4abbc187");'><span id='183aacea71f94d44afd357cd4abbc187_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>，29岁</div><div id='183aacea71f94d44afd357cd4abbc187' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　游华清池。作品：《汤泉赋》<div id='poem_1236916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汤泉赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236916")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236916'>陕西南坤，泉滃山涧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236916_comment'></div>崖谷焦烈，滚沸奔猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236916_comment'></div>汤池烝雾，腾泻浩汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236916_comment'></div>客曰：「异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236916_comment'></div>水在万物，其性必寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236916_comment'></div>胡然郁攸，无事烧燔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236916_comment'></div>草木烁烂，凫鸭煨燖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236916_comment'></div>汇为澄泓，而后可探。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236916_comment'></div>诘其从来，莫克考原」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236916_comment'></div>余盖知之，《易》有太极，是生两仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236916_comment'></div>风金火轮，世界执持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236916_comment'></div>火光生于巨海，波涛涌于汀岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236916_comment'></div>熔石成水，敲石成焰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236916_comment'></div>三伏炎曦，温暾河汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236916_comment'></div>百井隆冬，其气自暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236916_comment'></div>吾侪习俗，沦溺情见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236916_comment'></div>煮鼎负薪，而后晨爨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236916_comment'></div>欲穷理而尽性，至中和以推原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236916_comment'></div>徇耳目之寻常，昧造化之机关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236916_comment'></div>是犹火鼠不信冰蚕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236916_comment'></div>石中之火，火中斯泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236916_comment'></div>坎离相济，为汤固然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236916_comment'></div>此山岳之仁气，悯寒士之枯朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236916_comment'></div>假温慈而惠和，以洗浣其尘垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236916_comment'></div>使于斯而产金玉，终何益于野叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236916_comment'></div>惟荒山与乱石，无华堂与琼甃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236916_comment'></div>免污亡国，华清贵妃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236916_comment'></div>嬿婉之求，无取于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236916_comment'></div>予槁项黄馘，短发葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236916_comment'></div>青鞋直趋，老栉自随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236916_comment'></div>头轻目明，弹冠振衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236916_comment'></div>咏而风乎，配鲁之沂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1236916_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eee3ef4a56614ba68873399f60dc7d92_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eee3ef4a56614ba68873399f60dc7d92");'><span id='eee3ef4a56614ba68873399f60dc7d92_link' id='poem_sentence_4_139790'>愿以丝毫裨汉室，岂无弓矢毙胡星。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139790'>愚翁事业空遗臭，经义分明战血腥。<div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139658'><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（粤雅堂本作香）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139658'>梅雨闻君醉山阁，麦风招我步濠梁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139658'>惜春岁月那相贷，肠断连山草树长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139658'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139658_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月</a>　金人攻逼东京，宋遣使请和，金责以金银布帛，割太原、中山、河间三镇，宋皆许之。苏籀作咏史诗讽之。作品：《避地咏史一首》<div id='poem_139781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>避地咏史一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139781")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139781'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139781'>量力难贪督亢图，冯亭致地祸来欤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139781'>摸金公子驱长戟，割地先生醉堕车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139781'>乘传有人延剧孟，运筹何术困由余。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139781'>鬼方政赖高宗克，雅信周公无逸书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139781'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139781_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

武汉

<div class='label1' id='b65472098fec4278b6125cdb29408493_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b65472098fec4278b6125cdb29408493");'><span id='b65472098fec4278b6125cdb29408493_link' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游寒溪次醅字韵题九曲亭一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139883")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139883'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139883'>幅巾戏漉彭泽醅，尺书间觅来禽栽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139883'>招揖西山与东鲁，回首阊阖并玉台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139883'>标榜高甍方外景，不染时世毫端埃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139883'>倚空千重翡翠盖，落日万顷琉璃堆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139883'>兴酣鱼鸟安乐国，喜溢仆驭陶家罍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139883'>惜哉二老削旧迹，不论石上并墙隈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139883'>埼岸横舟昔时处，刻划独免漫苍苔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139883'>梵刹青莲旧僧社，径遂几合无人开。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139883'>方今九原如可作，足使四海无凋摧。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139883'>封章千载垂可否，玉堂黄閤犹儋雷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139883'>精义穷神致实用，不变生死无去来。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139883'>天下书生践遗迹，棠荫处处思贤哀。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139883'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_139883_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='09db6861625543a28f46bf10e54e027a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("09db6861625543a28f46bf10e54e027a");'><span id='09db6861625543a28f46bf10e54e027a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1129')">1128-1129年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='09db6861625543a28f46bf10e54e027a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　苏迟改知婺州，苏籀从居。作品：《去年一首》<div id='poem_139808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>去年一首<span class='inlineComment2'>（此篇原缺，据明抄本补）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139808")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139808'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139808'>去年胡来清水岩，黄河狭隘冬凌顽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139808'>戾如飘风速如鬼，犬豕淫虐豺狼贪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139808'>探马星奔汗流地，猛士眦裂发指冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139808'>潼雍见兵不及万，半阙甲胄屯河边。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139808'>隆寒身体例皲瘃，亦复勉强横戈鋋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139808'>它司金缯封雍府，犒军纸袄如泥钱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139808'>胡人隔水相笑侮，杀身于尔何值焉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139808'>同州告急唇齿喻，无兵赴救诚难旃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139808'>元戎钤下兵八百，苍头厮养争后先。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139808'>鄜延诏发五千骑，此日收兵姑自全。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139808'>平时保甲例乌合，县符迫促挥空拳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139808'>甚哉田夫无斗志，一夕惊走如穷<span class='inlineComment2'>（粤雅堂本作寒）</span>烟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139808'>汉将苍黄结旌遁，虏骑势合弥山川。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139808'>关中控弦诚万骑，忠臣义士力可宣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139808'>书生命运亦蹇劣，我师疲少邻敌坚。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139808'>却忆长安无事日，谈及祸乱为尤愆。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139808'>饭囊酒瓮誇厚福，捧土揭木皆才贤。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139808'>生灵未悉坐何罪，髓脑涂地尤苍天。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139808'>天公诚能祐戎虏，岂复不解兴中原。<div id='poem_sentence_18_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_139808'>案图戎索八百郡，我邦日蹙知谁怜。<div id='poem_sentence_19_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_139808'>吴中据江恃舟楫，惴惴慄慄聊偷安。<div id='poem_sentence_20_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_139808'>旅人流徙隘城郭，岁事寒薄理势然。<div id='poem_sentence_21_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_139808'>去年往矣不须问，安枕而卧祈来年。<div id='poem_sentence_22_139808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_139808'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_139808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　上书户部尚书叶梦得。作品：《上户部尚书》<div id='poem_1236961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上户部尚书书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236961")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236961'>籀闻建邦犹之作室，其成也非一木之所支，及其毁也非一绳之所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236961_comment'></div>昔者海内太平，规模远而基扃固，群材各胜其任，实实枚枚，贯百世而无敝，飘风暴雨不足虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236961_comment'></div>虽有匠庆，亦当袖手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236961_comment'></div>不幸蠹蚀蚁漏，栋梁不具，而榱桷欹侧，或不察焉，则摧堕圮裂，至于不可支梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236961_comment'></div>于是命工考室，以还旧观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236961_comment'></div>此虽劬疚辛苦，而亦功名之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236961_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236961_comment'></div>非良工师，何足以预于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236961_comment'></div>天下之材，乐育附辑而来，出其端良雄杰，而绳其挠腐拳曲，规矩斧削，可以无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236961_comment'></div>斲丧衰颓之后，妙手尤不易逢，珍材亦不易致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236961_comment'></div>使拙工率意为之，必将截榆以擎承露之槃，折柳以樊狂夫之圃，岂不殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236961_comment'></div>今兹天下涂炭，夷狄交侵，以安社稷生灵为心，持衡尺以正百工，此考室之师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236961_comment'></div>阁下负超然绝异之姿，挟出于形器之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236961_comment'></div>咺赫蚤闻，年如公瑾破乌林之岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236961_comment'></div>硕大尊显，功业先乎祖生而著鞭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236961_comment'></div>于时天下宁谧，伏猎状杜之徒，忌嫉高贤，故淹翔符鱼节钺之任，而卷怀埏陶烹斡之才，滞留畿辅，渔钓江湖者凡十馀祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236961_comment'></div>顾当途皆血指汗颜者，亦预知其误国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236961_comment'></div>一旦有警，事棼如丝，呼吸生变，战守之计未决，邻敌之情难料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236961_comment'></div>四海六合之大，化强狡而安反侧，喻日新之德意，求其识略宏达，尺纸片言可以排难解纷，万举万全而无遗筹失策者，在庭其谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236961_comment'></div>中外始有才难之叹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236961_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「絺兮绤兮，凄其以风」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236961_comment'></div>言庸人不可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236961_comment'></div>天下咸共推曰：阁下今之陆贽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236961_comment'></div>公卿之间，最为先进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236961_comment'></div>委任之久，最为更练；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236961_comment'></div>艺文之苑，最为美博；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236961_comment'></div>裁处之际，最为智辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236961_comment'></div>天子虚心，恨相见晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236961_comment'></div>眷奖之渥，旦夕大用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236961_comment'></div>考室之师，阁下是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236961_comment'></div>积穗以基之，裕民而庇之，方且巩固轮奂，安若太山，可以为天下贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236961_comment'></div>所用寻尺之材，必经顾盼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236961_comment'></div>班斤待郢质，而良工须利器，天下其谁不愿才乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236961_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236961_comment'></div>致君行道，蹈尧、舜、周、孔之堂室门庭，文字溢于竹帛，勋业昭于旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236961_comment'></div>绛帐受经之生，皆鹗立朝右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236961_comment'></div>堂下捉刀之士，有长万夫者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236961_comment'></div>天下之髦俊，经于阁下之耳目，既厌饫矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236961_comment'></div>文章道术，据其复明之根，而纵其爇天之焰，即之望之者骇愕眩晃，自失而走者有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236961_comment'></div>今夫琐琐之流，欲彻声闻于帐下者，亦僭越矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236961_comment'></div>恭惟孔氏之道，曾子、子思之传，而孟轲治气养心以扩之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236961_comment'></div>庄周、屈原，各以其所见而鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236961_comment'></div>汉扬、马振其光，而唐燕、许飏其芬，退之立言复古，扫诸子之陈迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236961_comment'></div>宋兴，杨、刘肇基，欧阳公始唱天下，削时文之敝，其文奄有孔孟之馀烈，兼众作之芳芗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236961_comment'></div>近世学者多不能诵习欧阳子而流入于异端，往往皆丧邦之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236961_comment'></div>天下所以流血，苍生所以困毙者，鲜不由异端之所致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236961_comment'></div>阁下之学，今日欧阳子之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236961_comment'></div>正人待之而为善，匪人待之而自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236961_comment'></div>籀窃伏下风，从诸父昆弟尝游门下，究观盛美之绪馀糟粕，不为不久，区区见闻，亦晞骥之乘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236961_comment'></div>近者避地江左，贫无置锥之地，平生之志，穷而益坚，老而益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236961_comment'></div>其磨研编削粗勤，其取舍是非甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236961_comment'></div>不揆其身之疏冗，辄进伏于阁下之宾次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236961_comment'></div>自谓推孔孟之派，讲韩欧之风者，世人之治此道者益衰少，故与我者亦希焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236961_comment'></div>大君子日进此道，为之不厌，尝试请益焉，庶几不拒也，吾道斯文乃所归向矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236961_comment'></div>昔羊舌肸弃乐王鲋而望祁奚之举，太史慈以北海知己而为之解围，关云长得孔明超轶之褒而增重于世，牛僧孺被退之题门之宠而名动京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236961_comment'></div>古之人心契气合，如鱼之游，如鸟之翔，甚可乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236961_comment'></div>顾惟潦倒之才，口耳之隘，譬之游侠、滑稽、力士、日者，大君子未遽弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236961_comment'></div>若夫选抡而加藻饰焉，共奏成厦之功，免于泥涂之辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236961_comment'></div>使涤虑潜心，以发扬盛德大业，当仁徇义，亦可以奋励出奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236961_comment'></div>惟阁下所以进退之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236961_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1236961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　上门下侍郎颜岐书。作品：《上门下侍郎》<div id='poem_1236960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上门下侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236960")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236960'>籀夙志于学，圭荜之下，盖尝妄意计议今古天下之事，耻为空言，必致实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236960_comment'></div>以前辈为之宗盟，如山如岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236960_comment'></div>然当世富贵功名之士，所欲见者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236960_comment'></div>窃伏阁下之义，不敢近舍而远希，因具道其区区焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236960_comment'></div>《语》曰：「时然后言，人不厌其言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236960_comment'></div>古者有大事，阖国人而问，谋及庶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236960_comment'></div>今日诚是庶人得言之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236960_comment'></div>故人有轻于一叶，而言有重于泰山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236960_comment'></div>盖天下不治，治之在本，福基祸胎，非偶然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236960_comment'></div>亡羊而补牢，胜于坐视也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236960_comment'></div>见兔而顾犬，犹为得策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236960_comment'></div>历数前后乱吾邦家者，大概皆鴃舌之相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236960_comment'></div>譬如蛇虿蝗𧌒遗类馀种，必为巨害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236960_comment'></div>仲尼作《春秋》，吴越未尝称人，荆舒咸在斥罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236960_comment'></div>今奈何不循覆车之戒，用闽蜑为相乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236960_comment'></div>前此维扬祸变，一薛居州齐言，不胜楚人之咻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236960_comment'></div>一屈原独醒，未解众人之醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236960_comment'></div>忠言至计，蔽于悍夫之当轴，刚狠怙权之所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236960_comment'></div>阁下正坐忧人之忧耳，事之不如尊意者十常八九，可想见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236960_comment'></div>甚矣，世俗之难悟也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236960_comment'></div>伏念艺祖、太宗聪明神武，知人安民，法制规模，防虑宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236960_comment'></div>士大夫孰不由之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236960_comment'></div>不幸鴃舌之徒崇饰穿凿，唱其奸言，鄙尧陋禹，变蔑旧章，扫地无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236960_comment'></div>四五十年来，人人风靡其说，沦于骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236960_comment'></div>纲纪颓圮，中原大乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236960_comment'></div>中才之流，甘心入于商鞅、李斯之术，天下滔滔，不知何者为正论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236960_comment'></div>所幸庆历、嘉祐之遗，世臣故家，尚有佩服义方之训，不流俗尚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236960_comment'></div>称尧言而希颜徒，其间固必有豪杰之士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236960_comment'></div>今日后生慕善者，期待阁下亦云甚重，谓可以修祖宗之法制，推前哲之范模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236960_comment'></div>群情颙颙，以为当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236960_comment'></div>古人谓举伊尹、皋陶，而不仁者远，谓仁者以类进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236960_comment'></div>如使伊、皋不引其类连茹而进，则不仁者何惮而远乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236960_comment'></div>今天下之猾贼，幸天下之有变而欲有所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236960_comment'></div>天下之贤士，倚朝廷之尊而欲输写其肺腑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236960_comment'></div>夫猾贼诛之，自有其衅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236960_comment'></div>贤士孜之，以旌其来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236960_comment'></div>此公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236960_comment'></div>兵戈之际，图书酱瓿，儒冠遭辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236960_comment'></div>古之定祸乱，岂特武人爪牙之功乎，文士实为之腹心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236960_comment'></div>士有待价而沽玉、抱璞而长号者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236960_comment'></div>且夫一发之不理，一指之不伸，尚且无聊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236960_comment'></div>视国家涂炭，则瞠然不能效尺寸，理必不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236960_comment'></div>忽而弃之，则过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236960_comment'></div>方今邻敌内侮，如未解倒悬之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236960_comment'></div>兵卫寡弱，有外强中乾之敝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236960_comment'></div>府库殚竭，有旦暮不给之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236960_comment'></div>盗贼江右，伺候乏羁縻绥御之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236960_comment'></div>此四患也，大者金人之害，尤为难图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236960_comment'></div>譬之洪水，堤防既立，水行无事而后可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236960_comment'></div>堤防不固，无所措手足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236960_comment'></div>吾以天险为堤防，不亦可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236960_comment'></div>塘泺不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236960_comment'></div>其次兵卫寡弱，当遣信臣招辑散亡，来者厚加存恤，则行且渐盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236960_comment'></div>其次府库殚竭，当效卫文公秉心塞渊，则万艘继来，国益富矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236960_comment'></div>其次盗贼江右，御得其道，寇雠化为亲戚，置而不问，将为大患，在所虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236960_comment'></div>古来夷狄之患，未尝及江以南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236960_comment'></div>累年秦、齐、晋、魏被其残虐，中原计掠殆尽，惟大江则不敢睥睨，其力不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236960_comment'></div>彼贪财好色，非有长久之计，肘腋之变，当在旦夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236960_comment'></div>朝廷据有荆、吴、越、蜀之饶，尚足以出力养锐，以俟其敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236960_comment'></div>然恃江立国，虽有天险之边防，荆襄、江汉上流，未见其能固守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236960_comment'></div>守御之备，莫急于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236960_comment'></div>使江汉之间，公卿刺史、下逮皂隶刍荛，人人具其术略，决择而参用之，其利害必尽得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236960_comment'></div>然后择高才绝识者统其事，朝廷用人何事不济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236960_comment'></div>且如拜尹逢于仓猝，收剧孟于扰攘，不以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236960_comment'></div>至于爵禄，曾无少吝，足以使才能者奋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236960_comment'></div>似是而非者，尚能聋瞽耳目，犹在察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236960_comment'></div>夫观人以所言，不如以其所学，考其所学，则处心积虑咸可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236960_comment'></div>然后试之以事，则无所逃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236960_comment'></div>夫以人事君，大臣之先务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1236960_comment'></div>阁下亚圣之裔孙，深得凫绎先生之文采风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1236960_comment'></div>箕裘典坟，组织道义，其仁如晋赵武，其博如郑国侨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1236960_comment'></div>翊戴社稷，有良、平之弥缝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1236960_comment'></div>成就人物，房、杜之明果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1236960_comment'></div>伟然柱石，诚可谓山东出相矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1236960_comment'></div>绛帐东阁之士，共由此道，不乏其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1236960_comment'></div>吾道未至大光，小人尚敢肆行，则十哲三千之徒未满也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1236960_comment'></div>宇宙之间，高才日少，士风不竞，可为太息！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1236960_comment'></div>汲汲孜孜，其可已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1236960_comment'></div>籀尝学于先大父栾城公，闻其许予所著《古史》，愿从尊先舍人咨考，有陋巷接尺椽之意，其相知可谓深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1236960_comment'></div>不肖顷者游梁，拜伏馆宇，辱枉题门之宠，今日非敢若众人畏贵慕势而唐突也，譬诸草木，在公之臭味矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1236960_comment'></div>顾惟潦倒疏冗，有琴张、曾晰之狂，无叔牙、管仲之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1236960_comment'></div>间关失职，遂哭穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1236960_comment'></div>灰心木形，槁项黄馘，岂可分毫贬屈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1236960_comment'></div>洴絖洒削，纬萧织蒲，岂不足以自食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1236960_comment'></div>籀之所学，恐不止于此，所求亦恐非为餔啜而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1236960_comment'></div>不揆其猖狂之辞，略及今日之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1236960_comment'></div>若蒙收录顾遇，使无补于邦家，斥之未晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1236960_comment'></div>俯伏宾次，罔知所裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1236960_comment'></div>阁下幸察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1236960_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1236960_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　颜岐论荐苏籀，苏籀作谢启。作品：《谢颜门下相公启》<div id='poem_1236976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236976?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢颜门下相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236976")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236976'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236976'>伏以乐附德门，实勤颂咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236976_comment'></div>过形荐牍，曲被矜怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236976_comment'></div>言重鼎钟，光生腐朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236976_comment'></div>饰说尝干于百里，载名敢渎于三公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236976_comment'></div>自缘顾念之私，乃致恩知之误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236976_comment'></div>窃以自别于常人者，必有高韵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236976_comment'></div>辱知于大贤者，尽抱殊能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236976_comment'></div>虽求之乘田委吏之间，而察其辅世安民之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236976_comment'></div>士难称惬，才鲜克堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236976_comment'></div>盖古今致理之权，公卿报国之志，奖擢之途忌隘，汲引之门在宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236976_comment'></div>拔十何辞，得五犹半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236976_comment'></div>将以备委任之大，岂徒掠好善之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236976_comment'></div>方今智勇俱劳，寇攘未弭，宣勋、华之泽而明俊德，分禹、稷之忧而建勋劳，裁成鞅掌之时，殆由举措之当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236976_comment'></div>凡有为而有守，皆与明扬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236976_comment'></div>诚无党而无偏，岂容鲁钝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236976_comment'></div>此盖伏遇宫使门下相公丈丈自得者极至，所履者醇深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236976_comment'></div>家传亚圣之风，世济哲谋之画，允协一德，恭断万机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236976_comment'></div>居常缘督以为经，不惮毁家而成国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236976_comment'></div>燮理劳而事夥，弥缝巧而功深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236976_comment'></div>逮燕处于琳宫，问摄生于庖氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236976_comment'></div>直谏无隐，会闻汲黯之召还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236976_comment'></div>末俗未敦，宜使杨公之亟用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236976_comment'></div>恢闳风化，保养遗黎，舍我其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236976_comment'></div>考慎其相，留意人物，振起纲维，天下将被其休功，国势殆从而安固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236976_comment'></div>籀酸寒下秩，流落寒踪，希昔仁贤，读古坟籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236976_comment'></div>群喧卑之俗状，困褒博之儒绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236976_comment'></div>既蒙品藻之优，足改朋僚之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236976_comment'></div>益祈博约，无辱提携。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236976_comment'></div>不间衰穷，眷殆伦于骨肉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236976_comment'></div>在夫臭味，愿终效于毫分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236976_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1236976_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　作上宰相书。作品：《上时相书》<div id='poem_1236962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上时相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236962")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236962'>籀不佞，谬忝读书，闻道家传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236962_comment'></div>古今治乱之学，理世及物之术，先儒之未悟，前圣之用意，尽发其枢，凛然略备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236962_comment'></div>椟载而缮藏之，以为士而无益于人，谓之苟生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236962_comment'></div>见三代以来成败得失，犹为之悲戚，为之欣怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236962_comment'></div>身经天下之扰攘，邦家之屯厄，当食不饱，坐以待旦，至于恸哭流涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236962_comment'></div>蓬庐荜户，贫守一席之间，无所役其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236962_comment'></div>狂狷不揆，思推所知以为世用，凌厉愤悱，知难而不知退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236962_comment'></div>皋陶、后稷，在千世之上，每愿为之执鞭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236962_comment'></div>共工、寒浞，见传记之间，至于作而按剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236962_comment'></div>恭惟主上时乘六龙，拨乱反正，天下安危，注意阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236962_comment'></div>阁下筹画精稳，左右弥缝，断大疑，决大计，视远听微，疚心竭力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236962_comment'></div>所以消恶运，遏乱源、因祸为福、转败为功者，何止六间三奇乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236962_comment'></div>迩者兵民就其条理，盗贼去其七八，边防增固，夷虏益驯，举直措枉，裁成中兴之业，天下咸知帝力之所自，弼亮之得人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236962_comment'></div>籀以忧时之深，故乐贤之切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236962_comment'></div>闻风览德，宽然自壮，毅然自立，击唾壶，抚绝编，仰天浩叹，稍温其所学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236962_comment'></div>譬如日侍仲尼、老聃之贤，而旁揖贾谊、陆贽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236962_comment'></div>思之而能信，固宜仕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236962_comment'></div>今天下疮痍未复，诟耻未雪，抱冰尝胆，不容少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236962_comment'></div>峨冠结绶，连茹而来，非徒然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236962_comment'></div>百虑岂独一得，尺短岂特寸长乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236962_comment'></div>或曰：「阳光盛于四海，敲石者何施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236962_comment'></div>霖雨泽于九土，抱瓮者徒劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236962_comment'></div>而况饰钻悬令之说造次直前，犹击瓦缶于洞庭之野，何足道哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236962_comment'></div>籀应之曰：岱岳沧溟，所以极高大者，不拒涓尘也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236962_comment'></div>骐骥鸿鹄，所以致千里者，四足六翮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236962_comment'></div>相公罄天下之思而用之无馀谋，竭天下之材而使之无馀事，长育天下之英才，譬诸草木，区以别矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236962_comment'></div>椅桐梓漆，长而谐律度，荐郊丘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236962_comment'></div>杞柳松柏，养而备雕斲，作器宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236962_comment'></div>姜桂因地而播其辛，兰芷在畹而飏其芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236962_comment'></div>乌喙、猪苓尽其用，蹲鸱、茯神不相渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236962_comment'></div>蘋蘩由斯而进羞，葑菲由斯而可采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236962_comment'></div>夫草木异禀，农圃不能易也，例能使之竭其才耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236962_comment'></div>如此处天下之英才，亦无不奋励而荣耀矣，盖得其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236962_comment'></div>忠智翘杰之士，康济之所赖也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236962_comment'></div>仁义学术之人，皇极之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236962_comment'></div>鄙如投盖冯河，憎如吐茵食马，贱如鸡鸣狗盗，陋如蘧蒢戚施，未尝废一焉，此长国家之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236962_comment'></div>大丈夫立太平之基，为邦家之光，天命享，人事尽，威怀四夷，日辟百里，安于太山，寿于乔松，声华蔼当世，馀庆及子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236962_comment'></div>得其人而任之，无强于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236962_comment'></div>今者国之龟鉴，道之渊薮，吾君之所尊礼，万国之所宗向，无逾于阁下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236962_comment'></div>学术之根源，事务之輗軏，官师之所准的，奸偷之所革心，无外于阁下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236962_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236962_comment'></div>一夫巧射，则百夫决拾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236962_comment'></div>一相忠嘉，则百寮景附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236962_comment'></div>天下之士，声气相求，道德相悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236962_comment'></div>阁下虽远权势，避私嫌，以斥退请谒，天下之士方且随阁下而不置也，咸望乎品题，而并祈于引达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236962_comment'></div>何特此哉，凡有不获焉，不胜其求也，其可却诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236962_comment'></div>士君子实不易得也，罗之如获凤麟，蓄之如宝珠玉，屏之如倒持太阿，失之如丧一敌国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236962_comment'></div>故视其士之得失，为其邦之兴衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236962_comment'></div>近者天下不宁，士之无赖如季布者，北走幽都矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236962_comment'></div>放逸有如管宁者，东走辽东矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236962_comment'></div>其怀土而重迁者，或陨身寇雠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236962_comment'></div>其遭难而失职者，或饿死坑谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236962_comment'></div>其得趋伏于相公之户庭者，固匪平时之比也，相公其念之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236962_comment'></div>籀所谓家传古今治乱之学，理世及物之术，可否献替，有成效矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236962_comment'></div>扫迹朝市，采薇山阿，有所未能，生生之具可谓窘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236962_comment'></div>居无屋而食无田，士之失职亦已甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236962_comment'></div>愁忧伤人，笔墨捍隔，鱼喁虫吟，嗥呼冻馁，空自悯笑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236962_comment'></div>相公命以位，竭其才力伏役国事者，不知几何人矣，其独遗一夫乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236962_comment'></div>昔籀之先大夫栾城公，以布衣奉书魏国韩公，大蒙许予，故达于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236962_comment'></div>魏公，守文之贤相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236962_comment'></div>籀之荒芜潦倒，曾何足以希先世之万一？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236962_comment'></div>当今创业之难，过于魏公之时远甚，是阁下比魏公有馀，然慎微接下，又当急于平世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236962_comment'></div>籀虽疏冗，岂得默默而已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236962_comment'></div>姓名茫昧，唐突帐下，辞情迫拙，不知所裁，愿赐优容，悯其胸臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236962_comment'></div>阁下其察焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1236962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　韩黯赴官萍乡尉，苏籀以诗饯行。作品：《送韩少汲萍乡尉》<div id='poem_139740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韩少汲萍乡尉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139740")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139740'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139740'>大门人望旧旌旄，岭表泷头罄错刀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139740'>中馈从谁合红卺，邮亭自诡絮征袍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139740'>青衫九品非君愠，黄卷连车慰我曹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139740'>兰蕙满山山水县，遥知放意咏离骚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139740'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139740_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月</a>　宋高宗自扬州入杭州。三月苗傅兵变，逼高宗逊位于皇子旉。四月，苗傅败死，高宗复位。时朱胜非为尚书右仆射兼中书侍郎，措置其间。作品：《上朱仆射书》<div id='poem_1236964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上朱仆射书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236964")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236964'>窃闻道之难行，自古所叹，于时危而尤难焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236964_comment'></div>惟大君子则易然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236964_comment'></div>社稷以为悦，华夷以为意，拯患拔艰，使礼乐征伐自天子出，虽百世而不失，此所以为大君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236964_comment'></div>以小丈夫之气临之，虑未及周，处之弗审，炫名而遗实，举一而忘三，左振而右靡，前顾而后倾，失足而入河海，呼吸而陷寇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236964_comment'></div>虽有经世之心，尊王之念，其身已不自保，而何以保其国、爱其君哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236964_comment'></div>徒为天下后世之嗤咤耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236964_comment'></div>学道者莫不欲施之于世，惟其弥缝提挈，无遗筹失策，故曰难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236964_comment'></div>昔仲山甫以不畏不侮而相宣王，致周室之中兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236964_comment'></div>季文子扶持鲁邦，诛戮巨猾，其君用宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236964_comment'></div>陈孺子居扰攘倾侧之中，汉室俾乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236964_comment'></div>三人者皆可谓大君子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236964_comment'></div>籀尝伏观建炎复辟之诏，而窃珍慕阁下真千载人也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236964_comment'></div>彼仲山甫、季文子、陈孺子而当兹时，其机略亦不过如此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236964_comment'></div>方二凶人之肆逆也，妇人小儿顿足切齿，欲死之而不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236964_comment'></div>虽有贲、育之勇，仓猝之际，无益于算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236964_comment'></div>阁下端委，神气不变，庙堂之浅深，使彼莫得而窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236964_comment'></div>大直若屈，伟度绝人，阴离其党，徐破其计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236964_comment'></div>天地顺叙，忠义炳著，称为社稷元功之臣，繄阁下得之学道稽古以御今之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236964_comment'></div>首出群公之表，祗膺太平之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236964_comment'></div>内宁矣，外患尚多也，求为首末无閒言，初终皆盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236964_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236964_comment'></div>是不徒然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236964_comment'></div>衣冠所以推予者，以阁下器识才谞，久有以服于人故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236964_comment'></div>今僭伪孔炽，强敌凭陵，急切之务，大者兵食攻守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236964_comment'></div>瓜步防佛狸之警，淝水虑苻秦之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236964_comment'></div>开口待餔者，不下十五万人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236964_comment'></div>可以控扼者，无虑数十馀处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236964_comment'></div>陆抗之疏，王浚之计，可谓龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236964_comment'></div>士马储械，简阅必当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236964_comment'></div>兼用柔辑表饵之略，其费不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236964_comment'></div>斟酌时宜，料敌论将，调帅乘之和，大小智愚，适可以相制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236964_comment'></div>将帅有志国家之急者，慨然以尽敌为意，而患在不能料敌，是以无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236964_comment'></div>如阁下专务料敌，善之善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236964_comment'></div>审察而预图之，故平居无废事，缓急有成算，庶几祖宗之宇内可复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236964_comment'></div>此数者立而吾道大光，首末初终之论可无憾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236964_comment'></div>数者不立，虽欲奠枕，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236964_comment'></div>大政所关，群情翘首，万物咸赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236964_comment'></div>天下有能有为之士，驾驭鼓作，入吾术中，所誉必试，用人之柄不可失也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236964_comment'></div>兼纳庶言，无壅下情，以冀奇谋异画之来，议论之权不可旷也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236964_comment'></div>向贤尊德，讲艺修辞，文章之宗不可避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236964_comment'></div>阁下力行之，无负天下之大而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236964_comment'></div>使斯人奋发激昂，勇于由义，乐而赴功，革其偷安苟且之俗，皆风化之致为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236964_comment'></div>用兵如方叔、召虎，机辩如鲁仲连，言语如行人子羽者，未必不获也，多君子以助治理矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236964_comment'></div>恭惟主上励精兴复，典学天纵，方且整齐乾坤，步骤汤武，委任之重，岂有它哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236964_comment'></div>阁下愤悱宵旰，翊赞经纶，遵导谟猷，每进仁义之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236964_comment'></div>君臣之际，简易健顺，超轶世俗数千万仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236964_comment'></div>此天下之士所以乐为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236964_comment'></div>夫妇之愚有不获焉，草莱之士有失职焉，则亦司其忧，任其咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236964_comment'></div>道固如是，不以为劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236964_comment'></div>仲尼有云：「知我者其惟《春秋》乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236964_comment'></div>籀之不肖，为天下安用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236964_comment'></div>自幼窃好《春秋左氏》之学，以为周孔之常道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236964_comment'></div>盖《春秋》，天子之权也，始隐，终获麟，二百四十二年之间，所以奖王室，理华戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236964_comment'></div>文武之王泽未远，诸侯大夫尚可告以义理，记其成败忠邪，引王法以绳之，加赏罚于千载之外，天人之际，靡不该贯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236964_comment'></div>施于后世，王者不可一日而无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236964_comment'></div>夫然，故知周公之德，与周之所以王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236964_comment'></div>微《春秋》，则周室不为周室，中国不为中国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236964_comment'></div>此书向遭诋斥废锢，故学者尚寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236964_comment'></div>今以此尊中国，攘僭伪，阁下殊有力于此事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236964_comment'></div>区区佔毕小生，见前古之闻人，尚知慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236964_comment'></div>尝伏光范之门，在坯陶之末矣，困于穷空，竟未有以献其愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236964_comment'></div>不能掩其无似之迹，点污记室之清尘，希觊贾逵、杜预之鉴，或者得一言以自壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236964_comment'></div>虽其适道杪忽，岂无纤毫补于朝廷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236964_comment'></div>窃妄论大君子行道之美，因得达其所闻，不觉喋喋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236964_comment'></div>不知者以为为利也，其知者以为为道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236964_comment'></div>阁下涤除四海，相王室礼乐征伐之出，天下复平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236964_comment'></div>籀亦愿不负夙昔为道之志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236964_comment'></div>伏惟贷其狂率之诛，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236964_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1236964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　有谢表。作品：《婺州谢增秩表》<div id='poem_1236928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺州谢增秩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236928")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236928'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236928'>调发佐军，幸无阙失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236928_comment'></div>褒赏增秩，叨被宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236928_comment'></div>揣己何功，汗颜无措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236928_comment'></div>伏念负乘致寇，伐鼓追逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236928_comment'></div>凡率土之王民，诛无礼于君首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236928_comment'></div>奋龙韬之洪毅，致鼠窃之被擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236928_comment'></div>州县运粟而济师，戎行操袂而献虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236928_comment'></div>辱在共理，例陟华阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236928_comment'></div>愧无奇策与异能，亦录微劳与片善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236928_comment'></div>示大公之渥泽，用劝奖于多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236928_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下功德日新，智勇天锡，正位凝命，赏庆刑威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236928_comment'></div>禁暴而生灵允怀，念功而吏士用命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236928_comment'></div>岂特一方之咸乂，殆将绵宇以削平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236928_comment'></div>臣敢不激昂犬马之心，展尽驱驰之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236928_comment'></div>誓效顶踵，用副焦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236928_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1236928_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月</a>　四月壬子，张浚以平苗、刘之乱，自礼部侍郎迁通奉大夫，除知枢密院事。籀作贺启。作品：《贺张枢密启》<div id='poem_1236972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236972")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236972'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236972'>伏审诞飏宸綍，全付枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236972_comment'></div>复辟云初，论功第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236972_comment'></div>黔黎大庆，将相调和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236972_comment'></div>获此具瞻，荣逾伦等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236972_comment'></div>窃以北巡未复，讴歌允归，南渡疾趋，环卫寡弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236972_comment'></div>值汲黯之在外，顾公孙如发蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236972_comment'></div>变生双阙之前，援乏它师之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236972_comment'></div>介甲而呼者，为吠尧之犬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236972_comment'></div>伐鼓而奋者，挥诛错之戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236972_comment'></div>孟贲骇于狂童，神龙制于群蚁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236972_comment'></div>天地尚顾于邦国，朝廷岂乏于仁贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236972_comment'></div>皆力薄而势孤，虽心非而口诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236972_comment'></div>毛先生以三寸之舌，使赵重于九鼎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236972_comment'></div>周太尉以一呼之袒，安刘氏于太山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236972_comment'></div>古常有之，今则复见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236972_comment'></div>伏惟知院枢密刚大塞乎天地，忠义一于死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236972_comment'></div>有旦莫千里之才，有吞纳百川之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236972_comment'></div>步武青云之上，身名北斗之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236972_comment'></div>捧檄者百列城，声飞仁者之勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236972_comment'></div>同心者三大帅，汗流烈士之颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236972_comment'></div>君王正位于法宫，将士悉还于天仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236972_comment'></div>见股肱爪牙之助，察脂韦首鼠之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236972_comment'></div>消恶运而遏乱原，抑奸锋而奋诚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236972_comment'></div>解腹心之疾而罔施箴砭，除城社之鼠而不假薰燔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236972_comment'></div>天下韪之，军中肃若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236972_comment'></div>深悼艰难之国步，共思英毅之王臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236972_comment'></div>顾得失存亡之际，非蓄缩鄙凡能办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236972_comment'></div>以阁下妙龄之人，杰立朝端，允代于天工，必进仕于元台，益更张于治具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236972_comment'></div>中兴可觊，大业弥隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236972_comment'></div>相衮命圭，分固当于得兔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236972_comment'></div>兵机国事，目不见于全牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236972_comment'></div>念祖宗之法度可循，讲贤哲之建明未泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236972_comment'></div>何止江南之王、谢，定配中原之管、萧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236972_comment'></div>籀玷桑梓之坤维，仰节旄之公府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236972_comment'></div>方且扬眉而吐气，不胜餍目而惬心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236972_comment'></div>欢欣交通，叹咏不足，无任为天下喜忭之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1236972_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　王次翁除江东转运判官，籀代作谢表。作品：《代江东运判表》<div id='poem_1236946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代次公谢江东运判表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236946")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236946'>祗奉丝纶，载驰驲驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236946_comment'></div>巡行封略，览视吏民<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236946_comment'></div>伏以江左兴王之上游，淮壖聚兵之严警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236946_comment'></div>逮间暇日，乃励精秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236946_comment'></div>筦榷市关，弛张贸化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236946_comment'></div>舟楫廒庾，纠擿蠹欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236946_comment'></div>惟筹度罔失纤微，而意见务知远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236946_comment'></div>乃振军以固本，兼实边而制戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236946_comment'></div>周爰咨谋，华彼原隰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236946_comment'></div>岂期器使，误及孤平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236946_comment'></div>激昂衰踪，负载山岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236946_comment'></div>安有异术，裨益涓尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236946_comment'></div>窃希一得于百为，或求千里于十驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236946_comment'></div>虚荷委寄，实深震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236946_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下勃然中兴，奋乎有作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236946_comment'></div>施博天地，仁察鸢鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236946_comment'></div>临下易而有亲，烛远幽而必照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236946_comment'></div>付外台之耳目，迩行宫之要枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236946_comment'></div>以臣肃奉宪章，粗穆朝听，施劳州县，恻怛黎元，责效方来，普劝仕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236946_comment'></div>臣敢不每怀靡及，食檗饮冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236946_comment'></div>当官而行，疚心焦虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236946_comment'></div>六条汉诏，务叶公言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236946_comment'></div>五术唐臣，专蕲厚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236946_comment'></div>殚驽蹇之微愿，副驱策之殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236946_comment'></div>苟缓旷瘝，宁辞顶踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236946_comment'></div>臣无仕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1236946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月</a>　八月，朱松监石井镇，籀有诗送行。作品：《送朱乔年被荐举监石井镇》<div id='poem_139731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送朱乔年被举荐监石井镇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139731")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139731'>石井镇初腾一鹗，管城子健斡千钧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139731'>已然自足雄吾党，其进祇应轶古人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139731'>衣被卉裳殊欲惯，解捐犊佩猾商驯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139731'>万钟他日扶危手，五斗怡怡为奉亲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年闰8月</a>　闰八月，闽中大旱，籀作《夏旱一首》<div id='poem_139871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏旱一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年闰8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139871")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139871'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139871'>阳厄会百六，骄亢惨如燬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139871'>素秋垂二七，十旬赤千里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139871'>土田灵龟坼，水车渴乌柅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139871'>历时书不雨，槁矣吁田稚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139871'>虽然海有潮，何堪井无水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139871'>塞鼻炎烟郁，吹面江风靡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139871'>憬俗雪不降，炎洲冰讵履。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139871'>虐魃岂胜诛，巫尪窘臞悴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139871'>雩禜按典彝，祝史殊跛倚。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139871'>资舟舟已尽，振廪廪馀几。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139871'>枵然望云汉，邈乎嗥屏翳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139871'>戎虏未入朝，耕战诚劳勚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139871'>收募联什伍，倍蓰给饷馈。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139871'>伊人亏颗粒，主者遭忿詈。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139871'>覆载疑亭育，蘧蒢视生类。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139871'>作为三日霖，霶沱万事理。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139871'>焦枯已不救，根檗或可冀。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139871'>疲民亿万口，生生荷天帝。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139871'>侏儒一囊足，孤寡千箱赐。<div id='poem_sentence_18_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_139871'>三军尽凫藻，邦邑岂小乂。<div id='poem_sentence_19_139871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_139871'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_139871_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f506d802c4bb4396ae24fbef2d146c85_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f506d802c4bb4396ae24fbef2d146c85");'><span id='f506d802c4bb4396ae24fbef2d146c85_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1140')">1138-1140年</a>，48-50岁</div><div id='f506d802c4bb4396ae24fbef2d146c85' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月</a>　奉祠居金华。张守罢参政知婺州，苏籀作文。作品：《牋判府张参政》<div id='poem_1237026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺判府张参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237026")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237026'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237026'>伏审判府参政大资荣分瑞节，作镇殿邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237026_comment'></div>诏命肇新，舆颂归戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237026_comment'></div>伏以任倚元老，日昃忠勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237026_comment'></div>体貌宗工，均畀劳佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237026_comment'></div>治理优于重寄，资秩艳于清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237026_comment'></div>未酬帷幄注瞩之隆，嗣有鼎铉绝伦之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237026_comment'></div>恭惟判府参政大资道侔夔稷，学贯典坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237026_comment'></div>鹢路鹏程，魁浚上俊髦之首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237026_comment'></div>天台凤阁，冠朝中秀彦之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237026_comment'></div>周《雅》老成之典刑，鲁《语》述作而信古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237026_comment'></div>毗屏弼谐之量，献替弥缝之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237026_comment'></div>补衮心精，贰公绩著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237026_comment'></div>勋业更祈于大受，经筵密侍于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237026_comment'></div>出处卷舒，百辟宗其模楷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237026_comment'></div>蕃宣屏翰，列郡竦其规绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237026_comment'></div>鱼符之问鼎来，欢呼之声相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237026_comment'></div>岂图畿甸，有此遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237026_comment'></div>籀侨籍小生，边堠宾佐，愿慕谈王之风旨，奉同乡校之民瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237026_comment'></div>吏士浃和，郊关相庆，辄当敛板于下道，庶几企伫于前旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237026_comment'></div>龙坂睎高，竿牍曷展！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1237026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年2月</a>　二月戊寅，高宗自建业至临安，苏籀为人作起居表。作品：《代驾幸临安起居表二首》<div id='poem_1236943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代驾幸临安起居表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236943")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236943'>六龙顺豫，旋轸劳归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236943_comment'></div>五玉骏奔，奉贽敢后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236943_comment'></div>廓吾天步，匪惟建业之江山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236943_comment'></div>徯我后来，延望武林之士庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236943_comment'></div>上宫闱之管钥，返羽卫于穹庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236943_comment'></div>遐迩讴吟，人灵胥悦<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236943_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下仁提三尺，道运六韬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236943_comment'></div>御世冰渊，弗遑宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236943_comment'></div>救民沸鼎，犹抑孝诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236943_comment'></div>旰昃焦劳，严恭寅畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236943_comment'></div>郁郁何心于居此，孜孜向善以强为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236943_comment'></div>念邦家祸乱之秋，恢祖宗丕显之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236943_comment'></div>勤而不息，乐以忘疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236943_comment'></div>殆获华夷之归，必期河雒之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236943_comment'></div>臣属婴郡治，阻觐旄头之尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236943_comment'></div>平定浚郊，即建干旟之旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236943_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1236943_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236944?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236944'>戎辂西辕，六师节制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236944_comment'></div>鸾旂返旆，万县骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236944_comment'></div>副吾王游豫之谣，谐我后来苏之愿，岂但却敌，凡以裕人<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236944_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下稽虞周之有为，恢祖宗之丕业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236944_comment'></div>班师旅而苗格，修德教而崇降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236944_comment'></div>从善易于转圜，应物明如观火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236944_comment'></div>决戎机于千里，拊幅员于一堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236944_comment'></div>使耋稚以怀安，顾江山之表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236944_comment'></div>鸣跸浙右，州县无供亿之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236944_comment'></div>尺书浚都，胡虏必驯扰而服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236944_comment'></div>臣周南跼迹，咫尺尧云；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236944_comment'></div>阙下驰神，祗聆禹会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236944_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a
