href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年3月</a>　苏籀上书秦桧，主张和议。作品：《上秦丞相第一书》<div id='poem_1236967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上秦丞相第一书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236967")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236967'>月日，籀谨斋沐裁书，献于仆射相公阁下：籀不佞，潜伏陇亩，积年甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236967_comment'></div>缪窥达者之概，尝窃念今天下之本，四海之势，惟闻道者足以论之，体道者可以揆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236967_comment'></div>故曰「论道」，又曰「道揆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236967_comment'></div>圣哲居于其位，拨乱守成，独知先觉，陶冶六合，运动裁成，不外乎是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236967_comment'></div>夫道也者，致之在学，承之在师，其体高妙，应用不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236967_comment'></div>其迹坟典索丘，其理仁义礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236967_comment'></div>始也因筌而求鱼，终也忘言而得意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236967_comment'></div>其至极也，天地待之而位，万物待之而育，圣人传焉，岂诬也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236967_comment'></div>或曰：天下未平，斯才智驰鹜之秋，而谈道岂切务乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236967_comment'></div>愚应之曰：不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236967_comment'></div>夫博问精思，涣然神解，包覆无穷，酬酢不匮，犹佩绳墨、带规矩焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236967_comment'></div>顺之则兴，逆取之则坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236967_comment'></div>才智所及，乃有限量，虽千虑百图而不合于道，则无益也，才智非道比矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236967_comment'></div>舜之戒禹曰：「惟精惟一，允执厥中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236967_comment'></div>《诗》颂后稷曰：「粒我烝民，莫匪尔极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236967_comment'></div>此理深博，袪名教之偏蔽，与生民为指南，解纷而不惑，更变而适宜，画功于无形，消祸于未萌，其于安危得失审矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236967_comment'></div>人主用其言，至孝、至仁、至大、至明，唐、虞、夔、契不是过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236967_comment'></div>子思、孟轲能言之，而不得施于政教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236967_comment'></div>管仲、蔿敖造之浅而所治小；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236967_comment'></div>子房得之黄石而神之，谓之《阴符》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236967_comment'></div>曹参得于盖公而悟焉，载其清静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236967_comment'></div>今也任社稷重寄，系生灵休戚，抱奇术，致帝王，开物成务，无所不综。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236967_comment'></div>天子咨沃，四夷钦想，巍巍青冥之上，位居第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236967_comment'></div>阁下膺时之运，万目胥眄，万颈胥延，天下之责，谁当任之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236967_comment'></div>以谓艺祖、太宗之郡县未复也，梓宫之未来也，太母之未归也，渊圣之久留也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236967_comment'></div>以道言之，四患之未弭，为邦何以立耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236967_comment'></div>建炎以来，亟战而求之，逾十祀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236967_comment'></div>《传》曰：「先王卜征五年，岁习其祥，祥习则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236967_comment'></div>不习则增修德而改卜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236967_comment'></div>改卜乌可已也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236967_comment'></div>主上焦劳，日勖夕惕，恭谦屑屑，寒暑勤勤，如蹈虎尾、涉春冰焉，臣下当糜捐以承旨意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236967_comment'></div>前此虏主虏酋，倾覆挠乱，涂炭宇内，其臣民往往助桀为虐者，则亦何颜与我通好，故所遣使命，徒劳而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236967_comment'></div>今虏立新君，一时用事之臣改易，非前日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236967_comment'></div>彼我之相与，既非敌怨，故使命踵来，言还地讲和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236967_comment'></div>议者谓其情难测，事未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236967_comment'></div>睿明日跻，观书乙夜，自诚而明，昭廓洞达，断然卓然以大信交异类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236967_comment'></div>朝廷应变度宜，观其会通，以行其典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236967_comment'></div>用侯公善诱之辩，贾生表饵之说，乃下议和之令，可谓导吾君以诚明仁孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236967_comment'></div>殆宸衷发此善意，道揆吾事，成此大策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236967_comment'></div>窒之则塞，抑之则绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236967_comment'></div>我之于彼，怨未尝平，愤未尝雪，忍耻含垢极矣，何异越句践、汉高帝之事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236967_comment'></div>古今不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236967_comment'></div>盖天意悔祸，穹庐革心，易战争为誓盟，变甲胄为皮币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236967_comment'></div>转睽离拘质为会合，改怨雠忾恨为恩惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236967_comment'></div>我之所得如此，复何求哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236967_comment'></div>顾措置应接，欲其曲当，浸灌薰揉，消其顽傲耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236967_comment'></div>夫战，不得已之举也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236967_comment'></div>和，名教之所许也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236967_comment'></div>方且郊馆劳犒，赠贿异礼，费虽千金，不愈于奔军屠城之衅乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236967_comment'></div>训兵练将，投石超距，保淮据江，过慎之防，先胜之计，我故自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236967_comment'></div>遣使之扰，较之交战，何啻相千万耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236967_comment'></div>彼大国也，杂用夷汉之士，岂无人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236967_comment'></div>若有人焉，其和岂徒然，其言必不妄，非可以毡毳腥秽待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236967_comment'></div>夫豪英不必在中国，彼之于道，得之五经之表矣，况亦有《诗》《书》等也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236967_comment'></div>万一地界渐复，信使又至，梓宫、太母、渊圣相继来还，此亦讲和之当然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236967_comment'></div>昔文王断虞芮之讼，相帅而归周者四十国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236967_comment'></div>瑕吕饴甥说秦缪，则晋惠改馆归绛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236967_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236967_comment'></div>文王能之，而吾君亦然矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236967_comment'></div>秦缪能之，而戎虏似之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236967_comment'></div>夫道德之化，其功岂可量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236967_comment'></div>名教之施，其理无所不服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236967_comment'></div>吾君躬蹈高世之行，天地可动，山河可移，金石可开，鬼神可格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236967_comment'></div>强悍不诎之虏，感而驯伏，理之必然，非硁硁之士、愦愦之子所能测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236967_comment'></div>又适当阁下谋王体，断国是，经济之学，大有施设，机神明鉴，天实相之，得道者多助矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236967_comment'></div>夫邻敌未宾，侵地不复，则仲尼相鲁为无效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236967_comment'></div>鸿沟不割，太公未返，则子房谋汉为无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236967_comment'></div>虏之守中原，其理明甚，众所共悉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236967_comment'></div>责我以岁赐，委我以故境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1236967_comment'></div>殆其款悃也，太母、渊圣、族属之归，又非若地土贡赋之饶，其所贪冒者何为不然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1236967_comment'></div>假令朝廷疑拒，虏使徒返，我不因此而加强，虏不由此而加弱，失事之机，触彼之怒，贻它日之大悔耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1236967_comment'></div>昔曹公不礼张松而天下分，齐威矜于葵丘而九国叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1236967_comment'></div>事有机会毫釐之差，其患大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1236967_comment'></div>今已纳其善意，加待使人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1236967_comment'></div>详观虏情，权其利，揣其害，不得不尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1236967_comment'></div>且澶渊故事，遣使会盟，南北宁一，无犬吠之警者百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1236967_comment'></div>岁叨我金币，充牣餍饫，岂不思前日之利乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1236967_comment'></div>今我兵日精，若不议和，虏岂有丝毫之得于我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1236967_comment'></div>务战胜、穷武事，自有见机之时，亦非天下之远虑至计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1236967_comment'></div>彼此民心，畏死一耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1236967_comment'></div>今无荷殳顿戟之劳，肝脑涂地之苦，而坐俟境土之归，问安之使兼具奉迎之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1236967_comment'></div>此非常之庆会，事若无阻，虽甚盛德蔑以加矣，虽甚勋业无以过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1236967_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1236967_comment'></div>阁下勉勉孜孜，建立中兴，道义益隆，四方所瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1236967_comment'></div>天下之士声同气合者，岂特腹背之毛、芝术之笼所蓄耶，亦相与乐夫志一道契之莫逆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1236967_comment'></div>故不量贱远，辄论中枢之豪末，以为门下贽，伏惟辍燕私而一览焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1236967_comment'></div>荒唐鄙野，非敢为佞也，矜愚而有择焉，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1236967_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_87_1236967_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月</a>　苏籀代苏符作谢人启。作品：《代仲虎兄回蒋扬州启》<div id='poem_1236995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代仲虎兄回蒋扬州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236995")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236995'>右，某启：叨尘上眷，俾代王言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236995_comment'></div>恳避莫遑，兢营靡措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236995_comment'></div>愧我朋好，稽驰谢笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236995_comment'></div>况夫枢衮之家，朝绅所属，发飏朽钝，有赖题评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236995_comment'></div>其爝火依日月之明，燥吻造雷风之震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236995_comment'></div>念忧患飘零之志，敷讨论润色之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236995_comment'></div>谓之称职克家，无能为役；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236995_comment'></div>期于致君及物，但切疚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236995_comment'></div>切磋冀禀于清规，顾代敢烦于妙斲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236995_comment'></div>至多溢美，无乃过情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236995_comment'></div>某官轶邵、杜之能，蕴商、偃之学，以博闻而直禁域，以宏才而肃外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236995_comment'></div>淮海赖于抚循，朝廷之所钦注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236995_comment'></div>必归台阁，实慰师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236995_comment'></div>合并可期，即驾四骊而入奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236995_comment'></div>缄縢永好，固当十袭而宝藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236995_comment'></div>感佩实深，敷染奚既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1236995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月</a>　苏籀再上书秦桧。作品：《上秦丞相第二书》<div id='poem_1236968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上秦丞相第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236968")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236968'>月日，籀谨斋沐裁书，献于仆射相公阁下：籀今春狂僭，冒干宰旅，误效计以勉庙堂之治，特辞意芜拙，至今惕若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236968_comment'></div>伏幸朝廷未赐严谴，近日又睹诏令事宜，弗能自退，斐然妄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236968_comment'></div>窃观自古道术通明之士，正倾安危，解倒悬，出陷溺，皆不世之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236968_comment'></div>三代久远矣，汉平津侯上疏武帝云：「周公旦治天下，期年而变，三年而化，五年而定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236968_comment'></div>愚心晓然见治道之所以然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236968_comment'></div>又曰：「期年而变，臣尚窃缓之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236968_comment'></div>武帝奇焉，遂以入相，卒号世宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236968_comment'></div>而董仲舒所陈稽缓，所以不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236968_comment'></div>唐太宗问魏郑公：「致理宁可造次而望乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236968_comment'></div>郑公曰：「圣哲施化，人应如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236968_comment'></div>期月而可，信不为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236968_comment'></div>三年成功，犹谓其晚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236968_comment'></div>太宗纳其说，贞观大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236968_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236968_comment'></div>方其始进也，何所据而出此言以许其君哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236968_comment'></div>儒者学以辅万物之自然，文以达古今之妙旨，执大器、定大业、趋大时、集大勋，所过者化，若置邮传命，旦暮燕越，固千载一遇，亿众一人耳，岂易曰期年期月天下于变且信耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236968_comment'></div>其未效也，若妄谈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236968_comment'></div>观公孙辅武帝，表章六经，罢黜百家，儒术光明，时尚侈靡，而务兵刑，事业浅陋，平津之说不甚用也，其言故不大验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236968_comment'></div>太宗克己慎微，寅畏恭俭，卒致刑措，郑公之言少行而验矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236968_comment'></div>夫在宥天下，言必称二帝三代，非可局于汉、唐孙、魏而止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236968_comment'></div>大抵治功神速，惟体道者为然，二公概先觉斯民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236968_comment'></div>方今天下难驯者莫若北国，一旦回面请和，稽首来享，慕礼假义，顾信修睦矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236968_comment'></div>难复者莫若中原土宇，而三京八路版图来献，肆颁大眚，一洗惟新，声教风靡者数千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236968_comment'></div>于是梓宫母后，许我迎奉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236968_comment'></div>兄弟宗族，许我遄返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236968_comment'></div>凡吾君之所愿者无不得，所求者无不获，岂非圣贤相逢，通于大道，柔远能迩，和阴阳而平天地，召致感格，如此其神乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236968_comment'></div>仲尼曰：「楚昭王通大道，故失国而能再兴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236968_comment'></div>百里奚曰：「行道有福，晋君不从而失邦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236968_comment'></div>历数近世，屡阅它相，其体履或未尽善，其任责或未克堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236968_comment'></div>术略抢攘，功业茫昧，虽欲许国爱君，而才谟有限矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236968_comment'></div>岂有一德一心，谋允事遂，赫赫炎炎，磊磊落落，寰区一变，品物再生，合仳离，复奔迸，太平之象卓绝古今乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236968_comment'></div>汉辅不逮其言，唐相克酬其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236968_comment'></div>阁下揆政庇民，再尹天下，今仅一年，孙、魏之言，效见兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236968_comment'></div>凡誉人者，惟其公则无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236968_comment'></div>阁下首膺经纶之任，峻功盛烈，乃无与二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236968_comment'></div>意者吾君朝夕念兹，盟府之典，扬庭之号，当不逾时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236968_comment'></div>窃料每存降抑，深自挹损，故使宠命稽停；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236968_comment'></div>虽然，固已播传远迩，光于四海矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236968_comment'></div>而不受其名，不居其勋，此大贤之高致，世俗固不识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236968_comment'></div>昔齐威公使管仲平戎于周，王以上卿之礼享之，管仲力辞，卒受下卿之体，君子韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236968_comment'></div>仲尼曰：「微管仲，吾其被发左衽矣，如其仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236968_comment'></div>孰谓其霸者之佐而已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236968_comment'></div>其学必本于王道也，故不怵于功利之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236968_comment'></div>阁下逊避勋爵，得仁者之心术矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236968_comment'></div>重器大名，著竹帛而铭鼎钺，终恐不免耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236968_comment'></div>愚不肖如仆者，亦能知其所谓焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236968_comment'></div>盖圣上天纵日跻，诚则明矣，所往者顺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236968_comment'></div>明则诚矣，知来者逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236968_comment'></div>此伏羲、西伯之极至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236968_comment'></div>凡功业远大，称其所得之高深云圣学，非所敢议矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236968_comment'></div>故令群臣副睿图之难焉，最后登庸阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236968_comment'></div>盖道德有馀而勋绩自遂，气合而张治具，谟契而运化机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236968_comment'></div>朝廷之上，泊然若山，澹然若渊，势静则不可动，计远则不可窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236968_comment'></div>至诚之实覃于鬼方，慈爱之衷孚于动植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236968_comment'></div>本于清心省事，无取智名勇功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236968_comment'></div>畴昔天下不幸，波摇云扰，时以谓流涕痛哭，赞翊军国，惟诈力之是务，至于马不解鞍，筹不辍手，移檄忘昼夜，介胄生虮虱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236968_comment'></div>然吾君之意未尝怡，吾民之瘼未尝去，视太平若梯天焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236968_comment'></div>道德之治，虚一而静，岂弟平易以接民物，天地交畅，故能使南北二国以信义相欢，割百城，奉皇族，而于我曾不少靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236968_comment'></div>彼非近道不能为此大度之事，我非有道无以受此殊特之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236968_comment'></div>开辟以来，华夷讲和，未有如本朝之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236968_comment'></div>昔尧忧洪水，先明五教，畴咨四岳，求贤治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236968_comment'></div>若以流俗观焉，岂不阔远事情欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236968_comment'></div>谓当日夜先从事于江河矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236968_comment'></div>使五教弗明，求一日之安不可得，而何治水之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236968_comment'></div>此尧之用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236968_comment'></div>今我国家正心诚意，蹈仁义之实，五教已明，夷狄滔天怀山，忽然如潦水归大壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236968_comment'></div>天子无愧舜禹之圣，阁下可谓致君矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236968_comment'></div>自今中原日趋平泰，求所以安辑存恤，使渠帅豪杰无失职，刺史县令勤抚字，法祖宗所以得民者勉行之，酌僭伪所以失民者蠲除之，悉皆吾土与民也，夫何患焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236968_comment'></div>然大江以北，略言之惟见其利，详虑之其害何可忽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1236968_comment'></div>念万世不拔之基、无疆之业，何得不详也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1236968_comment'></div>王猛有云：「善作者不必善成，善始者不必善后」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1236968_comment'></div>是以哲王良相，战战兢兢，虽享其乐，每思其终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1236968_comment'></div>夫亿万豺狼凯旋并、冀，盟约未甚久固，边徼帅乘始遵汉仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1236968_comment'></div>人情臲卼之秋，恃羁縻之形势，譬之解衣包火，张罗防虎，其可忘戒慎也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1236968_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1236968_comment'></div>治效患不速，所愿患不成，今速且成矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1236968_comment'></div>功大患不谦，图虑患不戒，今逊且慎矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1236968_comment'></div>前虑却顾，使无遗筹，此圣贤优为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1236968_comment'></div>仆之肤受末学，过计私忧，何补于算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1236968_comment'></div>其幼闻长者骨髓之论，拳拳不能置也，归耕其分矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1236968_comment'></div>再伏光范之门，尚幸一见，岂容无所献，庶于时有涓尘益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1236968_comment'></div>伏惟大钧诲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1236968_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1236968_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　奉祠居金华。富直柔知衢州，苏籀作诗送之。作品：《送富枢知三衢三首》<div id='poem_139737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送富枢知三衢三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139737")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139737'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139737'>琳馆屡青书带草，玺封荐捧紫芝泥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139737'>寅车暂此纡台绂，黄阁依前执命圭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139737'>表按山川裤襦内，劝农云水插秧齐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139737'>论毗国是惟公韪，令顺民心不曰卑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139737'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139737_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139736?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139736'>代天<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>襟量服英髦，能扈王舟出海潮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139736'>轻重裴公陈梗切，安危汲孺绝麾招。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139736'>吟笺访古羊腾石，奕局行春柯烂樵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139736'>谢傅不应丘壑尚，绝尘机警冠当朝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_139736'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_139736_0'>⑴ 原作夫，据明抄本、粤雅堂本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_139736_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_139735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139735?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139735'>山林引避一无求，遄返岩廊岂自由。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139735'>圣主尊贤载谟诰，故家纪善付春秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139735'>公诚愿奖朝中意，密勿谋先天下忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139735'>臭味久令参籍湜，斐然攀赋畔牢愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139735'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139735_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　诗人徐俯知信州，苏籀题其诗集。作品：《题徐师川诗卷一首》<div id='poem_139780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题徐师川诗卷一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139780")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139780'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139780'>学究村村自谓贤，西京泾渭派沦涟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139780'>古人圣处工研贯，新义阿时力洗湔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139780'>炳阔多闻包宇宙，阒寥馀韵出蹄筌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139780'>飘然径造骚人室，老愤应加视后鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在金华。王次翁以尚书工部侍郎试御史中丞，苏籀作贺文。作品：《贺王中丞启》<div id='poem_1236997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺王中丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236997")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236997'>伏审显膺休命，擢领南司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236997_comment'></div>席绝百僚，副清衷之重委；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236997_comment'></div>胪传万口，诚圣上之知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236997_comment'></div>凡在听观，莫不钦竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236997_comment'></div>恭惟帝王立本建中之道，朝廷褒直尽下之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236997_comment'></div>揆策于无眚之途，置器于永宁之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236997_comment'></div>致君子小人咸适其分，使庶工群品各竭厥能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236997_comment'></div>宽恤疲羸，抵排邪枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236997_comment'></div>屈人兵于不战，消祸衅于未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236997_comment'></div>老成仪刑，师表动静，虚伫咨访之益，允若忧勤之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236997_comment'></div>百志惟熙，万问必理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236997_comment'></div>伏惟中丞阁下有专通新一之学，极切磨餍饫之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236997_comment'></div>析蜀执戟之元文，究鲁感麟之旨趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236997_comment'></div>澄清揽辔，民誉攸归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236997_comment'></div>模范贤关，士风丕格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236997_comment'></div>不枉己以阿徇，惟信道而全醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236997_comment'></div>告老投闲，穷而不愠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236997_comment'></div>弼违救失，辩且难当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236997_comment'></div>初无爵禄之心，宁复得丧之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236997_comment'></div>丘樊恬佚，甘独乐于无何；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236997_comment'></div>轩冕傥来，蹈中庸而克合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236997_comment'></div>迁陟二史，超历三台，减仪休之圃蔬，仍平津之布被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236997_comment'></div>词章藻鉴，宜典掌于文盟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236997_comment'></div>诚正威风，妙弥纶于国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236997_comment'></div>显显大节，郁郁高谟，积著忠劳，殆登疑弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236997_comment'></div>然不鄙蓬蒿而徙眷，罔憎筦库以移交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236997_comment'></div>笑常情之猥卑，见达人之大观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236997_comment'></div>朴遫小吏，偃伏下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236997_comment'></div>曾何毫末之裨，每借江湖之润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236997_comment'></div>叨尘选取，出自称知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236997_comment'></div>误玷周行，方依奖诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236997_comment'></div>抠衣坐末，或偶合于小言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236997_comment'></div>仰首朝端，真难逢之嘉会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236997_comment'></div>不愿执鞭而求富，幸观极笔以谈王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236997_comment'></div>欣戴之私，敷颂难悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1236997_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　楼仲辉丁忧居永康，苏籀作文。作品：《上楼仲辉牋》<div id='poem_1236996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上楼仲辉笺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236996")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236996'>窃以文梓艅艎，致厦成而川济；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236996_comment'></div>大鼎鸾辂，佑餗饪暨皇舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236996_comment'></div>天资正始之英，自结睿文之柬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236996_comment'></div>贱疵本末，栖托桑枌，遐睎绛帐之徒，稍际青云之附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236996_comment'></div>颂文章而瞻德度，接旨趣而觌仪刑，赐超百朋，见荣万户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236996_comment'></div>下风引领，未至扫门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236996_comment'></div>渎餐沐燕息之私，猥干主记；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236996_comment'></div>道古今盛美之誉，准拟前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236996_comment'></div>上臣事君，在雅怀之素蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236996_comment'></div>尊贤体道，宜仁者之位高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236996_comment'></div>医门不拒于病羸，巫谒更增于默塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236996_comment'></div>参陪宥府，升擢大僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236996_comment'></div>出元常而督关西，似仁杰而抚河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236996_comment'></div>刺投栉比，予进后尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236996_comment'></div>谈吐春温，甄明萌意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236996_comment'></div>逮夫榆塞旋旆，绣里昼行，寿亲带九牧之黄金，过家养五鼎之丰膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236996_comment'></div>巨鳞纵壑以快意，威凤览辉而发祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236996_comment'></div>匪曰易得之时，卓尔殊常之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236996_comment'></div>寔名望显著，天子倚重而咨嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236996_comment'></div>惟谟画无双，元老稽疑而取式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236996_comment'></div>狐白不容反衣，太阿非所倒持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236996_comment'></div>用善良则国不虚，多君子而邦无难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236996_comment'></div>矧岩廊崇峻，惟衡石度量之平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236996_comment'></div>畎亩搜求，忘渔钓刍荛之鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236996_comment'></div>其大纲既得，虽小能不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236996_comment'></div>昔国侨取不飏之姿，郑事因兹鲜败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236996_comment'></div>博阳宽逋荡之咎，汉边所以精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236996_comment'></div>孙令君进善弗用而勿休，房玄龄一物失所而不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236996_comment'></div>要在存公而屈己，归于图治而得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236996_comment'></div>伏惟枢密阁下山峙庭中，嶷然特立，洞达机会，渊乎内明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236996_comment'></div>审谛闲详，夷易恬澹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236996_comment'></div>窥之阃奥，不见畛畦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236996_comment'></div>迎其锋铓，悉当肯綮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236996_comment'></div>凑搢绅之宗向，副黔黎之具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236996_comment'></div>平阳规随于咸京，公琰翊亮于益部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236996_comment'></div>以今究度，未足贵珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236996_comment'></div>籀萧飒雪髯，弭忘儿女之好；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236996_comment'></div>呻吟汗简，屡省圣贤之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236996_comment'></div>性理切磨，利名迂阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236996_comment'></div>偶窃主祠之三载，敢议作者之七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236996_comment'></div>羞矫激而恶奇邪，务拙讷而尚朴直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236996_comment'></div>自诡林薮之浪漫，不并才智之忧劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236996_comment'></div>龙钟实然，雌伏何较？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236996_comment'></div>仰止施设，未间空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236996_comment'></div>旨味纷然，或求药笼之物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236996_comment'></div>众声翕若，未掩车铎之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236996_comment'></div>倘邂逅以荐飏，增激昂而勉懋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236996_comment'></div>滔滔何算，艰于辱契而辱知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236996_comment'></div>屑屑至卑，罕或受容而受察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236996_comment'></div>诚自输于肺腑，殆将玷于坏陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236996_comment'></div>归依之情，敷染奚既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1236996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年12月</a>　苏符擢礼部尚书，仍兼资善堂翊善，苏籀代作表。作品：《代谢礼部尚书表》<div id='poem_1236947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代谢礼部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236947")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236947'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236947'>王政所关，天台治本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236947_comment'></div>邦礼专掌，春官望穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236947_comment'></div>贰卿方愧于官箴，六长所资于民誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236947_comment'></div>冒尘予进，阔略旷瘝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236947_comment'></div>启处莫遑，辞避罔获<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236947_comment'></div>窃以至孝睿明之主，议礼为宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236947_comment'></div>兴复迎奉之期，显亲笃志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236947_comment'></div>由仁义而起，尽钦爱而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236947_comment'></div>近正长乐之隆名，祇严徽册；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236947_comment'></div>发自清衷之诚悃，钦庀攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236947_comment'></div>钟鼓玉帛之设施，承禀咨诹之程度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236947_comment'></div>绵力何有，纶言所嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236947_comment'></div>谓蚊能戴于邱山，顾爝或裨于日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236947_comment'></div>忝窃论思之地，荐加宠擢之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236947_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下旰昃劳谦，释四海之郁结；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236947_comment'></div>励精覈实，致百度之咸熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236947_comment'></div>天纵圣神，生知儒学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236947_comment'></div>方且投戈而息马，不忘论道以横经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236947_comment'></div>被访对于延英，屡奏篇于黼座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236947_comment'></div>遭逢何啻于千载，鸿私殆历于九迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236947_comment'></div>矧草木之枵芜，当天地之渥泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236947_comment'></div>非德智学艺，不足以膺柬注；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236947_comment'></div>非公正节行，不足以玷畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236947_comment'></div>眷录前修，褒美先绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236947_comment'></div>施及不肖，误被超升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236947_comment'></div>位高深惧于疾颠，才小胡能于为役？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236947_comment'></div>念喉舌之任，期吐茹之得中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236947_comment'></div>居台阁之间，循规矩而斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236947_comment'></div>敢不靖共无懈，勉殚夙夜之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236947_comment'></div>知无不为，以答生成之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236947_comment'></div>激昂衰陋，曷惮捐麋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236947_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1236947_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　苏籀作书拟上宰执，犹主和议。作品：《庚申年拟裁此书》<div id='poem_1236969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚申年拟裁此书<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236969")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236969'>月日，籀谨斋沐裁书，献于某官上宰阁下：籀闻裨谌野谋也，公孙侨应对邻敌，载而与俱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236969_comment'></div>吴武陵疏逖也，裴度折冲靖国，深识其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236969_comment'></div>子产、中立，巍巍勋劳，裨、吴二生爱悦从之，而言亦不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236969_comment'></div>士固尚志，虽位下迹微，攘袂搀说王公之前，系时机权，何小小之得失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236969_comment'></div>君子慷慨之心，切不取小人循默之态矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236969_comment'></div>窃惟高明代天之工，慎微接下，野谋疏议所以至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236969_comment'></div>国家隐忧，避狄之馀，议论盈廷，有偏狭愦眊之见，昧久近彼己之势，不深惟羁縻之，良策则将安出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236969_comment'></div>前春金虏引去，军屯河北，止限一水，岂不能触天威，挠淮壖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236969_comment'></div>有善意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236969_comment'></div>不必张大虏兵，贬駮我旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236969_comment'></div>昔日闾阎惊窜，蹂践之酷，有目有足者见且蹈焉，亦不在多言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236969_comment'></div>彼兀术辈与吾诸将等矢刃相加，比长絜大，尝失地形，粗能越江，而归途狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236969_comment'></div>悔恨之，故更求万全，故久不攻我，况大江舟楫，非胡夷所长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236969_comment'></div>宋之为宋，卜年千万，恩浃民之骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236969_comment'></div>虏狃常胜，吾人面从，岂真服乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236969_comment'></div>使割地和好之利在我而不在彼，彼安肯先割汴、雒、陕西乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236969_comment'></div>盖和好之利，彼此共之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236969_comment'></div>夫拒抗鄙夷，勿与交接，终不能屏绝之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236969_comment'></div>擐甲谷马而来，惟有斗耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236969_comment'></div>幸而一胜再捷，兵挐衅结，忧未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236969_comment'></div>恭惟两宫问安不辍，何名而战？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236969_comment'></div>天下倒悬，生灵重负，岂不欲解悬息肩耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236969_comment'></div>盖玉敦珠槃、留犁金匕，岂无用之物哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236969_comment'></div>议者每曰：「累年割地议和，此其诡谋狡算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236969_comment'></div>使轺不得其要领，忠信无如其变诈，邀索百端，使我不能堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236969_comment'></div>和事难成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236969_comment'></div>故虽得敌国之附、五十城之归，而我自视欿然，良以此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236969_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236969_comment'></div>不为何成，不行何至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236969_comment'></div>危而费财者战也，安而费财者和也，然二者皆不易焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236969_comment'></div>我养兵劳敝，又加以赂虏，诚何以给？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236969_comment'></div>赂不多则虏所顾不重，要须将帅强则彼有所忌，盟誓坚则诈无所施，量入为出，币之多少适宜而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236969_comment'></div>和之计钝滞，战之事疾捷，非不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236969_comment'></div>假使留止一使，尚胜覆败一军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236969_comment'></div>彼四荒之外，封圻之中，安生乐业，易如反掌，岂他术哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236969_comment'></div>夫据朝夕之池，储海陵之仓，斡鹾茗之利，介邕管之驹，国家非得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236969_comment'></div>虏人资我以五路，河陇壮士健马指日可收，彼亦不较，知我尚强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236969_comment'></div>爱戴吾君，似若不薄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236969_comment'></div>昔艺祖之临御也，南北未尝通好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236969_comment'></div>驾驭英杰，使李汉超、马仁瑀、韩令坤、贺惟忠、何继筠以备契丹，虏骑莫敢犯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236969_comment'></div>太宗继统，用曹彬、潘美出征燕蓟，互有胜负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236969_comment'></div>国史载之详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236969_comment'></div>自祖宗时不能制虏之死命，章圣皇帝澶渊之役，聚天下精锐，寇莱公为相，岂不知兵乎，竟用文德，不穷武事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236969_comment'></div>自后名臣如范希文，岂不知兵乎，亦以皮币讲好为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236969_comment'></div>天生骄子，骑射绝艺，礼义不可以速化，干戈未可以遐征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236969_comment'></div>我国家以神武不杀，混同文轨，圣圣相承，专用一道，不贵征伐，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236969_comment'></div>今朝廷以道为原，以仁为根，合符于祖宗，稽疑于坟史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236969_comment'></div>卜之于天，虏情可见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236969_comment'></div>谋之于鬼，事理不悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236969_comment'></div>昆虫草木咸知好生之德，天壤日月咸明至诚之意，大策灼灼，亦既著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236969_comment'></div>修政事、讲武备，足以取重戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236969_comment'></div>夫金铁可以磨鍊，龙虎尚堪豢絷，万一野心弗驯，历稔逾时，靳固和事，所请不允，岂容中辍乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236969_comment'></div>人情未有卑词馈饷，极耳目口腹之欲而不悦豫者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236969_comment'></div>金玉锦绣，迷心酖毒，珍玩奇巧，无益治理，投以予之，亦何吝耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236969_comment'></div>将命之人未得其要领，赍送之物未塞其无厌，纵使不甚婉顺，亦非怒气直辞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236969_comment'></div>此宜用汉高隐忍之计，陈平见机之速，斟酌审谛而行之，夫何患焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236969_comment'></div>虏人方且观我知权与否，有策与无，得失安危之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236969_comment'></div>且鲁酒误赵而邯郸被攻，女子争桑而吴师入郢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236969_comment'></div>张骞之强力宽信，王乌之衅面穹庐，刘琨长啸以解敌围，段颎破虏致无种类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236969_comment'></div>所当擢其智士闻一知十、妙通蕃情者备行人之任焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236969_comment'></div>艺祖搜揽英豪之多，彼一时也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236969_comment'></div>章圣之任寇莱公，尚可继述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236969_comment'></div>虏人功无以加，富莫与伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236969_comment'></div>粗中武夫犹喜驰驱，儒生有识者岂不知和好之事有轨可循？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236969_comment'></div>利博而归于戎主，且必无意外之败者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236969_comment'></div>愚故曰：和之利，彼此共之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236969_comment'></div>众人见朝廷越在江右，以疢笃疮大，疗愈难缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236969_comment'></div>夫良医消疢、神砭除疮必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236969_comment'></div>阁下实尸此责任，不然，何以贵经国之高略、济时之至计也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1236969_comment'></div>《传》曰：「齐君之母，犹晋君之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1236969_comment'></div>布大命而强质其母，是令不以孝名也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1236969_comment'></div>岂有两国之君结为兄弟，而尚留人眷属者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1236969_comment'></div>平日胶胶扰扰之虑，行且为泄泄融融之乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1236969_comment'></div>如使和好之外，复有上策，古今大贤亦必言之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1236969_comment'></div>穷发之酋与中国之杰，复有妙见过于此者，亦可以咨访研寻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1236969_comment'></div>斯事诚非小小得失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1236969_comment'></div>明公以英风异才，独当炉锤，廊庙高深，懵学琐议，岂能损益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1236969_comment'></div>假如刍言毫末可用，必不弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1236969_comment'></div>区区尘冒，惶恐俟罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1236969_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1236969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在金华。有诗。作品：《侨居一首》《夜凉》<div id='poem_139688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>侨居</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139688")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139688'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139688'>买僮贷宅愈迂疏，颖士皆能讲旧庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139688'>典学前闻质郯子，天人定胜取申胥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139688'>未应孤负囊中笔，粗尔消磨架上书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139688'>借问棼丝谁任理，岂惟短发每晨梳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139688'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139688_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜凉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139696")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139696'>白屋秋声里，蹉跎旅食春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139696'>挑灯鲁酒薄，拊枕越鸡晨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139696'>学术家传业，风流德有邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139696'>似闻川陜捷，吾道付峨岷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139696_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fbfda0fa973546f79374be82c2a509d4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fbfda0fa973546f79374be82c2a509d4");'><span id='fbfda0fa973546f79374be82c2a509d4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1157')">1153-1157年</a>，63-67岁</div><div id='fbfda0fa973546f79374be82c2a509d4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　居金华。苏籀姑父王浚明卒，苏籀代苏迟作墓志铭。作品：《故中奉敷文阁王公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1237062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故中奉敷文阁王公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（代伯父侍郎作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237062")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237062'>某之先伯东坡公、先人栾城公，夙从太原伯扬甫游，嘉祐文安公犹子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237062_comment'></div>以能出入，持节浙部，时弛危弦，以宽瘥瘼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237062_comment'></div>详谛警切，见远识微之明，僚友赖焉，以为有不可及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237062_comment'></div>子家侍旁，冠而缔姻，栾城以妹氏归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237062_comment'></div>苏宗五女，伦次季婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237062_comment'></div>公蚤仕劳勤，晚为郎，出按闽部，资望弥峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237062_comment'></div>朝廷以栾城旧德施泽，藉公才节，图任之意炳然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237062_comment'></div>以莫齿非可进为，自诡退休，脱落氛埃，秩琳宫凡五祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237062_comment'></div>绍兴二十三年七月二十六日以疾卒，享寿八十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237062_comment'></div>栋等累然苫次，谋所以葬，具行事爵里，求为志铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237062_comment'></div>某不容以老倦为解。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1237062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1237062'><span class='label'>谨按：</span>王氏本姬姓，在太原祁县者八世。祖项为后唐辉州刺史。子孙避乱，徙居单州砀山，去应天不远。至国朝，移家于应天虞城。曾祖讳渎，通守泰州，赠太师、中书令兼尚书令；曾祖妣徐国夫人仇氏。祖讳纯臣，任濮安懿王宫教授，迁河东漕，赠金紫光禄大夫；祖妣建康郡太夫人吴氏。父讳廷老，任两浙漕，左宣奉大夫；妣硕人元氏，所生令人何氏。公讳浚明，字子家，熙宁八年以世赏补太庙斋郎。少敦柔警拔，属词日课千言。缉熙事业，令问发闻于吏理，向公不择剧易，健敏曲全。元祐五年任宿州司法，岁满，调阳谷尉。老吏宿猾，敛戢詟伏。绍圣间，河决新堤，东注眉邱，阳谷正当其冲。老壮迁避，盗贼乘间充斥，啸聚朋扇，一日之间至十馀万。本路安抚使发将兵捕袭，渠首窜轶，馀众徬徨无归。公虑武人贪功，滥杀非辜，旂榜谕以祸福，大书招出诱陷之人名姓，于其衣背以图印记之，分遣归业，但推首恶主名，报于帅司及统兵官，由是所全活者动以万计。微公，良民几至涂炭。以不自言功，故无赏典。建中靖国间，辟陕右茶司官属，举职最闻，诸司交荐，遂迁京秩，授真州六合、又沂州新泰两邑。事丛务剧，民大服其政。既去，思之如父母然。政和三年，赐五品服，掌金耀门书库。丁所生何氏忧，服阕，通判婺州。终更提举福建茶事。建炎初，建卒为乱，凡职掌兵民之官，束手颠踣。公诚至岂弟，众所共知，一言抚存，千夫帖然，由是魁首就戮。朝廷谕贷诖误，许其自新，遂以乂宁。除知泰州，虏骑犯边，江淮尘扰，孤垒守捍，沮遏其锐。以功迁直秘阁，改知建州。初，郡中有招降贼兵数千屯驻，已而复叛，坊市尽为诱胁，贼党僭窃，势如蜂蚁。公徐行避寇，以仁厚素著，贼不敢害。上章自劾，除领宫祠。复起知秀州。未几，又授亳州，不果行。绍兴七年，赐三品服，改知常州。未赴閒，召拜尚书兵部郎中，寻迁司勋郎中。久之，领福建漕计，朝论委重。陛辞，条奏民政赋役、筦榷时宜、纠奸禁暴之画，上意嘉之。到官芟烦解绕，尽蠲积弊，俭出薄入，阖境归厚。建安岁贡新茶，官囿素号膏腴，而壅培卤莽，岁颇不登，循习取足私园。乡户买茶输纳，病于侵扰，官囿科拨荒废。公始议补治，区垄增茂，岁入优裕，民力益苏。土人德之，建生祠，镵碑以颂其美，公止绝之，事寝。上闻，诏升直敷文阁。替归，朝命再领宫祠，实以优佚其老。遗表上陈，远迩士流兴嗟，姻党咤惜，曰：「哲人亡矣！」公扶危拯溺，心如金石。解纷释结，信发于声，仁形于色，故乱庶遄定。奉上临下，未尝谄讦。交际酬酢之閒，谨审抑畏，与物虚邪，故无怨恶。盖饫闻虎达之训，切磨熏染其中，所养者厚矣，非止笃于行世之道也。中馈慈懿，姆仪温淑，故鞠子众多，无不均一。仕宦七十馀载，历任二十官，阶至中奉大夫，勋文安县男，尊荣寿考，可以无怼矣。诸子以是岁十一月十八日葬公于兰溪县紫岩乡昭化寺之南麓，苏氏令人祔焉，从日者之言也。男八人：栋，通判镇江府；植，从政郎；棣、棁、楫、权，从事郎；柄、棫，通事郎。女六人，皆适良士。孙八人。铭曰：/显显文安，燀赫宗盟。负奇堂室，弟妷奋能。惟公父子，嗣烈其馨。位不称才，实浮于声。百鍊明断，龙泉青萍。世值纷揉，当官而行。翾浮之伍，失据陨生。公仁而勇，排难定倾。从容颐旨，汰浊理棼。氓戎宁壹，凶不失刑。纂文安公，拊乱疲精。菑穫伯扬，恻怛公诚。治洽雍熙，遇文王兴。善类见知，郎于夏卿。七闽瘠土，惠泽荐零。庶几古人，揽辔澄清。隶职宸居，敷文禁廷。寿登大耋，八子簪缨。阴骘阐迈，籯金六经。性如植德，龟食佳城。谁其验者？东晋景纯。委祉丛休，殆莫与京。(《双溪集》卷一五。)/奇：原缺，据库本补。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1237062_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　蜀人李谷、刘翁访苏籍于毗陵，又访苏籀于兰溪，苏籍、苏籀皆有诗唱酬。作品：《李隐卿名谷，与青城刘翁同舟至兰溪，卿大夫修生者馆之，道侣赠诗有李郎涉世似虚舟，片帆来渡楚江秋之句，毗陵家弟季文和此篇云梦蝶岂知真是蝶，骑牛何必更寻牛。老夫亦慕道者，次韵和之，记刘李事迹。刘本书生，工诗，奇异飘然尘外也》<div id='poem_396021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_396021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/396021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李隐卿名谷与青城刘翁同舟至兰溪卿大夫修生者馆之道侣赠李诗云李郎涉世似虚舟片帆来渡楚江秋之句又毗陵家弟季文和此篇云梦蝶岂知真是蝶骑牛何必更寻牛老夫亦慕道者次韵和之记刘李事迹刘本书生工诗奇异飘然尘外也<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作 元 耶律铸 诗）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_396021")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_396021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_396021'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_396021'>白公枉识郭虚舟，刘李飞符袒剑裘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_396021_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_396021'>兴轶壶中身混世，气酣酒里意横秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_396021_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_396021'>运调朱凤啄白石，耕莳金钱掣牯牛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_396021_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_396021'>赤子返真标指妙，阿伽陀药肯言不<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_396021_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 自注：刘吐丹千百粒示人，遭毒药不能伤害。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_396021_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139598'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139598'>鸟咮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>倾蓝雨春霁，琼芳入眼雾冬昏。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年12月</a>　十二月甲申，周葵复直秘阁、知绍兴府，苏籀作文。作品：《牋周尚书》<div id='poem_1237010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237010?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺周尚书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1237010'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237010'>伏审光膺褒诏，宠畀近藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237010_comment'></div>东浙虚股肱之邦，中台辍喉舌之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237010_comment'></div>搢绅遵承而翕若，吏民豫附以讴谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237010_comment'></div>遐竦车尘，驰想旌棨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237010_comment'></div>伏惟某官窥古今之奥，适时务之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237010_comment'></div>超冠素云之曹，寤柬隆赫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237010_comment'></div>摄空清鉴之长，注倚精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237010_comment'></div>爵秩逢年而九迁，才具一日而千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237010_comment'></div>委重文昌之枢要，望邻公衮之民瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237010_comment'></div>究宣周变之能，加崇牧伯之柄，俞音甚渥，召节俯颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237010_comment'></div>籀听郑履于朝端，尝获亲近；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237010_comment'></div>买龚犊于部内，实赖惠慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237010_comment'></div>仰存诲之夤缘，形庇庥之僭冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237010_comment'></div>其为欣幸，殆逾等伦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　张浚母九十六寿辰，苏籀作诗。作品：《张孺人九十六岁签判求眉寿堂诗二首》<div id='poem_139675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张孺人九十六岁签判求眉寿堂诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139675")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139675'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139675'>鹊巢流庆嗣如参，鹤发人间仰达尊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139675'>经眼尽知三世事，含饴已看几重孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139675'>承颜捧诏疏封邑，扇枕温床不倚门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139675'>取数西方无量佛，满堂氛馥贝多翻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139675'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139675_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139838?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139838'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139838'>萧同叔子无令笑，绵上之推乃弃官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139838'>咸羡此堂称圣善，累从治剧劝平反。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139838'>晨昏不怠谆谆诲，僮使皆沾泄泄欢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139838'>紫诏又当称大国，安舆五马叠荣观。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139838'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139838_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　五月辛丑苏符知邛州。壬寅，沈该自参知政事授左朝议大夫，守左仆射，同平章事，苏籀作文。作品：《牋沈左相》<div id='poem_1237023' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237023' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237023?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺沈左相</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237023")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237023_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237023'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237023'>伏念堂号昭文，曩渎光尘之末至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237023_comment'></div>班联布武，叨从表著之卑微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237023_comment'></div>仰高弥隆，挹深罔测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237023_comment'></div>矜顾幸承于谈麈，夤缘宗慕于德门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237023_comment'></div>眇兮后来，不与抠衣之数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237023_comment'></div>蕞尔前躅，犹是扫扉之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237023_comment'></div>干二仪寅亮之司，走九服具瞻之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237023_comment'></div>恭惟𡾰嵼崇崛，岳岳兮那可涯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237023_comment'></div>炜烨光辉，炳炳其罔弗烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237023_comment'></div>如天有斗，人所测以稽疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237023_comment'></div>若岁逢春，物应时而华茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237023_comment'></div>日者潜伏荒野，未遑奉《淇澳》之章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237023_comment'></div>遐屏殊方，不获献沙堤之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237023_comment'></div>恭惟圣天子畴咨嘉注，考慎佑贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237023_comment'></div>珍策良畴，不落落而必合；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237023_comment'></div>崇论闳议，即语语而见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237023_comment'></div>昨者趣负鼎之装，赴追车之诏，奏封虚伫，帝席屡前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237023_comment'></div>神比天同，利断金而莫间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237023_comment'></div>乾刚坤易，石投水之何难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237023_comment'></div>瞩柬穆清，尊奖元辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237023_comment'></div>卓然凤举，荣寤龙颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237023_comment'></div>乃畏天法祖之鸿猷，述尧纂禹之英概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237023_comment'></div>功利宣布，诏意溥合于朝佥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237023_comment'></div>弼谐寅恭，典册欢腾于民听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237023_comment'></div>窃惟仆射昭文相公生知先觉，自得资深，媚兹一人，诞敷四事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237023_comment'></div>禀《易》之精微洁静，遵《诗》之广博易良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237023_comment'></div>十二阳秋，洞开衡鉴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237023_comment'></div>二十八宿，罗列胸膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237023_comment'></div>邻国相窥，赖叔向无敌对；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237023_comment'></div>党友咸赞，谓臧孙真圣贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237023_comment'></div>千载一时，九德咸事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237023_comment'></div>国是定循于艾猎，民心切望于诸梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237023_comment'></div>端挺冲深，清嶷渊懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237023_comment'></div>熟复详计，调揉弥缝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237023_comment'></div>号令美新，非复前日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237023_comment'></div>纲条肃振，皆倚公诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1237023_comment'></div>唐建中八百之除，克谐素蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1237023_comment'></div>汉平津期年而变，宁不裕然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1237023_comment'></div>考大隆至治之由，乃持正不私之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1237023_comment'></div>究多方之疾患，警庶务之弛张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1237023_comment'></div>革敝蠲烦，而励精之实昭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1237023_comment'></div>激浊扬清，而廉直之道启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1237023_comment'></div>主善协一，维清缉熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1237023_comment'></div>迩者纪翟辂之归法宫，圣德超逾于载籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1237023_comment'></div>搦金管而书伟绩，信史比大于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1237023_comment'></div>实以睿佐明，不胶漆而固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1237023_comment'></div>以道致主，陋管、葛之卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1237023_comment'></div>故内而百辟所仪刑，外而庶邦之宗仿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1237023_comment'></div>籀粗疏潦倒，寒悴陆湛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1237023_comment'></div>乐休明附义之隆，被教育登堂之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1237023_comment'></div>因此禀咨之际，聊陈毗赞之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1237023_comment'></div>恳丐圣朝，详味则哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1237023_comment'></div>前修贵德而尊士，上臣以人而事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1237023_comment'></div>仁义礼乐，相求者不隔于显严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1237023_comment'></div>操术方略，可采者不问于雠党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1237023_comment'></div>本之以汇进之声望，假之以引类之公明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1237023_comment'></div>取器业忠良，岂先代而求士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1237023_comment'></div>探词意覈实，乃今时而藉才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1237023_comment'></div>酌其可而揣其长，度其宜而责其效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1237023_comment'></div>发明无倦，课试不轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1237023_comment'></div>圭璋昭焕于汩湮，栋干咨嗟于胜任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1237023_comment'></div>驽蹇钝质，甄藻旌酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1237023_comment'></div>书缄安事于常仪，德輶誓祈于爱助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1237023_comment'></div>归附之切，造次罔敷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1237023_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年12月</a>　苏籀与弟苏简、苏策祭奠苏符，作祭文。作品：《奠亡兄尚书龙学文》<div id='poem_1237065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奠亡兄尚书龙学文<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十六年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237065")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237065'>维绍兴二十六年十有二月戊戌朔，初六日癸卯，弟持服苏籀与简、策，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于亡兄阁学、尚书仲虎之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237065_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237065_comment'></div>肇基二祖，颍川有苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237065_comment'></div>希古孙、陈，宣哲世模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237065_comment'></div>步趋陪从，探讨诗书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237065_comment'></div>咨仿阙里，吟咏而雩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237065_comment'></div>郏鄏松楸，坟籍衣盂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237065_comment'></div>简编椟传，吾道岂诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237065_comment'></div>公弱敦敏，耽玩经旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237065_comment'></div>康成、王弼，《风》、《雅》、《彖》、《系》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237065_comment'></div>《语》、《孟》、《檀弓》，发微究体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237065_comment'></div>斟酌心精，应用词绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237065_comment'></div>烱然独识，洒落清制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237065_comment'></div>缊袍颜巷，淹此国器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237065_comment'></div>伟欤东坡，百代之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237065_comment'></div>公其元孙，家学在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237065_comment'></div>举朝注之，贾嘉、子思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237065_comment'></div>真主龙翔，育材马栈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237065_comment'></div>庙廷评衡，俞音首柬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237065_comment'></div>横经资善，注记黄省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237065_comment'></div>舒华发藻，不殒先范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237065_comment'></div>忠告之求，宜居给谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237065_comment'></div>超据西垣，代天笔舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237065_comment'></div>纶言雅奥，封章密勿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237065_comment'></div>第七属车，甘泉世职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237065_comment'></div>请间论事，燕闲玉色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237065_comment'></div>兼官弥近，台阁跬陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237065_comment'></div>命实迍邅，三返岷峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237065_comment'></div>天涯地角，水陆奔波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237065_comment'></div>牧守乡邦，程路邈遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237065_comment'></div>排抑根却，奉祠婆娑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237065_comment'></div>惠洽鳏孤，荐多寒远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237065_comment'></div>推食解衣，周给衎衎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237065_comment'></div>待人孔炽，自处疏淡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237065_comment'></div>克家之珍，佐时之彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237065_comment'></div>籀等无堪，友爱岂弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1237065_comment'></div>采其偏长，矜其不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1237065_comment'></div>解手脩门，尺书相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1237065_comment'></div>竟不一面，襟抱曷既？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1237065_comment'></div>讣来西南，宗属殄瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1237065_comment'></div>陟冈靡瞻，挥涕雨泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1237065_comment'></div>秩大常伯，七旬何怼？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1237065_comment'></div>正一诚明，安有沦坠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1237065_comment'></div>下从高曾，即穸济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1237065_comment'></div>斲刻乡枌，德音不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1237065_comment'></div>念夙饫饮，擎跽奠酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1237065_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1237065_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1237065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年6月</a>　六月戊申，汤思退自知枢密院事，授右通奉大夫守右仆射，同平章事，苏籀作牋书。作品：《牋汤右相》<div id='poem_1237025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺汤右相</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237025")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237025'>伏审妙柬圣知，参酌民誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237025_comment'></div>符梦叶卜，选众与能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237025_comment'></div>眷巍峨负鼎之英，倚卓尔济川之杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237025_comment'></div>天同神比，乾健坤从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237025_comment'></div>爰立丕图，集贤宠陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237025_comment'></div>右揆崇重，百辟由仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237025_comment'></div>诏纶诞宣，群听惊喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237025_comment'></div>恭惟元圣之作，自得忠智之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237025_comment'></div>以诚明典学，谈帝王之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237025_comment'></div>以经术融明，演周孔之躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237025_comment'></div>以庙社生灵为己任，以机筹资略为治功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237025_comment'></div>相须急而遇合难，弼亮劳而致化速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237025_comment'></div>厥初则干戈戢而疆埸靖，历久则礼乐兴而刑狱清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237025_comment'></div>将俾华夏之治，轶越汉唐而隆成周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237025_comment'></div>英乂之谈，微薄管、萧而荣当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237025_comment'></div>执此道者，公其人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237025_comment'></div>绿发珥貂，跂其年则不可及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237025_comment'></div>青衫奏艺，度其才则弥以高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237025_comment'></div>籀俯伏下风，竦祈先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237025_comment'></div>尝获面台庭而汎扫，今荣观揆路以扬辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237025_comment'></div>磊落兮可谓达人，精敏而无复滞思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237025_comment'></div>倾耳刿目，合气齐心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237025_comment'></div>赞元之册已行，迓衡之志何远！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237025_comment'></div>士遭斯际，岂不愿谐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237025_comment'></div>嗟避地山泽之臞，睎上公药笼之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237025_comment'></div>究观东閤，引望后尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237025_comment'></div>略谈盛美之毫端，允超流俗之度外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237025_comment'></div>伏惟仆射相公抗浮云之志，养浩气之刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237025_comment'></div>竦壑昂霄，拔出伦萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237025_comment'></div>绝编汗简，洞澈根源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237025_comment'></div>高《过秦》、《喻蜀》之篇，富仙禁北都之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237025_comment'></div>魏相好文景贾董之故实，姚崇举贞观房魏之便宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237025_comment'></div>念天下未获之事，措置设施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237025_comment'></div>揽海内无穷之材，钩深引达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237025_comment'></div>奏御赞书之训，大辩英词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237025_comment'></div>夙夜宥府之谟，深图宏断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1237025_comment'></div>练典常权变，号该洽而贯通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1237025_comment'></div>或澄正改更，析群疑而警切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1237025_comment'></div>便蕃显近，烜赫闲详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1237025_comment'></div>外懋九功，内苞一德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1237025_comment'></div>谈笑规随之际，雍容造化之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1237025_comment'></div>权衡效验于三阶，鼎鼐调燮于六气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1237025_comment'></div>裁成聊发其素蕴，扶持有振于斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1237025_comment'></div>再念籀晚托云庥，稍承风旨，借势岂云于借誉，附义愈亲于附贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1237025_comment'></div>钦同中外之所宗，致忘荣贱之殊等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1237025_comment'></div>游上宰之门闼，皆明廷之孔鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1237025_comment'></div>幸世隆平，逢年亨会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1237025_comment'></div>区区旧习，老未弭忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1237025_comment'></div>龌龊小知，庶几一得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1237025_comment'></div>更祈予进，乃获依投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1237025_comment'></div>焦卷根芽，仰滂沱之霖雨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1237025_comment'></div>尘埃冠剑，俟披拂于德风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1237025_comment'></div>慕愿之衷，敷述罔罄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1237025_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　九月癸酉，参知政事张纲罢为资政殿学士，知婺州，苏籀作书。作品：《牋判府张参政》<div id='poem_1237026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺判府张参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237026")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237026'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237026'>伏审判府参政大资荣分瑞节，作镇殿邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237026_comment'></div>诏命肇新，舆颂归戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237026_comment'></div>伏以任倚元老，日昃忠勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237026_comment'></div>体貌宗工，均畀劳佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237026_comment'></div>治理优于重寄，资秩艳于清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237026_comment'></div>未酬帷幄注瞩之隆，嗣有鼎铉绝伦之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237026_comment'></div>恭惟判府参政大资道侔夔稷，学贯典坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237026_comment'></div>鹢路鹏程，魁浚上俊髦之首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237026_comment'></div>天台凤阁，冠朝中秀彦之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237026_comment'></div>周《雅》老成之典刑，鲁《语》述作而信古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237026_comment'></div>毗屏弼谐之量，献替弥缝之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237026_comment'></div>补衮心精，贰公绩著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237026_comment'></div>勋业更祈于大受，经筵密侍于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237026_comment'></div>出处卷舒，百辟宗其模楷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237026_comment'></div>蕃宣屏翰，列郡竦其规绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237026_comment'></div>鱼符之问鼎来，欢呼之声相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237026_comment'></div>岂图畿甸，有此遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237026_comment'></div>籀侨籍小生，边堠宾佐，愿慕谈王之风旨，奉同乡校之民瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237026_comment'></div>吏士浃和，郊关相庆，辄当敛板于下道，庶几企伫于前旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237026_comment'></div>龙坂睎高，竿牍曷展！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1237026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　戊寅，陈康伯自吏部尚书兼侍读为参知政事，苏籀作书。作品：《邵博陈参政》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　邵博作亭于金华，苏籀题名“蒨绚”，并赋一绝。作品：《金华邵氏面山临溪而居又架木为亭云林丘壑之胜趣乃兼得之邵氏求其名予诵东坡江郊诗名之曰蒨绚题一绝》<div id='poem_139609' class='_poem'><div
