ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　擢奉常丞。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b523f6dcdc5341a6bebea493232a5c64_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b523f6dcdc5341a6bebea493232a5c64");'><span id='b523f6dcdc5341a6bebea493232a5c64_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1164')">1160-1164年</a>，70-74岁</div><div id='b523f6dcdc5341a6bebea493232a5c64' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年7月</a>　范职奉祠。回金华居住。七月，周麟之自翰林学士兼侍读，除同知枢密院事，苏籀作书。作品：《牋周枢密》<div id='poem_1237032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237032?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺周枢密</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237032")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237032'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237032'>伏以瑞世儒师，贡无矿黄金之璞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237032_comment'></div>宗工内相，嘉起草白玉之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237032_comment'></div>擅美标奇，密勿自结于荣遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237032_comment'></div>开怀前席，从容褒倚而奋庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237032_comment'></div>向者词令铿鍧，耀辉华于日月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237032_comment'></div>乃今枢机俨恪，契感会于风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237032_comment'></div>巩固太平之基，弥纶掌武之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237032_comment'></div>多算却敌，全策宪邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237032_comment'></div>奖王室于尊强，训戎容于果毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237032_comment'></div>窃以拯天下之急者，宜仗哲谋奇士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237032_comment'></div>广圣时之教者，必擢宏博蓺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237032_comment'></div>镠琳圭璋，皆万乘之器使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237032_comment'></div>股肱笔舌，惟九重之柬求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237032_comment'></div>进陪论道之司，欣慕得贤之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237032_comment'></div>恭惟枢密同知雅邃清韵，殊特轶材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237032_comment'></div>饫读典籍而逾五车，不出樽俎而见千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237032_comment'></div>辞科中隽，文苑乐推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237032_comment'></div>贯道理而养其渊源，窥阃奥而不见畛域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237032_comment'></div>用意远迈，典故该明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237032_comment'></div>若褚、马入閤而陈谟，如高、崔应问而白事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237032_comment'></div>专对见苏卿之节，甄综齐卢毓之平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237032_comment'></div>化率百僚而表庶民，威振五兵而遵七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237032_comment'></div>敷资略智辩之杰，付竹帛丹青之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237032_comment'></div>奖鉴人伦，作成品藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237032_comment'></div>门阑诱掖，海县仪刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237032_comment'></div>籀念岩跂龙津，幸海纳槐府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237032_comment'></div>奋祠馆之蕞质，渎庙堂之具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237032_comment'></div>自揣头颅，只合躬耕于陇亩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237032_comment'></div>扶持门户，不忍遐弃于箕裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237032_comment'></div>顾丘壑之芸樵，睎江海之膏润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237032_comment'></div>愿垂渥泽，所藉涓流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237032_comment'></div>敝帚荒言之粗，骇鹿华轩之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237032_comment'></div>珍颂之切，裁染奚殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237032_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1237032_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　楼炤卒，苏籀有诗悼之。作品：《楼枢密挽词二首》<div id='poem_139892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楼枢密挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139892")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139892'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139892'>决科腾踏无前勇，比牒联飞第一流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139892'>召直毫端准谟诰，甄评皮里韫阳秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139892'>槐班鼎辅膺荣柬，玉陛封章究远猷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139892'>楚挽凄酸泄遗恨，柏台金殿望隆优。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139892'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139892_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139769?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139769'>岳镇巍峨幕府雄，紫青颐旨禀趋风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139769'>布宣条目都无扰，求瘼慈祥概所蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139769'>宾位樽罍人事改，影娥花月画堂空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139769'>诸方故吏多才藻，撰纪徽嘉篆刻丰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139769'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139769_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年3月</a>　三月壬午，杨椿自兵部尚书兼权翰林学士除参知政事，苏籀作书。作品：《牋杨参政》<div id='poem_1237036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺杨参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237036")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237036'>伏审举任中宸，参毗大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237036_comment'></div>通吴蜀之中外，鼓命令而怿欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237036_comment'></div>在于下风，孰不竦庆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237036_comment'></div>丕钦进贤之礼，咨嗟理世之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237036_comment'></div>明良相求，鱼水合契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237036_comment'></div>所以答斯民之望，固当先寰海而忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237036_comment'></div>礼貌之嘉注特殊，佥同之推予卓绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237036_comment'></div>以其得十而举一，殆非小能而大知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237036_comment'></div>吁谟萃于清衷，绝识明乎毕睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237036_comment'></div>适时之杰，舍我而谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237036_comment'></div>恭惟参政六事之贵，夏官纳言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237036_comment'></div>万人之英，春闱举首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237036_comment'></div>内庭书命之云委，台阁拨剧之鼎新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237036_comment'></div>百篇奏御而副忧勤，十策发挥而破疑滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237036_comment'></div>公正如白居易，笃实如郑文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237036_comment'></div>喜筹算而敦简编，规绳管、葛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237036_comment'></div>探索丘而稽经律，根蒂孟、荀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237036_comment'></div>深乎帷幄之言，至矣樽俎之画！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237036_comment'></div>弥纶庙论，弼佑国钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237036_comment'></div>机柄得人，猷为济治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237036_comment'></div>方且燮理至和之气，扶持大化之源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237036_comment'></div>毗厚太平之基，振起偷薄之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237036_comment'></div>蕴怀建事，其巧妙而功多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237036_comment'></div>酌古制今，必天同而神比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237036_comment'></div>钟禀岷峨之灵秀，肇新旌节之闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237036_comment'></div>由危科而寤睿文，夙有故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237036_comment'></div>居复门而升二府，亦若前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237036_comment'></div>谦恭愈崇，静密不伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237036_comment'></div>文武之宗慕弥固，才节之齐量无涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237036_comment'></div>何止于咸乂军民，殆将以永安夷夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237036_comment'></div>致缉熙光明之效，皆谟明弼亮之谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237036_comment'></div>籀琐琐卑凡，拳拳倾向，藉乡枌而瞻几杖，蒙顾接而先品流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237036_comment'></div>幸待次而侨居，政屏身而退伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237036_comment'></div>霖雨之渥无间，权衡之审愿遵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237036_comment'></div>长铗每弹，竿牍小智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237036_comment'></div>欣属之切，敷叙奚殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1237036_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年3月</a>　三月庚寅，陈康伯自右仆射授左光禄大夫、兼左仆射，同平章事，苏籀作书。作品：《牋陈左揆》<div id='poem_1237035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺陈左揆</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237035")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237035'>伏审丕显休命，超任元台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237035_comment'></div>亲宠冠于百僚，宰制通于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237035_comment'></div>诞传涣号，盈溢欢声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237035_comment'></div>窃以三公赖于全人，二柄萃于一品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237035_comment'></div>惟当宁御世之具，代天为工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237035_comment'></div>惟大臣体道之诚，与上协契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237035_comment'></div>其施教正俗，俾比屋向道而回心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237035_comment'></div>其顿纪正纲，必全策察微而烛远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237035_comment'></div>提持万务之凑，独斡一毂之枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237035_comment'></div>悠久无疆，遐迩丛仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237035_comment'></div>恭惟左揆仆射相公渊怀卓玮，峻范清崇，端本适时，长虑却顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237035_comment'></div>负耸壑昂霄之器，若造舟成厦之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237035_comment'></div>挟邓仲华之文明，兼宋广平之风度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237035_comment'></div>励精凝弼，罄忧勤之百为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237035_comment'></div>宥密岩廊，孚始终之一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237035_comment'></div>在璿玑而均四气，负鼎饪而和庶官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237035_comment'></div>穆如景风，霈若时泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237035_comment'></div>课覈精于致理，绩效著于佥言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237035_comment'></div>黼扆之注倚敦隆，弥纶之志气刚健。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237035_comment'></div>消祲沴之灾患，赖雄俊之修攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237035_comment'></div>荒裔来王，祗惮坐筹之真相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237035_comment'></div>多方允乂，咸归维石之具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237035_comment'></div>舒缓佩绅，浑同文轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237035_comment'></div>平宁六合之责塞，图任积贤之功昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237035_comment'></div>化驰如神，风行无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237035_comment'></div>籀伏念时数偶合，视尺璧为至轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237035_comment'></div>炉锤首当，嗟顽矿之必化。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1237035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　居金华，有文。作品：《迎婺守周侍郎启》《牋判部汪侍郎》<div id='poem_1237033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎婺守周侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237033")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237033'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237033'>伏审命移江介，宠镇辅畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237033_comment'></div>歌股肱之良，风声洋溢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237033_comment'></div>见节旄之美，道路荣华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237033_comment'></div>窃以图旧念兹，清衷遴选，重寄亲擢，褒嘉出纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237033_comment'></div>汲汲共理求瘼之功，优优中和乐职之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237033_comment'></div>朝佥竦其挺特，士庶慕而归依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237033_comment'></div>曩者恭惟知府某官侍郎蕴道艺之端诚，际德音之延纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237033_comment'></div>登禁严而极台阁，演圣籍而侍扆帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237033_comment'></div>封章感达于穆清，礼乐饫陈于奇论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237033_comment'></div>自诡一麾之佚，曲留三节之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237033_comment'></div>准的列城之师，光辉九牧之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237033_comment'></div>盖乡党健讼，何烦繁露之《春秋》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237033_comment'></div>课督稽违，暂屈次公之精力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237033_comment'></div>摅智能高妙之政，推公明岂弟之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237033_comment'></div>籀忝预侨人，钦跂公望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237033_comment'></div>田畴务穑之隙，溪堂请益之初，钦庇乃情，敷叙曷究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1237033_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺判部汪侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237034")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237034'>伏审祗膺上柬，擢贰天官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237034_comment'></div>畴咨右贤，入从禁涂之橐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237034_comment'></div>倚瞩华选，钦传谐训之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237034_comment'></div>甄鉴俊良，朝绅钜荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237034_comment'></div>蕞尔瞻依之下客，镇于旧治之名邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237034_comment'></div>奉双鲤以裁缄，歌棫朴而称庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237034_comment'></div>恭惟判部侍郎英嶷清懿之望，绝纶茂异之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237034_comment'></div>抱器识股肱之才，炳光辉魁躔之冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237034_comment'></div>章奏处画，倾省寺而慕崇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237034_comment'></div>修述建明，翕词林之跂向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237034_comment'></div>曩者召还秘府，谈言居易之俦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237034_comment'></div>兼职儒宫，介节亢宗之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237034_comment'></div>得靖密之风以在位，敦警敏之虑以取名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237034_comment'></div>中外展措世之休功，论辩著戴君之至分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237034_comment'></div>方将致太平之尽美，补大化以燮调，台阁吁谟，国家深策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237034_comment'></div>准的毗益于邦政，经纶究观于日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237034_comment'></div>乃术高于稽古揣摩之多，智出于审官拘挛之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237034_comment'></div>岂惟铨管之有叙，必致淘汰之知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237034_comment'></div>量推多士之先，艺盖大廷之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237034_comment'></div>何止挥紫宸之翰，亦将参岩庙之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237034_comment'></div>某冗龊凡流，夙侨属部，偶合一词之善，遂蒙温厚之颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237034_comment'></div>以道相求，非萌心于禄利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237034_comment'></div>引经相质，期析喻于知闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237034_comment'></div>欣承省上之初，开慰时机之会。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1237034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　吴芾知婺州，作迎启。作品：《迎知郡吴侍郎启》<div id='poem_1237037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎知郡吴侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237037")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237037'>伏审诏音新渥，使符旧邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237037_comment'></div>天台鉴裁，奉方隅之殊柬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237037_comment'></div>地官剧柄，虚畿辅而辍贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237037_comment'></div>声敷道涂，欣溢邻壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237037_comment'></div>跂想旌旟之色，扫洒甘棠之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237037_comment'></div>恭惟知府待制侍郎懿实光辉，淳诚暇裕，渊邃士林之标矩，雍容国器之圭璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237037_comment'></div>论议建明，适宸衷之虚伫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237037_comment'></div>枉直献替，钦柱下之威棱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237037_comment'></div>登高揽辔之澄清，启沃前席之谐允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237037_comment'></div>酌王度而裁国制，斡运变通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237037_comment'></div>调军赋而节货泉，鍊详取予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237037_comment'></div>究穆清之重委，无中外之密疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237037_comment'></div>听子渊宣布之谣，流次公岂弟之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237037_comment'></div>期召节之何远，奉奏计于片时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237037_comment'></div>籀夙蒙庇于云霞，久偃伏于风范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237037_comment'></div>心诚素依于惠爱，气合渴愿于趋承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237037_comment'></div>引领贵阍，缪裁讷启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237037_comment'></div>龙坂可登之际，毛颖无画以陈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1237037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　真歇和尚游龙翔，苏籀作诗送行。作品：《龙翔真歇和尚求诗一首》<div id='poem_139816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙翔真歇和尚求诗赠一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139816")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139816'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139816'>象骨岩居闽府教，江海两封黄纸召。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139816'>孤云自南仍更东，阻觐尧蓂友廊庙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139816'>讲通明论毗昙经，一佛出世祇为人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139816'>凝师白傅有真契，凿齿弥天必相值。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139816'>河汉滔滔渺涯涘，三反九折时游戏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139816'>簦屩跻堂累千辈，鍧雷激电非思议。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139816'>毫忽微差失大千，同尽鸳鸿与蝼蚁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139816'>菩提一切皆具足，刮膜分光诚岂弟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139816'>体味龙宫七佛书，卢老面目云何是。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139816'>馀生流浪无明窟，回首尘尘非自己。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139816'>季咸鬼眼必见窥，和璞妙算应不遗。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139816'>大士知言善呵蔽，朝闻夕殒甘如饴。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139816'>疑蛇一祛病当愈，识路还家要有时。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139816'>金华士女涕泗流，胡为决往龙翔游。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139816'>是间虽住亦非住，奔轶常行祖师处。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139816'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_139816_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　吴芾知绍兴府，寄贺牋。作品：《牋越帅吴侍郎》<div id='poem_1237039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺越帅吴侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237039")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237039'>伏审光奉纶旨，妙柬镇东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237039_comment'></div>显拜惟新，柄兼文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237039_comment'></div>俞咨荣奖，器倚功能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237039_comment'></div>权均九牧之雄，任总十连之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237039_comment'></div>建旟植棨，列城遵听于禀承；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237039_comment'></div>飞檄颁条，庶政恪祈于抚御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237039_comment'></div>励禁闼之精采，诧嘉褒于盛时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237039_comment'></div>恭惟知府安抚殿撰端靖先勤，慈良凝重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237039_comment'></div>天台司会，物望穹隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237039_comment'></div>华殿论思，章奏臻美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237039_comment'></div>礼律国侨之详允，考课次公之精明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237039_comment'></div>重临馀刃之何劳，亟去众情之怀暌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237039_comment'></div>会稽曳笔，将庶瘼之尽蠲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237039_comment'></div>驲使赐环，必三公之遄召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237039_comment'></div>蕴抱岩廊之矩范，眷注弥纶之设施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237039_comment'></div>理体当然，舆谈共属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237039_comment'></div>伏念籀耕耘代禄，造请承颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237039_comment'></div>渌水红蕖，不图幸会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237039_comment'></div>象筹韬略，误寘空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237039_comment'></div>祗悚轩墀，诹度职局，更睎上术之提掖，愿殚下走之揣摩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237039_comment'></div>阅礼乐而敦诗书，巍峨大帅之威惠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237039_comment'></div>秉刀笔而缚绳尺，琐尾宾寮之讲求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237039_comment'></div>归慕忱诚，造次无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1237039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年6月</a>　陈康伯以少保、左仆射判绍兴府，苏籀作牋。作品：《牋绍兴帅陈左揆》<div id='poem_1237041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺绍兴帅陈左揆</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237041")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237041'>伏审诏恩倚重，时推良弼之名高；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237041_comment'></div>镇拊仰成，众附爰立之望允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237041_comment'></div>声华甚耀，控督维雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237041_comment'></div>屏毗王室之忠勤，表率海隅之政理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237041_comment'></div>颁行旨意，振激干能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237041_comment'></div>屯营训齐，闾里咸乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237041_comment'></div>不忝陶钧之赐，将蒙调一之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237041_comment'></div>伏惟判府少保安抚大观文相公精邃诚明，公正慈惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237041_comment'></div>伟度当朝之柱石，妙略应物之权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237041_comment'></div>经纶崇、璟之才，该贯孟、扬之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237041_comment'></div>笃尊主赞邦之画，慰倾耳拭目之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237041_comment'></div>柬注弥深，寄委特渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237041_comment'></div>冠先九牧之方伯，不晚三吏之赞元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237041_comment'></div>宣化承流，素同心德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237041_comment'></div>纠奸旌善，虔遵律文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237041_comment'></div>纲条整顿乎藩州，课最优隆于江国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237041_comment'></div>霖雨即霈，但舆论之不伸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237041_comment'></div>薤水风流，实吏戎之欣幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237041_comment'></div>颂旧德尊贤之诰，歌乐职宣布之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237041_comment'></div>念僚属景仰诚心，顾追锋未谐迅召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237041_comment'></div>亲依提诲，奉行教条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237041_comment'></div>仰戴钦崇，荷戢欣竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237041_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1237041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　作鞏庭芝挽诗。作品：《鞏来若求厥父德秀挽诗》<div id='poem_139652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_3_139652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139652'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　在金华。有迎丁侍郎启。作品：《迎丁侍郎启》<div id='poem_1237038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎丁侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237038")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237038'>伏审出纶遴选，剖竹颁符，辍奖倚之贵涂，畀股肱之上郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237038_comment'></div>簪绅爱戴，道路光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237038_comment'></div>凡在荫庥，孰不敛衽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237038_comment'></div>伏以知府侍郎某官懋颙卬之膴仕，彰瑰玮之清能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237038_comment'></div>黼扆亲除，眷渥蕃宣之显拜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237038_comment'></div>台阁名品，参联上列之英躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237038_comment'></div>例持橐而横经，亦分忧而剸剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237038_comment'></div>精覈详谛之老手，该广允切之周才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237038_comment'></div>惇仁民驭吏之条，懋正躬公听之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237038_comment'></div>旄节部伍，谈笑而齐肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237038_comment'></div>朱墨移檄，纷错而有伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237038_comment'></div>声实轩腾，何止徐、陈之辈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237038_comment'></div>谟画渊懿，超出龚、黄之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237038_comment'></div>籀慕乐事贤，耕稼封部，弗因刀笔之末伎，曷表景仰之衷情？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237038_comment'></div>恭惟高明，不见疵谪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1237038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　喻樗提举浙东常平，苏籀作迎启。作品：《迎喻提举启》<div id='poem_1237040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎喻提举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237040")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237040'>言念昨者际晤标表，悚承謦音，实未容请益而质疑，又未许升堂而望室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237040_comment'></div>留落顽薄，邂逅邈暌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237040_comment'></div>慕文儒博约之规，平生咏叹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237040_comment'></div>展部使公参之礼，今者幸遭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237040_comment'></div>眇镇东油幕之僚，拜记室泥缄之禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237040_comment'></div>尘埃俗状，玷渎高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237040_comment'></div>通下走之微情，惭古人之三语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237040_comment'></div>恭惟提举郎中端敏聪哲，士林所宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237040_comment'></div>恢廓公廉，朝佥允洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237040_comment'></div>课绩权衡于邦计，学艺冠冕于时流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237040_comment'></div>铜盐之干浩穰，朝廷之知倚办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237040_comment'></div>任分台察，事重按廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237040_comment'></div>咨访度诹，致精力乎五善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237040_comment'></div>稽遵庇覈，察殿最于六条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237040_comment'></div>岂弟布宣，优游有裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237040_comment'></div>攀援交态，纳卑吏之凫趋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237040_comment'></div>徐听召音，伫名贤之虎变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237040_comment'></div>籀附山仰德，补隙寒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237040_comment'></div>受任权舆于代更，卑飞上赖于宽政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237040_comment'></div>亲近门闼，佩服训言，向慕之诚，敷述奚既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1237040_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　居婺州尝作雪堂砚，作赋以记之。作品：《雪堂砚赋并引》<div id='poem_1236919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪堂砚赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（并引）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236919")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236919'>伯祖父东坡先生琢紫金石为砚，圭首箕制，置雪堂中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236919_comment'></div>形范卓豁，鸿笔钜墨，宽然运而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236919_comment'></div>先生以遗先人，此研与诗书并藏于家，子孙不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236919_comment'></div>遭乱后不知所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236919_comment'></div>仆忧患馀生，悼失故步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236919_comment'></div>北苑凤咮山溪石，先生所谓胜龙尾者，因命工采斲，复为斯制，庶几乎不失旧物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236919_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236919_comment'></div>所以记录遗书轶事，传君子百世之泽，点𪑮殆非复世俗器矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236919_comment'></div>乃作赋曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1236919'>东坡先生入道穷微，旷听娄视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236919_comment'></div>不贪之宝，不凿之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236919_comment'></div>辅物理之自然，廓无心于数外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236919_comment'></div>发为艺学，举世莫二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236919_comment'></div>契圣哲之奇韵，示名教之乐地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236919_comment'></div>穷于黄冈，斲石为研。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236919_comment'></div>底滞聱牙，发明不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236919_comment'></div>皂白经纬，箴规忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236919_comment'></div>穷《易》之刚柔贞悔，尽《诗》之兴观群怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236919_comment'></div>原法语以折衷，续《盘》《诰》之断烂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236919_comment'></div>评论铭志，幼妇黄绢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236919_comment'></div>波撇点画，出入万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236919_comment'></div>北扉东閤，言成谟典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236919_comment'></div>感麟凡例之笔，医国膏肓之砭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236919_comment'></div>邻敌为之折冲，奸邪以之丧胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236919_comment'></div>观刹溪山之刻，槃盂枕几之篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236919_comment'></div>揭日月于简牍，耀龙蛇于琬琰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236919_comment'></div>搢绅微公则聋瞽，吾道非公则黯闇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236919_comment'></div>讽诵伏膺，思见斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236919_comment'></div>斯人九原，其器尚坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236919_comment'></div>不居庙廊，非砚耻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236919_comment'></div>枕中之诀，父子之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236919_comment'></div>裹以缇衣，藉以青毡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236919_comment'></div>其器羽化，其制殆泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236919_comment'></div>雷槌取璞，月斧砺刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236919_comment'></div>三郛二趾，淋漓纤颖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236919_comment'></div>色如青铁，质如镵鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236919_comment'></div>思公洒翰，毛发竦凛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236919_comment'></div>笃古旧观，茵席之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236919_comment'></div>坡陀㳽漫，地阔海浸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236919_comment'></div>提耳画一，危失先训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236919_comment'></div>志一气随，旨达词顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236919_comment'></div>遗韔忘弓，断弦折轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236919_comment'></div>窥乎窔奥，愿窃绳准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236919_comment'></div>龊龊腕脱，忽忽道听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236919_comment'></div>至若葺宇庑下，施床榻上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236919_comment'></div>王蒙徐偃，坐卧摹仿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236919_comment'></div>骛之钻之，谁为远过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236919_comment'></div>人更相笑，儇浅丛脞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236919_comment'></div>拊砚三叹，韬翰亦可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236919_comment'></div>刚健流丽，融会尾琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236919_comment'></div>问思修省，老去疑惰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1236919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　有夜饮诗，寄托宁死守节之志。作品：《夜饮一首》<div id='poem_139852' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139852' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　曾校读苏辙所作《古史》，有诗。作品：《校雠古史二首》<div id='poem_139874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139874'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139874'>炎牺分纪到先秦，散脱前闻待发明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139874'>处士妄谈纷战国，专门阿党蔽西京。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139874'>尘沙涤荡川归海，故实符同史与经。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139874'>梦奠老人遗意得，摩天巨刃不留行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/139873?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139873'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139873'>貌从周孔讥诬伪，臆断诗书悉抵梧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139873'>悟鉴精明原本末，讨穷商略较锱铢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　作米友仁笔砚赋。作品：《米元晖山砚赋》<div id='poem_1236920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>米元晖研山赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236920")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236920'>噫欤玮哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236920_comment'></div>峦阜钟巧，巀嶭玲珑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236920_comment'></div>三茆九华之前后，二室五老之西东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236920_comment'></div>天作地宝，神力鬼工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236920_comment'></div>矩矱然而刳掇，斤斧斲于朦胧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236920_comment'></div>叟漱融结，出乎龙宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236920_comment'></div>积润秋涛之骨，霮䨴春岑之尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236920_comment'></div>特见怪而何谓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236920_comment'></div>乃壶中之仙丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236920_comment'></div>㳌渫泓坻，黝黯云浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236920_comment'></div>文字之祥，点𪑮之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236920_comment'></div>豁椟启幕，耳目清新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236920_comment'></div>扪叩而胸次块磊，赏激而肝胆轮囷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236920_comment'></div>虽一篑蕞尔，么么老拳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236920_comment'></div>瑰姿殊态，庶物莫先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236920_comment'></div>橘中肆游于园绮，耳门不蒂于兜玄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236920_comment'></div>邯郸黄粱之身世，此殆小有之洞天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236920_comment'></div>宝晋父子，负能使气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236920_comment'></div>紫渊苍璧，麝煤栗尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236920_comment'></div>挟此翠麓，用器之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236920_comment'></div>辟尘珍玩，凌云高致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236920_comment'></div>素霭扑襟，苍雾嘘机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236920_comment'></div>轨范相承，措言属意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236920_comment'></div>亭皋陇首之章，补亡正始之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236920_comment'></div>《鹅经》、《禊帖》，《洛神》、《乐毅》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236920_comment'></div>《破羌》、《梨橘》，《来禽》、《青李》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236920_comment'></div>神明还观，俚俗一洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236920_comment'></div>雄拔健峭，凝情仿效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236920_comment'></div>压邺侯之三万，得二王之秘奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236920_comment'></div>慎守玉轴，备御他盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236920_comment'></div>西清珥笔，承明应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236920_comment'></div>天子面试而加赉，巍乎致主之有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236920_comment'></div>著闻寰中，炜煌衒耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236920_comment'></div>后生标楷而趋造，前辈同明以相照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236920_comment'></div>一聚英灵，非其人而蓄峙，则崖讥涧愧，众峰诋诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236920_comment'></div>今造物出奇，副一门冥讨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236920_comment'></div>明窗细毡，对管简之嗜好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236920_comment'></div>云腾泉涌，好词似之，号称墨妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236920_comment'></div>时望公左右天造，允王国所珍，享南山寿考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236920_comment'></div>有开必先，此焉谶兆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1236920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　婺州居所有双溪，时一临游，有诗，其集亦名曰《双溪集》作品：《双溪诗一首》<div id='poem_139706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　晚居婺，有薄田数亩，足以养老，有诗。作品：《娱老一首》<div id='poem_139872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_139872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139872'>揃白追游味殊寡，所图荣绮访仙臞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
福州
-----detail

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1132')">1130-1132年</a>，40-42岁</div><div id='3133c4b6acf847b5a0b16cb0cfe4c862' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　入闽中为官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月</a>　正月，金兵以舟师追高宗。二月，高宗至温州，籀代福州守、建州守作慰问表。作品：《福州问候表》《代建州上表》<div id='poem_1236929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州问候表</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236929")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236929'>臣某言：建炎三年十二月二十六日，有入内内侍省东头供奉官徐珣等，附海船至本州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236929_comment'></div>伏闻大驾以十五日发自明州，及二十九日被温州牒，备准劄子，圣旨车驾权幸温州者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236929_comment'></div>遵海而巡，盖不获已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236929_comment'></div>避狄之患，厥惟艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236929_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236929_comment'></div>应系官属吏民等，不胜敌忾之心，各奋同仇之誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236929_comment'></div>王室之忧未弭，臣子之义不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236929_comment'></div>窃惟本路八州近寇，诸隘筑堡立栅，募民为兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236929_comment'></div>天成限隔之牢，地利金汤之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236929_comment'></div>长乐重镇，行宫切邻，悉力经营，祇备巡幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236929_comment'></div>臣闻通大道者不失四国，克畏天者必保万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236929_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下多得天人之信助，少宽宵旰之忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236929_comment'></div>念生灵之厌干戈，如饥渴之思饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236929_comment'></div>熟讲万全之策，莫如五饵之优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236929_comment'></div>更祈任贤使能，据险守要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236929_comment'></div>致使凶渠效顺，乱庶自消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236929_comment'></div>专务智谋，徐图兴复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236929_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1236929_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代建州上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236930")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236930'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236930'>臣某言：准进奏院关报，大驾以二月十七日权驻温州者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236930_comment'></div>千艘攸济，勤营卫于海隅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236930_comment'></div>三捷奏功，朝衣冠于帝所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236930_comment'></div>南牧之师悉遁，东巡之策最良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236930_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236930_comment'></div>伏以民之归仁，犹水之就下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236930_comment'></div>天之助顺，如响之应声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236930_comment'></div>我师鸷鸟之匿形，虏骑长蛇之荐食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236930_comment'></div>虽强弱之势异，而曲直之理明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236930_comment'></div>讲论绥靖之图，已见收复之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236930_comment'></div>臣新叨守土，久忝殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236930_comment'></div>愿奔行宫，省视官具；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236930_comment'></div>招辑战士，启先戎行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236930_comment'></div>内驰蝼蚁之诚，岂胜云日之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236930_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下寅畏天戒，怀柔物情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236930_comment'></div>引咎责躬，训词恻怛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236930_comment'></div>绝甘抚字，宵旰焦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236930_comment'></div>岂图一切之近功，方兴万世之长利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236930_comment'></div>忍忿避狄，斗智从戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236930_comment'></div>怀鸮鸱以好音，不惜皮币；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236930_comment'></div>消祲沴为和气，益省征输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236930_comment'></div>庶几多算之有成，以致群凶之向化，二圣遄返，四境解严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236930_comment'></div>憬彼鬼方，亦三年而能克；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236930_comment'></div>修我国政，无一日之茍安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236930_comment'></div>经纬乾坤，尽纳富寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236930_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1236930_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　徐俯至漳州，籀与洪炎作“建除”诗迎之。作品：《奉和洪丈迎谏议徐公建除之什，并次元韵》<div id='poem_139853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139853?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和秘监洪丈迎谏议徐公建除之什并次元韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139853")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139853'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139853'>建极翊皇舆，蓬庐怀致主。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139853'>除书肆时夏，提纲众目举。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139853'>满朝想风采，爱及巾垫雨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139853'>平平戒自守，落落进攻取。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139853'>定倾繄其人，防秋今尚暑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139853'>执舆岣嵝岭，栉风闽海浦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139853'>破的出新诗，江山缭樽俎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139853'>危机见未萌，刚鲠殊不吐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139853'>成宪万方瞻，作者七人数。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139853'>收召无遗贤，商山非为吕。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139853'>开悟尧舜心，亢宗诚刻苦。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139853'>闭门踰厥垣，孰与驱驰许。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139853'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_139853_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月</a>　福建范汝为率饥民反。州兵出讨，为其所破。籀代某州守作放罢表。作品：《代人谢放罢表》<div id='poem_1236932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236932?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人谢放罢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236932")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236932'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236932'>忝承朝命，祇解郡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236932_comment'></div>敷宥从轻，省躬兢惕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236932_comment'></div>伏念臣草芥微贱，天地生成，愿尽忠诚，无忝器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236932_comment'></div>郡当孔道，实为逋盗之奔趋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236932_comment'></div>衅起邻邦，责在守臣之捍御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236932_comment'></div>不能固护于封壤，何以抚循于吏民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236932_comment'></div>敢避严科，幸蒙罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236932_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下茂日新之盛德，恢天覆之兼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236932_comment'></div>厚生惟和，慎微接下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236932_comment'></div>照临幽枉，兼纳贤愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236932_comment'></div>藏疾并容，矜愚不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236932_comment'></div>臣仰荷仁政，俯念悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236932_comment'></div>靖言初终，亦非偶尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236932_comment'></div>向者凶党方炽，州兵至微，驱乌合而待其冲，收瓦解以抑其势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236932_comment'></div>屡献俘馘，遂失枝梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236932_comment'></div>徙老弱于它山，济府库于别浦，贼无所得，民亦保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236932_comment'></div>论其众寡之间，难遏奔冲之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236932_comment'></div>弹章荐击，吏议不轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236932_comment'></div>席藁何言，负芒不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236932_comment'></div>誓当洗涤于尘垢，庶几脱露于锥囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236932_comment'></div>稍赎眚愆，更图绩效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236932_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1236932_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年8月</a>　谢克家自礼部尚书迁中大夫、除参知政事，籀作《贺谢参政启》<div id='poem_1236973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236973?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺谢参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236973")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236973_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236973'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236973'>伏审人觐严宸，延登近弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236973_comment'></div>虚襟前席，咨大计而条陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236973_comment'></div>运规从绳，获真贤而柄用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236973_comment'></div>岩石增峻，飘风自南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236973_comment'></div>立政平章，同心参贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236973_comment'></div>窃以左右洪造，执持大权，弛今日之忧虞，讲当世之备御，可为痛哭者非一，如解倒悬之未苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236973_comment'></div>天子思治励精，志勤宵旰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236973_comment'></div>元臣远猷辰告，力振纲维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236973_comment'></div>武夫虚骄，殆矣偏见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236973_comment'></div>文吏丛脞，疚哉浅闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236973_comment'></div>庙堂须不世之才，蓍龟戒往事之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236973_comment'></div>寔符人望，宜亮天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236973_comment'></div>恭惟参政相公断金剸裁，绝尘超迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236973_comment'></div>识邦国远大之体，得军旅信伏之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236973_comment'></div>论思代言，窥伐苗命说之作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236973_comment'></div>解纷排难，卑射聊喻蜀之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236973_comment'></div>惟其正色而立朝，固已折冲而却敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236973_comment'></div>仁厚恻怛，副黔黎饥渴之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236973_comment'></div>赏擢精华，致豪杰兴起之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236973_comment'></div>太平之责允塞，勋庸之盛当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236973_comment'></div>籀入道不优，登门为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236973_comment'></div>鳣堂之瑞，久矣伏膺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236973_comment'></div>牛角之歌，旧蒙采听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236973_comment'></div>崎岖直辔，龌龊断编，无劳可书，有愿自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236973_comment'></div>风俗四维之克举，刍荛片说之必行，窃听倚毗，伫观施设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236973_comment'></div>王度金玉，共式昭于德音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236973_comment'></div>人材茹茅，益广开于贤路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236973_comment'></div>仰颂之喜，敷述难工。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1236973_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年8月</a>　福建安抚使程迈讨范汝为。苏籀有诗。作品：《程帅父朝议年八十余，诸人作诗褒咏，次韵一首》<div id='poem_139762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139762' id='poem_title_139762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139762'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139762'>郎潜华首寤銮舆，连帅元戎十乘车。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139762'>吏道薛公何必问，史才倚相妙称书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年8月</a>　为福建安抚使程迈赋诗。作品：《程帅新作止戈堂索诗谨赋三首》《福州程使君止戈堂二首》《程待制迈父求挽词》<div id='poem_139765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139765' id='poem_content_139764'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139764'>都士万家吁盗守，日行三百檄书驰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139764'>蛮刀短楯相绳擿，章甫毛锥亦可支。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139764'>三道来攻吾设儆，千艘利涉尔焉知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139764'>三州十万归农亩，櫜戢无穷歌颂诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139764'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139764_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139763' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139763?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139763_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139763'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139763'>楚王禁暴惭京观，汉世残民辟徼边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139763'>伐叛从来非得已，修文自古属高贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139763'>禽鱼草木无垠惠，乡校康庄议论妍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139763'>尽悴使君朝听美，不然海国岂安全。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139763'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139763_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>程待制迈父求挽词<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139887")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139887'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139887'>从班有子莳陔兰，三贵相承德齿官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139887'>政理庭闱贻济美，暄凉枕席问平安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139887'>箕裘桑梓人钦羡，滫瀡膏饴养色难。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139887'>千乘送车倾井邑，剑留传宝涕汍澜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139887'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139887_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_539525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_539525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/539525?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_539525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_539525'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_539525'>太古衣冠绮季风，厖眉鹤骨似霜松。<div id='poem_sentence_0_539525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_539525'>一枰瓜葛为嬉笑，奕叶芝兰真睦雍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_539525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_539525'>珍具乞言端有属，搢绅歌咏庆惟钟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_539525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_539525'>归全五福殊无憾，密印行将一品封。<div id='poem_sentence_3_539525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_539525'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_539525_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年9月</a>　富直柔升御史中丞，籀作贺启。作品：《贺富中丞启》<div id='poem_1236974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺富中丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236974")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236974'>伏审柬在宸衷，擢领风宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236974_comment'></div>任隆献替，用乂抢攘，当大有为，盖非常选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236974_comment'></div>多士攸庆，前修不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236974_comment'></div>窃以道不虚行，人惟举类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236974_comment'></div>念昔烈祖之辅，有如郑公之贤，门绪萧然，闻望卓尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236974_comment'></div>庙食赫奕，鼎彝著明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236974_comment'></div>后昆寔似其渊源，世俗岂知其髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236974_comment'></div>取故家之成效，在高位必仁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236974_comment'></div>温故益新，象贤崇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236974_comment'></div>典刑有自，箴训可追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236974_comment'></div>今海岱失于太平，而黔黎丧其常产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236974_comment'></div>约己陈锡，将以收敌忾之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236974_comment'></div>公听使能，将以建勃兴之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236974_comment'></div>此意甚切，厥功惟谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236974_comment'></div>从容访道之求，类非俗吏之事，必明哲同于山甫，而刚大比于孟轲，其智辩足以平厉阶，其仁强足以遵美志，汎应曲当，无颇至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236974_comment'></div>伏惟中丞妙讲规模，深识壸奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236974_comment'></div>蹇谔匪躬之节，高奇足用之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236974_comment'></div>论思甚确而朝无阙遗，执法允明而士知趋向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236974_comment'></div>声邮传于天下，谟辐辏于上前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236974_comment'></div>定倾丕平，制胜未战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236974_comment'></div>求懿德而肆时夏，总群策而殄妖氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236974_comment'></div>谀鬼奸魂，巨蠹曩烦于白简；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236974_comment'></div>散材泛驾，小疵稍洗于丹书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236974_comment'></div>知无不言，允副殊眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236974_comment'></div>位邻揆路，迁补拟汉之大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236974_comment'></div>进参调元，图任方今之近例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236974_comment'></div>籀粗为君子所与，竦闻长者之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236974_comment'></div>读先正之书，愚不希其万一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236974_comment'></div>拜高轩之日，理有契于三言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236974_comment'></div>瞠然超轶之踪，率尔狂狷之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236974_comment'></div>庆咏之切，敷染奚殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1236974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在闽中代人上谢表。作品：《代谢赐茶药表》<div id='poem_1236934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代谢赐茶药表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236934")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236934'>奉命登车，顾遵周道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236934_comment'></div>使华按节，传谕尧言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236934_comment'></div>不远威颜，竦慄矜眷<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236934_comment'></div>伏念臣琐才无取，赋命数奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236934_comment'></div>矧经忧亹之馀，骤领蕃宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236934_comment'></div>体上医之活国，念灵草之济民，安危所关，锱铢责效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236934_comment'></div>惟时故事，亦玷常科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236934_comment'></div>罔间孤踪，有兹好赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236934_comment'></div>珍奁品剂，焜耀室家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236934_comment'></div>异数殊恩，歆艳朝野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236934_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下使臣以礼，御世须才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236934_comment'></div>有攘消疵疠之方，以聚蓄收采为富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236934_comment'></div>臣敢不推原斯意，勉尽其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236934_comment'></div>抚调发之疮痍，雪鳏孤之困惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236934_comment'></div>芟荑寇乱，如决赘疣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236934_comment'></div>崇奖忠嘉，若护元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236934_comment'></div>思之熟矣，幸而得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236934_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1236934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年11月</a>　富直柔签书枢密院，籀作贺启。作品：《贺富枢密启》<div id='poem_1236980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺富枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236980")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236980'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236980'>伏审出纶扬命，近辅升贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236980_comment'></div>枢政处中，机谟密勿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236980_comment'></div>礼秩甚重，尊遇更光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236980_comment'></div>窃以副宵旰之求，则无惊乎殊宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236980_comment'></div>妙裁成之业，乃得位而可欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236980_comment'></div>盖论定于乡校之游谈，望隆于将士之节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236980_comment'></div>苍生悬命，赖经理之远图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236980_comment'></div>有识快心，怀先正之遗烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236980_comment'></div>赫赫愈著，新新不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236980_comment'></div>致奸邪惮国之有人，使寇攘回虑以革面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236980_comment'></div>裴度进而朝廷重，召伯成而王心宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236980_comment'></div>伏惟枢密知院中大稽古制今，怀仁附义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236980_comment'></div>以迈往之略承天眷，以不倦之智收人才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236980_comment'></div>司耳目于台端，言必有中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236980_comment'></div>赞心膂于揆路，知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236980_comment'></div>懋深实之谟，摅醇积之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236980_comment'></div>应对邻敌，折冲伐谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236980_comment'></div>备御盛秋，据险知要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236980_comment'></div>惟其卓荦之度，曾无肯綮之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236980_comment'></div>咸具尔瞻，无出其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236980_comment'></div>支倾补绽，正九伐之纲维；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236980_comment'></div>端本整棼，慰万方之饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236980_comment'></div>善类增气，旧章举行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236980_comment'></div>庶几山甫之贤，不忝烝民之雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236980_comment'></div>籀附于龙津骥尾，跂于凤举鸿轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236980_comment'></div>念多事之且平，独空餐而自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236980_comment'></div>同奖王室，或用九牛之一毛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236980_comment'></div>走庆台阶，尚须十驾于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236980_comment'></div>敢辞藜藿之陋，将恐桑榆之枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236980_comment'></div>钦咏之私，敷染奚既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236980_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1236980_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　苏籀此时在福建为官，初为管库，后升参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　苏籀此时在福建为官，有文。作品：《谢闽帅启》《谢帅司举启》《谢刘宪启》《牋任参政》<div id='poem_1236977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢闽帅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236977")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236977'>右，籀被命天阙，效官海邦，未闻画诺之谁欤，忽睹除书之腾播。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236977_comment'></div>继承开府，竞欲登门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236977_comment'></div>睎骥仰高，已云积岁，芘云附德，实获素心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236977_comment'></div>道路交欣，顽懦增耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236977_comment'></div>伏惟知府安抚待制儒术先觉，朝论咸推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236977_comment'></div>辞绮心精，才高行峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236977_comment'></div>宜处岩廊之上，暂淹藩屏之维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236977_comment'></div>柬在渊衷，益当委重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236977_comment'></div>盖备尝风俗之利病，得以为条教之弛张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236977_comment'></div>旄节旧临，何止昔襦之惠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236977_comment'></div>乡枌所在，斯为昼锦之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236977_comment'></div>翕然大慰于风谣，何特鄙凡之受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236977_comment'></div>籀僚属之内，官秩最卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236977_comment'></div>崎岖随牒之行，艰苦丧家之状，无伎自给，待禄纾贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236977_comment'></div>幸遇宽明，稍矜衰朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236977_comment'></div>庶殚夙夜，有补毫分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1236977_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢帅司举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236978")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236978'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236978'>伏念每怀靡及，寡过未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236978_comment'></div>特达飞章，贬屈裁鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236978_comment'></div>荷瞻烛之明恕，忘踪迹之诚微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236978_comment'></div>广度包荒，深仁扶弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236978_comment'></div>怀檄愧汗，僚友改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236978_comment'></div>窃以时运艰难，才谟匮乏，惟用能可以致理，故体国莫如荐贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236978_comment'></div>邀剧孟而拜尹逢，事其可缓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236978_comment'></div>尊乐毅而起王剪，势固宜然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236978_comment'></div>筦库之卑，本何关于算略？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236978_comment'></div>判司之秩，但稍擢其久淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236978_comment'></div>既穫大田，亦兼敛其滞穗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236978_comment'></div>别识劲草，不遂偃于疾风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236978_comment'></div>拔十觊于五收，虑千岂无一得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236978_comment'></div>顾甄藻之已误，何事为之可称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236978_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官，诵《丘》、《索》与《祈招》，多知往事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236978_comment'></div>拾甲乙之科第，遍接名流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236978_comment'></div>叙事之文，俪花斗叶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236978_comment'></div>方人之论，嘘枯吹生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236978_comment'></div>声飞九牧之先，恩浃八州之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236978_comment'></div>倦符鱼之条教，怀桑梓之菟裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236978_comment'></div>朝廷方倚其才，吏士顾依其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236978_comment'></div>岂乏邹湛之辈，共登元礼之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236978_comment'></div>猥以空疏，骤玷清举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236978_comment'></div>籀欷歔忧国，流落馀生，潦倒何成，粗疏无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236978_comment'></div>力薄不足以承绪业，伎拙不能于谋稻粱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236978_comment'></div>亲承诲音，仰止芘赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236978_comment'></div>孤学寡予，世俗之所忽遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236978_comment'></div>旧闻不愆，寤寐之所详味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236978_comment'></div>年已至于不惑，道应得于少分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236978_comment'></div>惟有进修，是其志趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236978_comment'></div>念裨益之效浅，徒铭刻之心牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236978_comment'></div>策蹇磨铅，为山学海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236978_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1236978_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢刘宪启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236985")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236985'>右，籀伏承牒命，保举某充改官亲民任使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236985_comment'></div>误开藻鉴，收录刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236985_comment'></div>辞避靡遑，惭惧兼至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236985_comment'></div>窃以陈力就列，右贤援能，考课实而事绩光，髦彦作而流品辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236985_comment'></div>中都有选曹之铨叙，方州任刺史之明扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236985_comment'></div>人才由是盛衰，国势以为强弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236985_comment'></div>岂鄙判司之冗，未嫌筦库之卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236985_comment'></div>达于家邦，由兹汲引；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236985_comment'></div>咨于岳牧，所幸称褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236985_comment'></div>通者必能举穷，显者宜于索隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236985_comment'></div>外台重寄，所治无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236985_comment'></div>卒岁颁宣，荐闻有几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236985_comment'></div>岂期冗琐，在所知怜，使锱铢增重于鼎钟，而欬唾随生于珠玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236985_comment'></div>籀之潦倒，望绝升华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236985_comment'></div>巢林一粒之资，久矣安分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236985_comment'></div>趋市半钱之利，殊不欲争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236985_comment'></div>素无狎俗之能，安得佐世之具！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236985_comment'></div>寡偶希合，倦飞拙鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236985_comment'></div>山窟海陬，半人禽于生理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236985_comment'></div>天寒日暮，恃卉葛之常温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236985_comment'></div>汝颍田庐，岷峨松槚，风尚昔多于奇士，门庭咸谓之故家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236985_comment'></div>锻铁之步空名，系剑之树合抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236985_comment'></div>悲断弦之莫续，号良冶而何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236985_comment'></div>方且敛板走趋，仰皇华之六德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236985_comment'></div>枢衣擎跽，窥理窟之一斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236985_comment'></div>伏遇提刑少卿入道醇深，秉心挺特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236985_comment'></div>厚党勤类，接下慎微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236985_comment'></div>世惩荆舒，学推歆向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236985_comment'></div>悟宜官之波画，似居巢之博闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236985_comment'></div>使斧抗威，百城以肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236985_comment'></div>从橐归觐，群公允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236985_comment'></div>信穮蓘之千箱，欲扶摇于九万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236985_comment'></div>昔乐天之思元亮，殊爱陶宗之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236985_comment'></div>文举之忆中郎，犹赏虎贲之貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236985_comment'></div>或出或处，而能同心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236985_comment'></div>无古无今，共归一揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236985_comment'></div>嘘呵衰冷，芘护孤贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236985_comment'></div>永惟此恩，其何以报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236985_comment'></div>籀更当钻研吏道，靡敢怠遑，恪警官箴，如恐弗逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236985_comment'></div>勉自激励，不辱门阑，求为可知，益敦来效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236985_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1236985_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺任参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236986")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236986'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236986'>右，籀伏以记室响报，不弃咫尺之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236986_comment'></div>东閤诺延，祗捧联翩之檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236986_comment'></div>伟度英鉴，优遇殊私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236986_comment'></div>训鄙矜愚，深容熟察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236986_comment'></div>拳拳珍仰，盖谋道而非贫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236986_comment'></div>眷眷甄谈，致怀刑而后惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236986_comment'></div>其为光幸，何以克当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236986_comment'></div>念古人之事贤，钦盛美而归往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236986_comment'></div>应对进退之末，讲画指授之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236986_comment'></div>师亲而习专，业勤而志立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236986_comment'></div>咸号登龙之士，皆来隐豹之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236986_comment'></div>扫门执御以服劳，升堂入室之尤密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236986_comment'></div>平时坐论于经旨，他日擢升于庙朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236986_comment'></div>依王公游毂之荣华，仕州县抗尘之汩没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236986_comment'></div>籀一介鲁钝，十年具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236986_comment'></div>才不副心，求称职而安在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236986_comment'></div>学无所就，顾承诲之未闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236986_comment'></div>徒有耽古求善之情，好节慕声之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236986_comment'></div>世不知而奚愠，时所尚之为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236986_comment'></div>希管、萧之荣途，顾仇、梅之末品，求其遇合，实难自媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236986_comment'></div>譬如弱羽必栖于高松，蛟龙先阶于尺木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236986_comment'></div>蝇附骥而行地，鹏积风而负天，无物不然，惟人犹是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236986_comment'></div>况今词林之根蒂，此时圣上之畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236986_comment'></div>一诺如锡于千金，一见如封于万户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236986_comment'></div>狐裘岂容反衣，不倦挽搂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236986_comment'></div>马栈无取凡材，何祈辑附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236986_comment'></div>寸长尺短，樗散液樠，悦于见知，孰不奋励！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236986_comment'></div>此盖伏遇宫使参政大资清纯养素，博笃通方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236986_comment'></div>协搢绅之公言，被旒冕之听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236986_comment'></div>悯劳以日昃之务，优游于道味之腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236986_comment'></div>学识坚高，谋猷迈远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236986_comment'></div>斥破碎臆说之缪，嗤浮躁少年之狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236986_comment'></div>雅意属于本朝，群情待于爰立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236986_comment'></div>天下有未获之事，渊衷念畀付之谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236986_comment'></div>不止居季、孟之间，行且已杨、陈之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236986_comment'></div>洗六合而攘膻秽，维四方而抚疮痍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236986_comment'></div>救民于水火之中，行师于几席之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236986_comment'></div>为家国深虑而审画，宽君王旰食而宵衣，凡所贤愚，于焉举措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236986_comment'></div>籀舍筦库而领邑，升从事而治中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236986_comment'></div>省循寸进之阶，诚为拙宦之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236986_comment'></div>至若提挈不间乎棣萼，吹嘘悉取于弓箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236986_comment'></div>曷尝小补于纤微，岂意荐叨于宠待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236986_comment'></div>籀敢不服膺惠贶，益勉操修，积累锱铢，增裨远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236986_comment'></div>舟驶舆壮，亦祈众力之同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236986_comment'></div>厦广栋隆，寔惟群木之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236986_comment'></div>孰云小己，无益高闳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236986_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1236986_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　苏籀此时在福建为官，有诗。作品：《梅雨一首》《冻雨一首》<div id='poem_139755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
