href='/Writing/139755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梅雨一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139755")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139755'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139755'>柑花销殒荔殊小，海上雨云氛气昏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139755'>感慨干戈异乡客，愁思骨肉与谁论。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139755'>白鱼紫笋清庖隶，卢橘杨梅积市门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139755'>作吏天涯何所得，一春黄卷伴芳樽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139755'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139755_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冻雨一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139671")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139671'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139671'>淋淋冻雨滴春朝，正月寒威倍凓憀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139671'>汩淖不甘劳皂隶，执舆岂必胜刍荛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139671'>素餐致寇思长策，失业疲氓想易招。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139671'>驯伏强豪苏馁乏，济时筹略直须超。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　送苏文瓘，有诗述怀。作品：《赠苏文瓘》<div id='poem_139795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠苏文瓘</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139795")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_139795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139795'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139795'>推明能隼骨专车，按地谈天河洛图。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139795'>汉魏晋唐皆贯澈，典坟今昔不荒芜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139795'>君家庭户闻风旨，吾事分毫等博屠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139795'>岂待曲终思雅颂，直缘背痒遇麻姑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139795'>预求补益三年艾，深识妖邪九尾狐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139795'>博物伟然窥子产，济时岂必愧夷吾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139795'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_139795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　代人作醮词。作品：《代醮词一首》<div id='poem_1237066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代醮词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237066")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237066'>伏念妾随夫干禄，去秦走闽，流落五年，尪孱数口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237066_comment'></div>脱违战国，探间关之路途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237066_comment'></div>瞻仰昊天，荷生全之大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237066_comment'></div>缪忝参佐，累历惊危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237066_comment'></div>顾方隅风气之异宜，或妖孽疠疵之莫测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237066_comment'></div>上渎盖高之听，深惭久祷之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237066_comment'></div>誓愿干戈不历于见闻，骨肉永远于灾障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237066_comment'></div>省躬懿戒，直心道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237066_comment'></div>妾无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1237066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月</a>　正月，高宗谓群臣曰：“福建僻陋，盗贼踵起，得非首领不知其疾苦乎？其令监司帅臣各条上弥盗及便民利物之事，朕当施行之。”苏籀应诏作表。作品：《应诏论福建盗贼表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年8月</a>　八月己卯，富直柔自端明殿学士签书枢密院事除同知枢密院事，苏籀有贺启。作品：《贺富枢密启》《贺富知院启》<div id='poem_1236980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺富枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236980")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236980'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236980'>伏审出纶扬命，近辅升贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236980_comment'></div>枢政处中，机谟密勿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236980_comment'></div>礼秩甚重，尊遇更光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236980_comment'></div>窃以副宵旰之求，则无惊乎殊宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236980_comment'></div>妙裁成之业，乃得位而可欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236980_comment'></div>盖论定于乡校之游谈，望隆于将士之节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236980_comment'></div>苍生悬命，赖经理之远图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236980_comment'></div>有识快心，怀先正之遗烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236980_comment'></div>赫赫愈著，新新不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236980_comment'></div>致奸邪惮国之有人，使寇攘回虑以革面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236980_comment'></div>裴度进而朝廷重，召伯成而王心宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236980_comment'></div>伏惟枢密知院中大稽古制今，怀仁附义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236980_comment'></div>以迈往之略承天眷，以不倦之智收人才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236980_comment'></div>司耳目于台端，言必有中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236980_comment'></div>赞心膂于揆路，知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236980_comment'></div>懋深实之谟，摅醇积之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236980_comment'></div>应对邻敌，折冲伐谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236980_comment'></div>备御盛秋，据险知要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236980_comment'></div>惟其卓荦之度，曾无肯綮之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236980_comment'></div>咸具尔瞻，无出其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236980_comment'></div>支倾补绽，正九伐之纲维；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236980_comment'></div>端本整棼，慰万方之饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236980_comment'></div>善类增气，旧章举行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236980_comment'></div>庶几山甫之贤，不忝烝民之雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236980_comment'></div>籀附于龙津骥尾，跂于凤举鸿轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236980_comment'></div>念多事之且平，独空餐而自愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236980_comment'></div>同奖王室，或用九牛之一毛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236980_comment'></div>走庆台阶，尚须十驾于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236980_comment'></div>敢辞藜藿之陋，将恐桑榆之枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236980_comment'></div>钦咏之私，敷染奚既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236980_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1236980_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236975?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺富知院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236975")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236975'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236975'>伏审丕奉宠休，擢司宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236975_comment'></div>声实无忝，眷属益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236975_comment'></div>凡在芘休，与有荣耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236975_comment'></div>窃以有世臣者，所谓故国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236975_comment'></div>建明德者，其后达人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236975_comment'></div>岂特为阶闼奇异之观，寔能任邦家辅相之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236975_comment'></div>以才业之绝异，正名位之穹窿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236975_comment'></div>无替茂勋，复仍旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236975_comment'></div>副朝廷之企伫，厌华夏之倾瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236975_comment'></div>惟兹右武之要权，思得佐时之机略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236975_comment'></div>虽俎豆坟典之事，吾儒守文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236975_comment'></div>而鼙鼓金革之间，诸将易得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236975_comment'></div>措世大安则有道，使敌远遁则贵谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236975_comment'></div>顷刻微差，安危所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236975_comment'></div>呼吸生变，裁处尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236975_comment'></div>折冲于帷幄之间，度兵于枕席之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236975_comment'></div>六奇五间之策，可应无穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236975_comment'></div>九流七略之术，何所不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236975_comment'></div>是由文墨之士，自许驱驰之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236975_comment'></div>侧闻登庸，实允佥议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236975_comment'></div>伏惟枢密端明性与道合，意叶才周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236975_comment'></div>闭户揣摩，已仪式文王之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236975_comment'></div>前席献纳，实启沃高宗之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236975_comment'></div>有长国家之令名，以安社稷而为悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236975_comment'></div>约身厉操，比卢怀真之清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236975_comment'></div>因事建言，若萧望之之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236975_comment'></div>屡酌兽樽之美，痛绳旧洿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236975_comment'></div>最详马栈之施，独予善类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236975_comment'></div>务农蓄聚，训兵俟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236975_comment'></div>以代谋为奇功，以自守为进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236975_comment'></div>驯致辽夏之修好，庶几魏晋之复归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236975_comment'></div>度越前芳，非但无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236975_comment'></div>籀末品下秩，绵力散材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236975_comment'></div>不因笔牍之仪文，莫叙松萝之附倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236975_comment'></div>意向殊切，宣写难周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236975_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1236975_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在闽为官，有文。作品：《跋摹连昌宫辞》《跋惠州芳华洲刻石》<div id='poem_1237042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋摹连昌宫辞<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237042")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237042'>伯祖东坡先生尝为《易传》，以真书发扬伏羲、西伯之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237042_comment'></div>岭海草书，老笔精劲，自云不愧二王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237042_comment'></div>遭乱后，家藏书帖散失略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237042_comment'></div>尚明所摹《连昌宫辞》，顿还伯英旧观，而过于贺拔恕数倍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237042_comment'></div>书虽哲人细事，心慕手追如此，其大者鲜不深造，故余三叹而屡嘉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237042_comment'></div>绍兴改元十月日，苏籀题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1237042_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋惠州芳华洲刻石</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237045")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237045'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237045'>延平范公智闻使君，恬于荣进，自诡治民，不鄙夷峤南之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237045_comment'></div>鹅城左江右湖，想其城如堤防，民如雁鹜，屋如舟舫，树如菰蒲，故有古榜嘉名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237045_comment'></div>造物特发其秘，以遗公观，公与诸贤所记备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237045_comment'></div>或曰：「荒裔茅筱，与蛟人蜑户错杂，氛祲毒雾，发作无节，非华风矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237045_comment'></div>惟公能以循吏恻怛之实，尽心抚育，令闻晔然以光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237045_comment'></div>茀厥茨莠，化为廒仓，物无疵疠而户口增，山有嘉卉而桑果茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237045_comment'></div>尚儒而士甚文，遏寇而民益丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237045_comment'></div>芳流华显，名不虚应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237045_comment'></div>公夙有诗谶，与今石刻符合，岂偶然也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237045_comment'></div>期公奉三年计最，归报九重，用其实学，藻饰寰海，使品汇无凋枯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237045_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237045_comment'></div>出处有命，皆非人力，世人妄生欣愠，误矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237045_comment'></div>览芳华洲之事，可见也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1237045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在闽为官，有诗。作品：《东山一首》<div id='poem_139788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东山一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139788")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_139788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139788'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139788'>肮脏田官委吏偕，山于吾属倍青哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139788'>星言舆轿蒙茏里，山半振衣嚣鬨埃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139788'>针水布畦春泽匝，吟风夹路岁寒来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139788'>架岩刳木泉悲响，锁洞白云花烂开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139788'>灰冷虚堂敷白氎，爨清一饭脯青苔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139788'>欲求出世三空义，一咄疏狂道眼裁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139788'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_139788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　韩世忠、程迈平息范汝为之乱，光复建州，苏籀作诗。作品：《群盗》<div id='poem_139895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群盗一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139895")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139895'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139895'>贪得不知义，流风紊四维。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139895'>圭珇实盲昏，黥髡亦觊窥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139895'>谅非蹠蹻才，竞揭椎埋旗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139895'>巨猾肆滔天，小丑争攘欺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139895'>立国计安出，顾无以家为。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139895'>三州破竹势，吏卒伤挠隳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139895'>越人竟何能，非复尉佗时。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139895'>壶箪迎王旅，克捷剑之湄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139895'>闽府幸宴然，一毫未尝亏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139895'>噫吾有以待，致尔由他歧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139895'>残檗失追袭，诸将咸思归。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139895'>勉哉方伯职，力拯邻邦危。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139895'>漳滨拿未解，蜂蝎生武夷。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139895'>姑息倒囷藏，谆复行文移。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139895'>近事苟目前，远忧那敢知。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139895'>天运未太平，佛力亦其微。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139895'>武夫勿告劳，儒冠须出奇。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139895'>知人与安民，此责诚塞之。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139895'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_139895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　时李纲在福州，力劝韩世忠宽宥协从，苏籀作《上李丞相书》<div id='poem_1236963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上李丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236963")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236963'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236963'>恭闻大人之道，其高者登天，其深者潜泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236963_comment'></div>告之于人主，施之于四方，端伟咺赫，不名一器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236963_comment'></div>其在衮司，如斗如岳，指迷当世，镇服四夷，可否予夺，公议灼然，其外可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236963_comment'></div>其胸中之嗜好，尚德爱义，断可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236963_comment'></div>故无古今，无荣贱，取兹两者而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236963_comment'></div>仰惟崇堂钜屏，簪履奔向，投刺如栉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236963_comment'></div>一介之贱，束带以干门隶，求彻声闻于左右，草野唐突，诚可笑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236963_comment'></div>至于贪慕德义，则岂必疏于众宾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236963_comment'></div>夫绛、灌鼎贵，或不工文，霍、卫显重，鲜能喜士，则儒道何施欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236963_comment'></div>今日以斯道觉群黎，岂非在阁下耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236963_comment'></div>其为人也，挟至足体要之学，操梗切根本之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236963_comment'></div>爱君纳谏，革容悦之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236963_comment'></div>理乱振兵，破蓄缩之敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236963_comment'></div>气充区宇，名满四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236963_comment'></div>横翔捷出，间两社而总八柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236963_comment'></div>又方当盛壮之年，附之以韩、魏而初不矜，劫之以贲、育而未尝惕，眩之以儒墨之辩而不失其所是，投之以麇鼯之野而不挠其所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236963_comment'></div>伊、傅、周、召、狐、管、乐、萧，彼何人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236963_comment'></div>光于鼎常，耀于竹帛，拔天下之大艰，拯天下之大患，以为己任，随机应变，有馀裕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236963_comment'></div>阁下方且澹然渊哉，燕居无作，其实负素望，飨厚秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236963_comment'></div>比牒同时者已耋，当轴处中者晚进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236963_comment'></div>故夫格天之事业，物议所不置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236963_comment'></div>夫韦编蠹简，谈经䌷史，此亦盛美奇事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236963_comment'></div>治一卷书与治天下，闲剧之不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236963_comment'></div>又如释道二家，苦空妙义之宗，服食修炼之伎，此于养生则厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236963_comment'></div>治一身与治天下，缓急之不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236963_comment'></div>虽然，阁下高翔远步，以轩冕为絷维，以世味为浮云，视衮绣二府与黄冠白屋无异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236963_comment'></div>朝廷之倚任，有识之责望，在彼而不在此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236963_comment'></div>窃以谓有所闻见，不当缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236963_comment'></div>大计深虑，以安社稷为悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236963_comment'></div>示体国情义之亲，不亦宗工之任乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236963_comment'></div>或曰：「道之难行也，则如之何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236963_comment'></div>夫事固有小大，小者何足以云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236963_comment'></div>至于系安危成败，众所未察，我之独见，言出而后计从，亦何可缄默耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236963_comment'></div>且夫当朝岂无似韦处厚者，则在外有如裴中立，势不容久淹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236963_comment'></div>至于任贤使能，中兴之本，又阁下之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236963_comment'></div>今欲得常才之士，以无旷职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236963_comment'></div>欲得奇才之士，以共理世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236963_comment'></div>夷易其所入之途，使来者虚徐而自得，封植而淬励之，赏拔甄品，岂获已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236963_comment'></div>迩来丧乱之极，必将升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236963_comment'></div>阁下与凡门下之贤俊，实任其事，必将卓然大副天子之意，炳然审天工之付委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236963_comment'></div>言尽用，道尽行，朝廷得策，生灵晏粲，百官称职，殪戎正华，勋绩筹略，非我辈之所能测知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236963_comment'></div>只如本路群贼，阁下原其祸端由杀子之报，辞切理明，刻于路隅，凶党化之，油然忠孝之心生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236963_comment'></div>悯时忧世之所蕴，可窥其一斑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236963_comment'></div>一介踵阍者，未可以语人才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236963_comment'></div>大钧之播，其肯自弃乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236963_comment'></div>伏念昔日承平，书狱讼法律者三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236963_comment'></div>猃狁之故，调军实、论攻战者又累任，皆蹭蹬而无功，过则鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236963_comment'></div>椟藏旧书经传，略备陋目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236963_comment'></div>得一忘十，时求梦奠老人之旨，行诵而坐思之，不忍弃大而嗜琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236963_comment'></div>四十之仕，齿发将老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236963_comment'></div>九品之秩，炊舂无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236963_comment'></div>仰企光尘衰钝之踪，庶未摈斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236963_comment'></div>昔者郭驼鄙人，而理民者取之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236963_comment'></div>梓人卑冗，而相天下者取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236963_comment'></div>辄冒献其猖狂之说，有合于大人之道者，亦养木作室之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236963_comment'></div>至于谀而慕势，则不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236963_comment'></div>所祈向者德义，不可诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236963_comment'></div>才下论卑，幸垂照焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236963_comment'></div>如赐一字之惠以奖其进，执经秉笔，将继此而有请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236963_comment'></div>敢悉布之，可否惟命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236963_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1236963_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在闽为官，有诗。作品：《次韵待制王公出示李公丞相鼓山唱和之什不揆芜累奉和一首》《次韵王丈丰父待制荔枝诗二十韵》<div id='poem_139834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵待制王公出示李公丞相鼓山唱和之什不揆芜累奉和一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139834")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139834'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139834'>颙昂经世量，超轶尘秕净。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139834'>猗欤寻山屐，泛矣随波艇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139834'>颜笔振岩崖，戎眼清水镜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139834'>平籋青云步，何如苍藓蹬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139834'>忘怀挈伯雅，寓意弹韵磬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139834'>物外赤松期，域中兜率夐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139834'>江溟嘘吸际，霞祲廓亏映。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139834'>龙象千础攒，簦屩十方并。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139834'>弥天各纵辩，酌海终弗罄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139834'>公侯诚得一，品物将大定。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139834'>瞿昙旧摽蕝，嵌洞尤奇胜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139834'>雷唱涧流回，石刻惟人竞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139834'>半山琅玕响，一井玻瓈莹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139834'>松风瀑水合，时鸟慁人听。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139834'>慷慨羊邹游，雍容裴白并。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139834'>溪谷有佳色，题品益光幸。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139834'>渭滨行将猎，诏促预参乘。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139834'>王公居客右，羊舌偕赵孟。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139834'>小人缪好事，大册挟晨暝。<div id='poem_sentence_18_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_139834'>击节穆清风，续骚聊比兴。<div id='poem_sentence_19_139834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_139834'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_139834_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵王丈丰父待制荔枝二十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139821")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_139821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139821'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139821'>叶实根株尚老苍，龙鳞皋比贵先尝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139821'>千林断送诗骚酒，三绝无逾色味芗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139821'>烂酝恢台养风骨，涵滋沆瀣结天浆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139821'>怕寒僻处深于越，贽贡无阶遇有唐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139821'>葱郁梧楸共庭户，风流芝玉秀斋房。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139821'>剖缄绛锦纷狼藉，莹手摩尼可比方。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139821'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_139821", 139821, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>赪卵</span>鳞皴雄俎豆，双珠同蒂媚钗梁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139821'>摘忧林薄明朝竭，缪论蕉卢几许黄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139821'>口腹定非孤寓客，甘腴尽道胜吾乡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139821'>峡山高咏诗昌白，韶石英风赋予张。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139821'>芍药亦能烦驿置，蒲萄岂必擅西凉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139821'>弹圜金橘差坚久，瑛赤含桃讵可双。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139821'>逆目提笼过阛阓，解颐梦渴吸湖江。<div id='poem_sentence_12_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_139821'>仲宣鸿笔丝纶手，摩诘清才黼藻光。<div id='poem_sentence_13_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_139821'>妙绝拣枝墙欲动，纤攕称<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去声。）</span>擘侍于傍。<div id='poem_sentence_14_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_139821'>翰林纪绩延真赏，县长绳愆且弥忘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_139821'>赐燕行看与怀核，分题今日记升堂。<div id='poem_sentence_16_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_139821'>伤时有似少陵杜，上疏岂惟临武羌。<div id='poem_sentence_17_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_139821'>深忌河豚恕瑶柱，沈思橄榄过糖霜。<div id='poem_sentence_18_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_139821'>词情鉴裁俱超卓，促召龙墀献皂囊。<div id='poem_sentence_19_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_139821'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_139821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_139821'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_139821_0'>⑴ 自注：先伯祖云：莫遣骚人说功过。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_139821_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月</a>　在闽为官，与邓肃有诗唱和。作品：《次韵邓志宏三月辛卯大雨雹》<div id='poem_139822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵邓志宏三月辛卯大雨雹</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139822")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139822'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139822'>剥圭碎璧昆山颓，天容黯惨凝不开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139822'>隋和抵鹊虎兕吼，阳愆阴伏推从来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139822'>雀鼠怀安怖入壁，声侔海翻星陨石。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139822'>疾雷破山万壑沸，急雨悬河平地尺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139822'>嘉生春浅才纤毫，季子御雹勤嗟嗥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139822'>冲冲凿冰穷谷里，申丰此说殊未高。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139822'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_139822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月</a>　在闽为官，有文。作品：《跋海棠梦大字》《跋东坡拔豕帖》《题崧岭图》<div id='poem_1237043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋海棠梦大字<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237043")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237043'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237043'>猗欤伟欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237043_comment'></div>如见真本，庶几遗范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237043_comment'></div>赝者果能乱真耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237043_comment'></div>但瞠然慕叹耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237043_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237043_comment'></div>世人不得于心，勿求于笔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237043_comment'></div>其或笔骄，心不竞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237043_comment'></div>勉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237043_comment'></div>到圣处可谓善学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237043_comment'></div>绍兴二祀季春下旬，苏籀题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1237043_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋东坡拔豕帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237044")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237044_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237044'>先生早年在岐下写《楚词》一章，云似钟繇行体，笔能趁意，是时书画已绝出世俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237044_comment'></div>自壮逮老，周游四方，古人奇迹，无不临遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237044_comment'></div>峤南书帖，特为超妙，尝戏语云可比二王，所谓七十而从心不踰矩者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237044_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237044_comment'></div>虽天资殊异，亦须积习，始蹈大成，况常常者其可不勉耶！</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1237044_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237046' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237046?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题崧岭图<span class='inlineComment2'>（钱）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237046")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237046'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237046'>服道笃习水墨，幻云雾，走山海，笔力尤壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237046_comment'></div>细察其层叠高下，施设算数，繁悉杪忽，出意无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237046_comment'></div>体乎天造，厌于人情，可谓精能，老而不倦者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237046_comment'></div>尺素片纸，极目洒落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237046_comment'></div>此图，仆故山也，观二室间林壑寥落，使人增感怀耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1237046_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　四月庚午，翟汝文自翰林学士承旨、左中大夫、知制诰除参知政事，苏籀作贺表。作品：《贺翟参政启》<div id='poem_1236982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺翟参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236982")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236982'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236982'>伏审光膺制命，参贰衮司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236982_comment'></div>股肱惟人，典刑增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236982_comment'></div>系兵民之欣属，符夷夏之倾瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236982_comment'></div>温恭逊避以得之，将顺谋明之至矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236982_comment'></div>洪惟向道之主，必有命世之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236982_comment'></div>稽古以制今，吁谟而果断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236982_comment'></div>当天下之剧务，酌时变之机宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236982_comment'></div>首陈尧舜于前，大安社稷以悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236982_comment'></div>出于口而成于手，塞其责而获其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236982_comment'></div>乃者给赐锋车，虚伫已久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236982_comment'></div>逮夫入亲法座，见晚兴褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236982_comment'></div>重烦词翰之林，遂付机衡之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236982_comment'></div>卓然自结于中扆，俞哉甚眷于宗工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236982_comment'></div>拱揖庙堂，镇弭横溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236982_comment'></div>伏惟参政相公圭璋大器，鸿鹄高飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236982_comment'></div>道有觉于后来，才庶几于前辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236982_comment'></div>摘风骚之奇致，体训诰之坦明，迈轶《两京》，兼该《七略》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236982_comment'></div>伟中兴之石画，妙正始之金声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236982_comment'></div>难进易退而群士推，提纲正纪而万事理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236982_comment'></div>久处閒燕，无竞荣光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236982_comment'></div>自得孤高，公议咸予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236982_comment'></div>众狂且稚，弃衡石而妄量；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236982_comment'></div>道阻且长，却骐骥而不御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236982_comment'></div>名望难掩，时命大来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236982_comment'></div>管夷吾治于高傒，郑罕虎知夫东里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236982_comment'></div>务在救衰而已乱，未尝苟且以即安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236982_comment'></div>陆相之术弥精，贾生之言悉用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236982_comment'></div>下九天之膏泽，出万国于穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236982_comment'></div>神助人谋，淮淝俟《常武》之举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236982_comment'></div>飙驱电扫，河洛快《匪风》之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236982_comment'></div>运动英谋，已得全策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236982_comment'></div>并鼓作于贤杰，致风俗于太康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236982_comment'></div>籀仰止门阑，视效绳矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236982_comment'></div>误垂善诱，洞照空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236982_comment'></div>深思自托于陶镕，庶免排抑于糠秕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236982_comment'></div>干彼县令，饰小说以徒劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236982_comment'></div>浑于俗徒，谒大巫而自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236982_comment'></div>敝帚猖狂于英衮，苍蝇瞠若乎芳尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236982_comment'></div>诚依德范之崇，不知形迹之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236982_comment'></div>喜而不寐，允也大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236982_comment'></div>玉树瑶林，尽归抡选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236982_comment'></div>朽株枯蘖，亦出菌芝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236982_comment'></div>窃仰云霄，垂荫圭窦，但切称慕，乌能游扬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1236982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　任谅亦在福州，荐籀，籀作谢表。作品：《谢任参政》<div id='poem_1236986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺任参政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236986")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236986'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236986'>右，籀伏以记室响报，不弃咫尺之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236986_comment'></div>东閤诺延，祗捧联翩之檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236986_comment'></div>伟度英鉴，优遇殊私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236986_comment'></div>训鄙矜愚，深容熟察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236986_comment'></div>拳拳珍仰，盖谋道而非贫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236986_comment'></div>眷眷甄谈，致怀刑而后惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236986_comment'></div>其为光幸，何以克当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236986_comment'></div>念古人之事贤，钦盛美而归往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236986_comment'></div>应对进退之末，讲画指授之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236986_comment'></div>师亲而习专，业勤而志立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236986_comment'></div>咸号登龙之士，皆来隐豹之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236986_comment'></div>扫门执御以服劳，升堂入室之尤密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236986_comment'></div>平时坐论于经旨，他日擢升于庙朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236986_comment'></div>依王公游毂之荣华，仕州县抗尘之汩没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236986_comment'></div>籀一介鲁钝，十年具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236986_comment'></div>才不副心，求称职而安在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236986_comment'></div>学无所就，顾承诲之未闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236986_comment'></div>徒有耽古求善之情，好节慕声之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236986_comment'></div>世不知而奚愠，时所尚之为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236986_comment'></div>希管、萧之荣途，顾仇、梅之末品，求其遇合，实难自媒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236986_comment'></div>譬如弱羽必栖于高松，蛟龙先阶于尺木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236986_comment'></div>蝇附骥而行地，鹏积风而负天，无物不然，惟人犹是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236986_comment'></div>况今词林之根蒂，此时圣上之畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236986_comment'></div>一诺如锡于千金，一见如封于万户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236986_comment'></div>狐裘岂容反衣，不倦挽搂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236986_comment'></div>马栈无取凡材，何祈辑附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236986_comment'></div>寸长尺短，樗散液樠，悦于见知，孰不奋励！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236986_comment'></div>此盖伏遇宫使参政大资清纯养素，博笃通方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236986_comment'></div>协搢绅之公言，被旒冕之听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236986_comment'></div>悯劳以日昃之务，优游于道味之腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236986_comment'></div>学识坚高，谋猷迈远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236986_comment'></div>斥破碎臆说之缪，嗤浮躁少年之狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236986_comment'></div>雅意属于本朝，群情待于爰立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236986_comment'></div>天下有未获之事，渊衷念畀付之谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236986_comment'></div>不止居季、孟之间，行且已杨、陈之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236986_comment'></div>洗六合而攘膻秽，维四方而抚疮痍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236986_comment'></div>救民于水火之中，行师于几席之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236986_comment'></div>为家国深虑而审画，宽君王旰食而宵衣，凡所贤愚，于焉举措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236986_comment'></div>籀舍筦库而领邑，升从事而治中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236986_comment'></div>省循寸进之阶，诚为拙宦之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236986_comment'></div>至若提挈不间乎棣萼，吹嘘悉取于弓箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236986_comment'></div>曷尝小补于纤微，岂意荐叨于宠待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236986_comment'></div>籀敢不服膺惠贶，益勉操修，积累锱铢，增裨远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236986_comment'></div>舟驶舆壮，亦祈众力之同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236986_comment'></div>厦广栋隆，寔惟群木之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236986_comment'></div>孰云小己，无益高闳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236986_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1236986_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月</a>　与洪炎赋荔枝。作品：《和洪玉甫秘监荔枝三首》<div id='poem_139850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和洪玉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>甫秘监荔枝三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139850")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139850_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_139850_0'>① 原作王，据明抄本、粤雅堂本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139850'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139850'>林杪摘星陨，江干疑烧然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139850_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139850'>香包浣花锦，冰质藐姑仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139850_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139850'>巨擘纷璀璨，丁香吐妙妍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139850_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139850'>唐亡倾国笑，何物免罹愆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139850_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139850'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139850_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139694?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139694'>闽中谱殊盛，唐相赋初工。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139694'>万点凝霞赤，三危滴露丛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139694'>驱芦抵乌鹊，投李饫儿童。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139694'>子美吟西蜀，樱桃先后红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139694_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139695?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139695'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139695'>瘴乡骈琐质，善地最蒲闽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139695'>冠绝林间品，难为坐上宾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139695'>蟠桃寿天帝，萍实荐居宸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139695'>无逸为龟策，何烦万马尘<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《双溪集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139695'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　张守知福州，苏籀作迎表。作品：《迎张大资启》<div id='poem_1236983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎张大资启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236983")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236983'>伏审释会稽之组，虚讲读之司，改命鱼符，荐颁节钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236983_comment'></div>渊衷异简，均佚民政之藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236983_comment'></div>海徼东南，悉属天子之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236983_comment'></div>维无诸之都会，杂《禹贡》之岛夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236983_comment'></div>瘠土勤民，连年多事，屡致窃攘之寇，尤难镇靖之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236983_comment'></div>老者安而少者怀，非常才之所任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236983_comment'></div>廉其顽而宽其鄙，皆大贤之所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236983_comment'></div>侧聆休命之行，寔谐中外之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236983_comment'></div>诵十行之语，上恩恻怛于抚存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236983_comment'></div>总八州之人，憬俗慰安于节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236983_comment'></div>威风覃被，谣颂何穷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236983_comment'></div>伏惟知府安抚大资相公达六艺之旨归，该九河之伦类，廊庙之宝，柱石其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236983_comment'></div>磊落万乘之知，咺赫千载之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236983_comment'></div>竭诚论列，百神听而兆人瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236983_comment'></div>将顺谋明，一德协而九畴叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236983_comment'></div>顿纲正纪，虑远烛微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236983_comment'></div>湔涤旧污，帡幪吉士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236983_comment'></div>典诰大语，追还伊、傅之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236983_comment'></div>政理高能，远过龚、黄之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236983_comment'></div>出入将相，师保群黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236983_comment'></div>辍坐论于公朝，难久留于外服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236983_comment'></div>櫜鞬罗拜，改观遐方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236983_comment'></div>韊矢先驱，叨荣属吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236983_comment'></div>平生珍慕，邂逅遭逢，大惧刍荛，有玷幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236983_comment'></div>幸许扬眉于宾次，钦闻溢耳之欢声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236983_comment'></div>延跂来尘，颉颃成厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236983_comment'></div>依向之至，欣颂无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1236983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　有贺张守启。作品：《贺张参政入侍经筵启》<div id='poem_1236990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张参政入觐经筵启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236990")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236990'>伏审竦传急诏，钦想趣装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236990_comment'></div>麟趾金华，异等殊渥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236990_comment'></div>紫枢黄閤，虚位以须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236990_comment'></div>中外乐闻，士夫交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236990_comment'></div>籀尝备官属，企慕光尘，忝荷帡幪，倍切欣喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236990_comment'></div>窃以明主好要，理世须贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236990_comment'></div>帷幄畴咨，春秋起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236990_comment'></div>招延旧德，开济远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236990_comment'></div>慎人物之评，求讨论之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236990_comment'></div>上意先定，佥言允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236990_comment'></div>盖贯悉古今，故能为万世之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236990_comment'></div>博约经术，乃厌服群士之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236990_comment'></div>其在当今，无逾执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236990_comment'></div>伏惟观使侍读大资柔嘉维则，信美且仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236990_comment'></div>莫际波澜，臻极壸奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236990_comment'></div>高文典册，挽回正始之音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236990_comment'></div>经武振兵，允有中兴之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236990_comment'></div>夙参大政，未究吁谟，愈练典刑，不择剧易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236990_comment'></div>凛然岳牧之首，蔚为议论之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236990_comment'></div>惟忧国饥渴之心，见给饷艰难之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236990_comment'></div>至尊叹萧何之杰，训词褒韩滉之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236990_comment'></div>辍保釐于藩维，俾左右于天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236990_comment'></div>赞襄于规随之际，斟酌乎献替之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236990_comment'></div>建功名于鼎彝，形歌颂于竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236990_comment'></div>再念籀罢秩三载，待次一官，大丧其家，托迹无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236990_comment'></div>熊落于槛，攀援奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236990_comment'></div>敢怀侥觊于超升，自安分限之凉薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236990_comment'></div>惟流落之未艾，迫屡空以难堪，仰止高明，未遂遐谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236990_comment'></div>使霖雨遍润于枯槁，丹青粗变于嫫妍，拯拔穷途，允归洪造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236990_comment'></div>殚竭顽质，少答深恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1236990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　有跋文。作品：《跋东坡诗及所书黄门记》<div id='poem_1237047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋任氏东坡诗及所书黄门记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237047")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237047'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237047'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237047_comment'></div>二祖道德之范，见于笔墨，传示来世，不容拟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237047_comment'></div>观其述二大夫乐贤之意，炳然著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237047_comment'></div>辨书真赝，仆粗能焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237047_comment'></div>古人谓辞之不可已，故黾勉而题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237047_comment'></div>是岁九月丙辰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1237047_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　程迈荐苏籀为京官，苏籀作谢启。作品：《谢程殿撰启》<div id='poem_1236981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢程殿撰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236981")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236981'>伏念钦承嘉惠，误玷殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236981_comment'></div>度广包荒，恩多内恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236981_comment'></div>修辞謇讷，愧汗忸怩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236981_comment'></div>窃以选部典常，公庭殿最，铨综既有成宪，考课无失大纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236981_comment'></div>虽奔轶凌厉之人，以为拙宦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236981_comment'></div>而深实详练之士，多出此涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236981_comment'></div>底绩则其宣力也勤，保任则其量才也审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236981_comment'></div>顾藉五斗，更尽三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236981_comment'></div>殚竭云为，仅书中考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236981_comment'></div>黾勉或经于三仕，蹉跌有至于半生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236981_comment'></div>亦知京秩之微芒，冀脱判司之冗琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236981_comment'></div>籀之晚进，自以窭空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236981_comment'></div>希当世之簪缨，岂迂寸步；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236981_comment'></div>望前贤之糟粕，未得一毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236981_comment'></div>彼哉何堪，缺然无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236981_comment'></div>便合倒冠而落佩，岂期结网而羡鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236981_comment'></div>华衮垂只字之褒，敝帚增九鼎之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236981_comment'></div>此盖伏遇知府安抚待制警拔应猝，慎靖察微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236981_comment'></div>学惇及物之诚，辞富辑民之辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236981_comment'></div>窥典册之渊薮，援引古今；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236981_comment'></div>知议论之津源，多识成败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236981_comment'></div>故能扩将帅之韬略，宽国家之顾忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236981_comment'></div>移檄骈联，斥堠绎络；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236981_comment'></div>金谷流衍，器械精良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236981_comment'></div>厚结群心，兹为全策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236981_comment'></div>马首所向，三军伫瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236981_comment'></div>旂尾一挥，众凶屏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236981_comment'></div>不出樽俎，所恃机筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236981_comment'></div>威抚冥顽，部勒勇怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236981_comment'></div>纤悉举措，深副倚毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236981_comment'></div>王良当车，辔无诡窃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236981_comment'></div>医和负笼，剂必珍奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236981_comment'></div>至如籀者，踪迹飘摇，燕幕荣芘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236981_comment'></div>羽翮摧秃，鹗表飞驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236981_comment'></div>老矣转疏，贱而有耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236981_comment'></div>片言小物，不敢代帅而受名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236981_comment'></div>秉心奉公，戒在侵官而冒上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236981_comment'></div>循循乎寅集而酉退，稍稍乎昼访而夜思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236981_comment'></div>庶几摩厉以须，不忝称知之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236981_comment'></div>绣衮当轴，终赖埏陶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236981_comment'></div>诗礼在躬，岂云无补！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236981_comment'></div>再拂箧中之笔，仰谢终出之锥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236981_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1236981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　与范子仪等游福州东山、升山、怡山。作品：《招范子仪登升山次范韵》《次韵范子仪怡山饭讫访王仙君旧迹一首》《次韵范子仪东山之什》<div id='poem_139697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>招范子仪登升山次范韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139697")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139697'>束带殊憎市声沸，幅巾聊复隐居寻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139697'>凌虚马鞍林峦表，滴翠驼裘涧谷深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139697'>个里膏肓空自许，何期烟雨挠重临。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139697'>长瓶大白开狂喙，绝海驱山叹未禁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139697_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵范子仪怡山饭讫访王仙君旧迹一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_3_139755'>作吏天涯何所得，一春黄卷伴芳樽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139755'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139755_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陋居一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139705")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139705'>平生瓮牖蔀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>茆菁，江左那无寸土宁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139705'>游宦飘然纡幕燕，陋居粗有读书萤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139705'>浮生佛脚须当抱，乱世儒衣便欲停。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139705'>天定灾祥在淫善，北溟安得胜南溟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139705'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_139705'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_139705_0'>⑴ 原作部，据明抄本、粤雅堂本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_139705_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1236918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闽岭赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236918")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236918'>习被卉而用夷兮，极东南之海山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236918_comment'></div>叹造化之瑰诡兮，想禹绩之间关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236918_comment'></div>降丘坦其郭郛兮，曰无诸之市阛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236918_comment'></div>步窈窕经崎岖兮，获清穹而考槃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236918_comment'></div>陟越王之宫址兮，与升鼓之孱颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之体，既合别而贯属兮，又竞爽而丛攒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236918_comment'></div>蔽亏日月兮，横挂斗参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236918_comment'></div>臂趾根蘖兮，插万仞之海澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236918_comment'></div>上下左右兮，夷倾峻弯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236918_comment'></div>如削如染兮，奔峭多端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之气，溜耶燔耶兮，迫之难看。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236918_comment'></div>乍彤乍黑兮，纷郁蒙𩆓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236918_comment'></div>飓氛梅霪有阖辟兮，霍然雾除，圜顾而巑岏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之德，阴谷冥冥，崇朝多雨兮，阳坡茀茀，绿缛而难删。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236918_comment'></div>孕产金玉兮，栖集龙鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236918_comment'></div>屏鸩却蝮兮，庶类以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之险，天作百隘，虎落吴楚兮，盗攘罔干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236918_comment'></div>地脉络而无蹙兮，海不能以益宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之人，秦汉蛮夷兮，近世衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236918_comment'></div>未暇念夫庐阜兮，每帽欹而足酸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之望，雁台峤泷，邪界连延兮，潮汐喷射，撞水裔之坚顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236918_comment'></div>鲸鲵澒洞兮，渤澥㳽漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236918_comment'></div>掉心骇目兮，阔视纵观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236918_comment'></div>惟此山之游，倍于吴蜀，竞丹刻兮，招提刹竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236918_comment'></div>轮奂千所兮，敷译经教，架壑而冠岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236918_comment'></div>洪崖洞穴兮，天设神剜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236918_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236918_comment'></div>达人之既逝兮，有往牒之未刊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236918_comment'></div>俛仰谈笑兮，木杪云间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236918_comment'></div>搜奇践胜兮，领略莫殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236918_comment'></div>其石狠怪兮，岚薰而藓斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236918_comment'></div>蹲象舞马兮，麋麚踞蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236918_comment'></div>其泉清冽兮，嵌窦泻湍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236918_comment'></div>泄乳停膏兮，淙琤佩环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236918_comment'></div>万斛沸滚兮，灌浴体胖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236918_comment'></div>其果珍异兮，荔蕉黄柑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236918_comment'></div>地不爱宝兮，填谷映峦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236918_comment'></div>其木搀错兮，松桂榕楠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236918_comment'></div>千尺离奇兮，龙起熊攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236918_comment'></div>荣耀隆冬兮，时令犯干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236918_comment'></div>蓊茸晻霭兮，翡翠缨缦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236918_comment'></div>射干薜荔兮，美箭檀栾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236918_comment'></div>被覆缘连兮，薋菉荑兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236918_comment'></div>叱吸唱嗥兮，天籁自欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236918_comment'></div>吟啸啼喁兮，嘤嘤啧烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236918_comment'></div>形色声味，山灵千变以娱人兮，逃虚而却其神奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236918_comment'></div>岚光著于眉睫兮，清赏痼于脾肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236918_comment'></div>嗟此邦人兮，缩衣晏飧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236918_comment'></div>南亩萍布兮，田毛实悭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236918_comment'></div>蔗林芋区兮，萧散江滩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236918_comment'></div>水流通川，故居之而不疾兮，交锁岪郁，故隆暑而微寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236918_comment'></div>屈、宋未尝录兮，班、马非所般。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236918_comment'></div>隘狭欹侧兮，吁嗟永叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236918_comment'></div>济时利物兮，云扰大艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236918_comment'></div>救焚拯溺兮，君子不闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236918_comment'></div>引领浚都兮，恨无羽翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236918_comment'></div>石髓暂遇兮，金丹一钻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236918_comment'></div>白日青天兮，孰曰到难<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236918_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1236918'>溜：库本作「馏」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1236918_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉安镇闽王祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237067")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237067'>维神消禳患灾，仁爱国土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237067_comment'></div>闻于行阙，加崇大号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237067_comment'></div>恩宠甚渥，名实相当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237067_comment'></div>籀等钦奉新命，书勒标榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237067_comment'></div>繄聪毅之鉴，锡安靖之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237067_comment'></div>伏惟尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1237067_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b23f22a9153d4c868f0da5f4faca0f3d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b23f22a9153d4c868f0da5f4faca0f3d");'><span id='b23f22a9153d4c868f0da5f4faca0f3d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1137')">1133-1137年</a>，43-47岁</div><div id='b23f22a9153d4c868f0da5f4faca0f3d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年10月</a>　回朝。以右宣义郎为大宗正丞。作品：《拟上赵相公书》<div id='poem_1236966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟上赵相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236966")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236966'>恭惟理世之要，澄源拯敝，纤悉举措，罔非大公至正而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236966_comment'></div>伏闻朝论，吏员猥众，缺次极少，率一官而五人共之，一人任职四人待次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236966_comment'></div>仕者无穷，而常员有限，填咽充塞，不可区处，有至十年而后之任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236966_comment'></div>本祈奖拔之多，而贤路迫隘至于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236966_comment'></div>近制，中都官待次者并罢斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236966_comment'></div>详味美意，戒于汎滥，务在精切，此举非不善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236966_comment'></div>前岁修废，除用诸丞，所添不过三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236966_comment'></div>今者概行朝兵府僚属，以次皆黜之，不下七八十人，其閒不容稍留矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236966_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236966_comment'></div>以人物为怀，以宗社为悦，毅然确然，自任休戚而后及此，灼见阁下之心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236966_comment'></div>《传》曰：「治本在得人，得人在审举，审举在核实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236966_comment'></div>古之用人，取之至宽，用之至狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236966_comment'></div>取之宽，故贤者不隔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236966_comment'></div>用之狭，故不肖者无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236966_comment'></div>夫披沙以求金，其始未弃沙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236966_comment'></div>舂糠以取米，其始兼取糠也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236966_comment'></div>终藉陶汰、簸扬之功耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236966_comment'></div>自今公举慎选，官曹之清必矣，士之黜者，谁不曰然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236966_comment'></div>或者以谓舍之则藏，今既舍矣，则宜远举遐引，奉祠宫，从农圃而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236966_comment'></div>其长者以为安义命，坚特操，读书立言，贵于行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236966_comment'></div>修身正家，以治国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236966_comment'></div>自进之路尚广，长逝山林则过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236966_comment'></div>阁下统理中外，奖擢延引，覆载之内，跂行喙息，皆有赖于庇庥，而士大夫不蒙垂荫，理有不当然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236966_comment'></div>夫一意于退，自薄自弃者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236966_comment'></div>自奋自励者，岂钜其无取乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236966_comment'></div>彼七八十人中，其志意才略尚有人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236966_comment'></div>今夫天下之势，方且倒悬，神州陆沉，未能雪复，夷狄凭陵，腥秽寰宇，此正用才求贤之急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236966_comment'></div>夫负能挟策，自以绝出常流，则悯世忧时，亦谁能默坐而已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236966_comment'></div>亦不容逝去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236966_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236966_comment'></div>才之难也，吾君吾相岂终弃人也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236966_comment'></div>所黜七八十人者，岂将使失其职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236966_comment'></div>夫古之逐客，有复为尊官、成大功名者矣，三黜五去，复被礼遇者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236966_comment'></div>至于鄙夷厌贱，遏绝忽略，则识者不敢以此期阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236966_comment'></div>意者鉴裁称量，丹青造化已素定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236966_comment'></div>唐崔祐甫除吏八百，时无遗才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236966_comment'></div>裴垍荐士三十馀人，朝野翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236966_comment'></div>二子尚能然，是岂足以概论高明乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236966_comment'></div>士之无能、无求、无思、无欲，可以投闲散、群冗士者，莫如籀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236966_comment'></div>罢斥数中，不在有无多少之间，恃阁下之在上，犹复一鸣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236966_comment'></div>亦尝承风旨，辱轸念，自惟身贱迹疏，而有再三之渎，惶悚无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236966_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236966_comment'></div>自待固不忍薄，待阁下亦敢不厚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236966_comment'></div>今天下所谓魁垒豪杰，功业隆重，阁下当轴，实无忝焉，与天下之士共建皇极，固优为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236966_comment'></div>自惟非刘禹锡之才誉而求牛僧孺之知，乏杜牧之谋猷而觊李德裕之用，亦已难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236966_comment'></div>倘尚宽其愚，训其拙，未忘掇拾之意，实以有道贫贱为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236966_comment'></div>若夫流落无归，至于累年，私事也，非敢辄言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236966_comment'></div>经术道义，学于前哲，公论也，其或小用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236966_comment'></div>结发读书，白首不辍，亦尝侧闻长者之风，而窃窥梦奠老人之意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236966_comment'></div>庶几用其道，并其人试之以伎，效之以官，飞一檄，驰一传，裨补尘露，书生之事也，敢不勉焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236966_comment'></div>「吉甫作颂，穆如清风」，平生所慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236966_comment'></div>恭惟今春虏犯淮泗，阁下实为首相，捍患御灾之际，举无遗策，虏以败北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236966_comment'></div>诚愿纪述盛德大业，被之金石，以追配古中兴之佐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236966_comment'></div>狂斐干冒，俯伏俟罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236966_comment'></div>不宣<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236966_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1236966'>「非敢」至「小用」：原错简在前，据右引移补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1236966_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　尝代人谢时相吕颐浩。作品：《代谢吕相启》<div id='poem_1236971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代谢吕丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236971")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236971'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236971'>右，某蒙恩受前件差遣，已于某月某日赴上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236971_comment'></div>分安僻壤，自便养疴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236971_comment'></div>祗奉恩光，仰烦造物，揽辔沃若，握节慨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236971_comment'></div>抚民夷风俗之殊，斡山泽财币之夥，详味奖予，恐惧叨尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236971_comment'></div>伏念某少不逮人，老未更事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236971_comment'></div>初无进擢之望，终冀循良之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236971_comment'></div>华省振缨，穷途失子，哀悴所迫，衰疢相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236971_comment'></div>恳悃一陈，光荣曲被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236971_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官帝所奇宝，王佐异才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236971_comment'></div>社稷元功，扫阊阖之氛祲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236971_comment'></div>邦家系望，补衮职之工能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236971_comment'></div>国是定而纪纲明，兵势强而奸邪伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236971_comment'></div>书鼎彝而显赫，大陶冶以埏镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236971_comment'></div>致兹一介之微，亦获寸长之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236971_comment'></div>量才受任，藏疾包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236971_comment'></div>某敢不收晚暮之桑榆，增太山于尘露，庶几一篑，以补万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236971_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1236971_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　汲西湖东坡所浚井。作品：《汲东坡所浚井》<div id='poem_139663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汲东坡所浚井一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139663")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139663'>帅贰英英驻节旄，继唐流泽便滔滔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139663'>源深东绝三桥市，涨缩西湖二寸篙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139663'>沟驶甃坚无旱潦，瓶翻筒漏饮豚羔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139663'>私家诵佛千畦稻，官帑收功万斛醪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139663_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　吕稽中为川陕都督属官，苏籀为诗寄之。作品：《寄吕德元时为都督属二绝》<div id='poem_139620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄吕德元时为督府属二绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139620")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_139620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139620'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139620'>稍费江南万侧釐，多誊符檄喻亡齐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139620'>宽然折箠可入汴，已见票姚擒日磾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139620'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_139620_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139621?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_139621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139621'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139621'>祖生晚节并刘琨，独免声消贾谧尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139621'>虎士淮淝初小捷，谢庭兰玉绝常伦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139621'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_139621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年2月</a>　张浚自川陕都督任召还，论者劾其“五月在外，误国非一”，三月罢任。苏籀曾与之论兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月</a>　五月，友人韩昂进士及第，为常山主簿，苏籀作诗送行。作品：《韩簿之常山送行一首》<div id='poem_139891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韩簿之常山送行一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139891")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_139891_comment'></div><div
