class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139891'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139891'>苍隼卑飞亦将击，素琴不拟贵高张。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139891'>勾稽俛首亲朱墨，甘旨役心谋稻粱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139891'>吏干能称追伯仲，朝端近例寘周行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139891'>题名塔庙经坊市，俯瞷烟云越涧冈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139891'>相勉三馀牵著拟，助栽九畹待芬芳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139891'>絷维骐骥初从轭，强劲蒹葭要饱霜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139891'>县小官閒无甚责，秩卑俸薄又何伤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139891'>公田私亩工夫遍，世阀前修在激昂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139891'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_139891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在临安。有诗。作品：《常山主簿题名记》《瑞香一首呈韩子平》<div id='poem_1237061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常山县主簿题名记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237061")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237061'>衢所隶五县，西曰常山，溪谷回阻，曩时号为岩险僻左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237061_comment'></div>比年圣上驻跸临安，冠盖旁午，甲兵往来，乃江、湖、闽、广水陆之冲，坌为孔道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237061_comment'></div>津驿廪库之吏与其舆台迓劳无虚日，事倍蓰于旁近他邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237061_comment'></div>然县令之次，有尉无簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237061_comment'></div>夫百里赋政，非有佐贰，何以办治？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237061_comment'></div>譬如羽翮修而鸿鹄举，宫商应而琴瑟调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237061_comment'></div>苟补左而缺右，有唱而弗和，殆不济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237061_comment'></div>簿之于令，联事而不逼，分劳而不专，上下咸以置之为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237061_comment'></div>绍兴四年二月庚申，资政殿大学士、宣奉大夫阳夏郡谢公任伯知军州事，言于朝，吾友韩君昴子平实被选辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237061_comment'></div>越三月某日，奉命视事，因旧废馆缮公廨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237061_comment'></div>君以谢公见用之意，不陋枳棘，不懈箴儆，所治者虽小，务知者大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237061_comment'></div>出入朱墨，钩校精覈，一毫必利于公上，一豆不落于人手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237061_comment'></div>于文无害，其长蒙成，众谓称其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237061_comment'></div>至于沿牒而稽经决狱，弦歌而乘间摄县，嚬呻纤悉，情伪洞晓，盖有补当今、见思异日者甚多焉，故当路数数荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237061_comment'></div>逮终更伊迩，书来告曰：「凡官舍皆刻石题名，创制兹职，肇自我先，子为记之，以贻后政之君子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237061_comment'></div>余窃以古人谨始必书，夫兴废当理则见称，图治宜民则可纪，可纪虽黄绶传不朽，不然，虽千驷无足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237061_comment'></div>矧贤牧伯之首建明，而吾友效官如此，不患湮沦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237061_comment'></div>姑妄书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237061_comment'></div>绍兴六年六月十日，眉山苏籀记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1237061_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139770' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139770' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139770?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瑞香一首呈韩子平</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139770")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139770_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139770'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139770'>未拆娇红浅紫骈，差差众叶翠翘然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139770'>误称兰艳风流冠，且纵桃夭万一怜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139770'>列槛闭帷增峭烈，诉杯阁笔负婵娟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139770'>司花处子春风面，醲态奇香想象焉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139770'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139770_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月</a>　赵鼎被命都督川、陕、荆、襄，苏籀上书。作品：《上赵枢密都督书》<div id='poem_1236965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上赵枢密都督书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236965")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236965'>愚窃闻朝廷大臣系时理乱，惟文武兼资，则可以有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236965_comment'></div>今日国步艰难，譬如解髋髀者，不可婴以芒刃斧斤，砺而已矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236965_comment'></div>支倾坏者，不暇顾夫藻棁栋梁，壮而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236965_comment'></div>盖惟文可以附众，惟武可以威敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236965_comment'></div>入相则百度正，出师则四夷服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236965_comment'></div>古之人解兜鍪而冠貂蝉，自廊庙而履行阵，投壶而讲策画，缓带而观经传，乘胜决机，气势盈溢，丹青所画，竹帛所纪，皆文武之大才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236965_comment'></div>时危而用不武之人，有禅僧放鹰之喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236965_comment'></div>治远者必自近始，欲治夷狄，先辑中国，外内皆重任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236965_comment'></div>伟人在朝，知无不为，岂惮勤剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236965_comment'></div>搢绅属望，猛悍屈伏，咸愿其当轴处中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236965_comment'></div>然使其坐论王霸，燕安鸩毒，桑梓之邦，陷于涂炭，岂得不慨于怀乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236965_comment'></div>夫以隐情惜己为持重，厌事茍安为待时，则何贵乎智勇，何尚于功名乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236965_comment'></div>惟其英杰之度，专意兴复，忘家徇国，所以殊绝于凡庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236965_comment'></div>往者纲维不振，士风回邪，谈虚无、注篆刻以为儒术，厚包苴、弃韬钤而取将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236965_comment'></div>今其遗臭未远，馀孽或存，戎钺之寄，实难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236965_comment'></div>夷狄凭陵，中原膻秽，良以此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236965_comment'></div>冕弁端委之伦，非其能超轶世俗，改途易向，则何以步骤周宣中兴之佐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236965_comment'></div>主上励精，阁下激昂，吴越非劲兵健马之所出，关陇有胁从思汉之人心，多士盈庭，皆未易当此重任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236965_comment'></div>以阁下精治道，见兵势，以帝王之法则裁治中司，以桓文之节制抚循二镇，有恻怛绥靖之实，无侥倖行险之失，凛乎经世御军之略，信有文武之威风矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236965_comment'></div>故丝纶布出陕、蜀、荆、沔，先声万里之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236965_comment'></div>士卒凫藻，黔首壤歌，必相庆以为得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236965_comment'></div>识者谓吴之强弱在蜀之安危，蜀之安危在陇之向背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236965_comment'></div>夫骑兵出于陇右，而财赋从蜀来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236965_comment'></div>蜀为陇之根本，陇为蜀之股肱，秦为天下枢机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236965_comment'></div>故得陇而秦蜀大宁矣，不得陇则秦蜀无能为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236965_comment'></div>秦陇皆得，而梁宋在吾指掌之间，并地可绝河而收也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236965_comment'></div>论攻战者，千条万绪，进退得失，可豫言者此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236965_comment'></div>朝廷据有江淮，设险守要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236965_comment'></div>僭伪在齐梁，而秦陇、两河皆为虏守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236965_comment'></div>西南之人，不能出大散之关；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236965_comment'></div>督府所治，正当我之咽喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236965_comment'></div>建瓴席卷，世岂乏人也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236965_comment'></div>前日张公尝为此举矣，恃卓然之忠义，不料敌势之方炽，不察吾帅乘之未和，以新辑剉伤之馀，未暇少加练养，而与百胜无前之虏决死原野，此志士所为太息也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236965_comment'></div>愚顷者尝以书见张公，论兵不可必用，公易而不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236965_comment'></div>阁下之此行，比之张公，时易势殊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236965_comment'></div>邓禹归而冯异擅赤眉之捷，裴度行而李愬得李祐之降，阁下之功名，高于张公十倍可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236965_comment'></div>昔韩信佐高祖，乘章邯之结怨于民，故还定三秦，势如破竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236965_comment'></div>蜀人攻魏，以孔明之贤而不能得其志，值司马仲达之强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236965_comment'></div>成败可以鉴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236965_comment'></div>料敌制胜者，虽有娄、旷之聪明，终必凭于间探之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236965_comment'></div>虏暴骨以逞祸中国十馀年矣，重兵散归国内，再调发而无辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236965_comment'></div>子女玉帛，餍足充牣，再来而吾无可有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236965_comment'></div>彼所谓谋臣猛将，为陕右膏肓者，已天诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236965_comment'></div>故攻蜀则不能入而退，据襄则狼狈遁走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236965_comment'></div>是我师亦稍强于曩时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236965_comment'></div>虏之兵将既非前日之盛，此似有可乘之隙，敌似可料矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236965_comment'></div>然吾间探未精，殆见其皮毛之事，安知其无它谋臣，不能更遣重兵乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236965_comment'></div>故秦陇之事，在精其间探也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236965_comment'></div>古之用兵，惟间探为急务，且如一举而取伪齐，定京雒，唾手可办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236965_comment'></div>信如成功之后，而与我为敌者尚在北境，用兵亦未弭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236965_comment'></div>譬如搏虻去虱，何损于牛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236965_comment'></div>昔孙权尝谓曹孟德曰：「足下不死，孤不得安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236965_comment'></div>今吾朝廷，若非虏酋之死灭，亦不可谓安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236965_comment'></div>兵法曰：「知彼知己，百战百胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236965_comment'></div>不知己不知彼，百战百败」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236965_comment'></div>见几而作，攻守予夺之画，则阁下主其诺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236965_comment'></div>愚闻之师曰：「进取不如自守」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236965_comment'></div>知自守之至，乃进取而无后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236965_comment'></div>故羊祜、杜预之贤，巧于平吴而拙于谋晋，自守之术蔑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236965_comment'></div>谢安、桓温锐意并吞，所获不如所丧，所以无害者，知自守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236965_comment'></div>愿阁下威德加于雍、雒，畔将溃卒必相率以归服王化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236965_comment'></div>而自守万全之计，常使内重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236965_comment'></div>敌不能窥，国家永宁，兵革不频，至尊安枕而无忧，所以成方、召之业者，亦伟然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236965_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236965_comment'></div>中原要地，终必克复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236965_comment'></div>阁下犄之，阁下角之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236965_comment'></div>江南诸将，并力踣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236965_comment'></div>以蜀之饶，蓄谋养威，裕民劝农，下贤容众，先收陕右五路之师，与六军期会于韩魏之郊，将符尊专，号令齐肃，戮力一心，以酬特达之知，千载之一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236965_comment'></div>今六纛数日启行，用人之际，下走以潦倒贫困百僚之下，效匍匐于邯郸，受揶揄于燕蓟，其迂钝可笑，亦甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1236965_comment'></div>辄不自掩其缺短之见，卜媸妍于帐下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1236965_comment'></div>伏惟揖怒蛙、赦吐茵，钧播之广，宜无遐遗，吹嘘之荣，岂拒枯朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1236965_comment'></div>非所敢冒也，庶几不碌碌而负门下云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1236965_comment'></div>冒昧唐突，伏俟诛谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1236965_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1236965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1135')">1134-1135年</a>　在临安。有诗。作品：《甲寅岁雪一首》《牋胡枢密启》<div id='poem_139812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲寅岁雪一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139812")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_139812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139812'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139812'>冬燠阳淫遇上春，飞霙爽彻浩无垠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139812'>凌霄据壤平洼凸，破块抽萌蚀腐陈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139812'>皎洁肌容宜夜觌，培堆靀松<span class='inlineComment2'>（粤雅堂本作雺）</span>诘朝新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139812'>匀匀帝泽烝民粒，止止人寰世界尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139812'>野渡舟沈堆鹭羽，豪家堂下<span class='inlineComment2'>（粤雅堂本作室）</span>散瑶珉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139812'>袁生高卧诚清尚，慧可安心奈苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139812'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_139812_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺胡枢密</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236988")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236988'>窃以提纲而万目起，欲食者嘉鱼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236988_comment'></div>铸式而百体全，愿求者善马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236988_comment'></div>罩罩劳剧而始得，多多并蓄而后收，物理当然，人品犹是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236988_comment'></div>周南之叹未已，冀北之群岂空？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236988_comment'></div>使荣贱之势判然，则视听之知眇尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236988_comment'></div>盖扫除四海以为度，调一万汇以为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236988_comment'></div>圣贤所以驱驰，风俗从而趋竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236988_comment'></div>岩岩赫赫，高位固有常尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236988_comment'></div>勉勉遑遑，寒畯思有所试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236988_comment'></div>凡挟养材之柄，必禀知人之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236988_comment'></div>相期仁义之途，相引事功之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236988_comment'></div>附炎畏贵，则凡庸之所贪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236988_comment'></div>向道佑贤，乃豪杰之所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236988_comment'></div>开大公而广博，奋至鉴以昭融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236988_comment'></div>甲第朱门，何厌箴儆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236988_comment'></div>军符侯印，各祈代更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236988_comment'></div>刍荛肆言，屠钓寡合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236988_comment'></div>岂习熟卑隘之仕路，而鄙陋恬旷之山栖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236988_comment'></div>入吾选中，易于笼络；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236988_comment'></div>居吾术内，罔或遐遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236988_comment'></div>朝廷不可以空虚，天工殆急于分治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236988_comment'></div>拔十五而半获，得百一于已知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236988_comment'></div>勤礼挽推，甄藻题品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236988_comment'></div>天下喜乐，人皆往归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236988_comment'></div>宝储弥隆，缓急获用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236988_comment'></div>莛楹梁栱，合辑而成厦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236988_comment'></div>台莱栲杻，蔽覆而为山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236988_comment'></div>朝无旷官，士无失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236988_comment'></div>此自古类能之效，以人事君之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236988_comment'></div>不由兹途，亦复何觊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236988_comment'></div>忌之则往而不返，抑之则污而自羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236988_comment'></div>乐同肮脏于泥中，耻并伊优于堂上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236988_comment'></div>毁裂冠冕，欣属林丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236988_comment'></div>临事而叹乏才，治国者奚所赖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236988_comment'></div>藜藿不保，奸轨奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236988_comment'></div>籀尘埃糠秕，草野闻见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236988_comment'></div>夙有事道之慕，久怀量力之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236988_comment'></div>妄意古今，自待者敢不厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236988_comment'></div>缪耽义理，俗说者非所攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236988_comment'></div>居多长者之游，许予不凡之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236988_comment'></div>咀噍腐儒之执艺，酣咏素王之典彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236988_comment'></div>昼弹铗而悲吟，夜拊枕而太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236988_comment'></div>盖常处约，自守泊如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236988_comment'></div>分终为垄亩之民，无复视朝廷之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236988_comment'></div>谈王霸之馀策，意广心劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236988_comment'></div>遇管、萧之亚流，汗颜血指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236988_comment'></div>非有陆生之《新语》，又如奉春之便宜，何以少屈华簪，遽叨后乘！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236988_comment'></div>以嘉鱼善马之喻，或凡鳞病骨之容，上冒坯陶，仰攀槐棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236988_comment'></div>今明主劳精于复古，锐意于陟明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236988_comment'></div>殿幄演经，儒耋重席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236988_comment'></div>奖遇忠义，网罗放遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236988_comment'></div>论辨从容，举直措枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236988_comment'></div>除拟杂沓，念功计劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236988_comment'></div>昔晋元中兴，多擢中邦之世胄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236988_comment'></div>逮宋武北伐，亦赖江左之人英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236988_comment'></div>砥砺百官，系属三府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236988_comment'></div>枢密阁下登翼弼亮，斟酌裁成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1236988_comment'></div>积学高文，冠乎当代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1236988_comment'></div>潜计默识，准于古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1236988_comment'></div>戮力一心，革士风之媮薄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1236988_comment'></div>衔命万里，谕戎丑之服驯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1236988_comment'></div>绰然表饵之权，开示丹青之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1236988_comment'></div>贾生之学相埒，君叔之勋未优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1236988_comment'></div>介立孤标，智辨寡二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1236988_comment'></div>方且极夔、龙之洪业，体伊、葛之处心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1236988_comment'></div>三命益恭，百度咸理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1236988_comment'></div>至于好古而信，求善无餍，虽居功德之崇，略无高抗之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1236988_comment'></div>故籀近者忘其疏逖，饰其颛愚，拜揖奉承，神思消发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1236988_comment'></div>宜在摈而不省，孰谓高而难亲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1236988_comment'></div>徒步贵门，计拙百僚之下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1236988_comment'></div>抠衣末坐，蒙问五载之淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1236988_comment'></div>使其忘故园之思，不至剧寓公之窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1236988_comment'></div>微愿易满，小价即酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1236988_comment'></div>粗给烝尝，不恨枯槁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1236988_comment'></div>道前修而誉盛德，愈加令闻之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1236988_comment'></div>试家法以补明时，庶几先达之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1236988_comment'></div>非所望也，敢悉布之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1236988_comment'></div>亮惟垂矜，稍缓诛谴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1236988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月25日</a>　四月甲子，宋徽宗、宁德皇后郑氏卒于金，苏籀有挽词。作品：《挽词》《代慰国哀表》<div id='poem_1236940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代慰国哀表<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年4月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236940")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236940'>臣某言：伏睹今月二十五日圣旨，太上道君皇帝厌世升遐，宁德皇后上仙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236940_comment'></div>讣自龙荒，哀恫中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236940_comment'></div>奉讳之始，号慕攸同<span class='inlineComment2'>（中慰）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236940_comment'></div>恭惟太上道君皇帝二纪忧劳，万方亭育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236940_comment'></div>逊位贬号，谦抑逾涯，未返常岳之巡，遽陟鼎湖之驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236940_comment'></div>宁德皇后表正坤位，赞祐宸居，从翠华而远游，渡沙漠而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236940_comment'></div>群黎百姓，攀咽无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236940_comment'></div>皇帝陛下孝切羹墙，痛深屺岵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236940_comment'></div>伏惟降抑哀恸，俯全礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236940_comment'></div>臣无任瞻望陨越之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1236940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年5月</a>　五月乙巳，高宗生日，苏籀作文庆贺。作品：《祝圣寿表》<div id='poem_1236941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祝圣寿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236941")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236941'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236941'>兴王景贶，福生有基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236941_comment'></div>享国昌期，道乃能久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236941_comment'></div>里社鸣而纪节，嵩岳呼而发祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236941_comment'></div>浃绵宇之欢心，同一词而善颂<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236941_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下施由庚乎庶物，以无逸为元龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236941_comment'></div>三灵协祐以储休，九有来同于富寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236941_comment'></div>方将舞干羽而浑文轨，颁正朔而服要荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236941_comment'></div>寖明寖昌，袭无疆之历；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236941_comment'></div>时万时亿，降有永之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236941_comment'></div>臣阻扈和銮，依恋行阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236941_comment'></div>华封献颂，爝火太阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236941_comment'></div>小草何知，倾心委照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236941_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　七月，资政殿大学士知福州张守提举万寿观兼侍读，苏籀作贺启。作品：《贺张参政入觐经筵启》<div id='poem_1236990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张参政入觐经筵启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236990")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236990'>伏审竦传急诏，钦想趣装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236990_comment'></div>麟趾金华，异等殊渥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236990_comment'></div>紫枢黄閤，虚位以须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236990_comment'></div>中外乐闻，士夫交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236990_comment'></div>籀尝备官属，企慕光尘，忝荷帡幪，倍切欣喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236990_comment'></div>窃以明主好要，理世须贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236990_comment'></div>帷幄畴咨，春秋起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236990_comment'></div>招延旧德，开济远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236990_comment'></div>慎人物之评，求讨论之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236990_comment'></div>上意先定，佥言允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236990_comment'></div>盖贯悉古今，故能为万世之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236990_comment'></div>博约经术，乃厌服群士之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236990_comment'></div>其在当今，无逾执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236990_comment'></div>伏惟观使侍读大资柔嘉维则，信美且仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236990_comment'></div>莫际波澜，臻极壸奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236990_comment'></div>高文典册，挽回正始之音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236990_comment'></div>经武振兵，允有中兴之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236990_comment'></div>夙参大政，未究吁谟，愈练典刑，不择剧易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236990_comment'></div>凛然岳牧之首，蔚为议论之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236990_comment'></div>惟忧国饥渴之心，见给饷艰难之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236990_comment'></div>至尊叹萧何之杰，训词褒韩滉之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236990_comment'></div>辍保釐于藩维，俾左右于天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236990_comment'></div>赞襄于规随之际，斟酌乎献替之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236990_comment'></div>建功名于鼎彝，形歌颂于竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236990_comment'></div>再念籀罢秩三载，待次一官，大丧其家，托迹无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236990_comment'></div>熊落于槛，攀援奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236990_comment'></div>敢怀侥觊于超升，自安分限之凉薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236990_comment'></div>惟流落之未艾，迫屡空以难堪，仰止高明，未遂遐谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236990_comment'></div>使霖雨遍润于枯槁，丹青粗变于嫫妍，拯拔穷途，允归洪造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236990_comment'></div>殚竭顽质，少答深恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1236990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　有诗和韩驹。作品：《和卷中韩子苍梅花诗三首》<div id='poem_139693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和卷中韩子苍梅花三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139693")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139693'>先开媚晴昊，孤艳断魂时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139693'>绕树沈烟度，凌寒檀晕披。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139693'>参横明月观，雪细影娥池。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139693'>结实冥冥雨，君看雀啅枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139693'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139693_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139692?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139692'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139692'>冻蘖虽臞甚，含英山意催。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139692'>斲冰冲晓色，绽绿透春回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139692'>健步故人信，流芳好事杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139692'>不论山水僻，往往拾香来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139692'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139692_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139691?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139691'>国香倾国色，天质殆天怜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139691'>含笑冰崖侧，无言石濑溅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139691'>湘娥愁暮倚，孙令馥终筵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139691'>卜夜多松炬，玉容殊更妍<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：杜子美：巡檐索共梅花笑。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139691_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年6月10日</a>　友人韩昂修常山公庙，苏籀作记。作品：《常山县主簿题名记》<div id='poem_1237061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常山县主簿题名记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237061")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237061'>衢所隶五县，西曰常山，溪谷回阻，曩时号为岩险僻左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237061_comment'></div>比年圣上驻跸临安，冠盖旁午，甲兵往来，乃江、湖、闽、广水陆之冲，坌为孔道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237061_comment'></div>津驿廪库之吏与其舆台迓劳无虚日，事倍蓰于旁近他邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237061_comment'></div>然县令之次，有尉无簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237061_comment'></div>夫百里赋政，非有佐贰，何以办治？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237061_comment'></div>譬如羽翮修而鸿鹄举，宫商应而琴瑟调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237061_comment'></div>苟补左而缺右，有唱而弗和，殆不济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237061_comment'></div>簿之于令，联事而不逼，分劳而不专，上下咸以置之为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237061_comment'></div>绍兴四年二月庚申，资政殿大学士、宣奉大夫阳夏郡谢公任伯知军州事，言于朝，吾友韩君昴子平实被选辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237061_comment'></div>越三月某日，奉命视事，因旧废馆缮公廨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237061_comment'></div>君以谢公见用之意，不陋枳棘，不懈箴儆，所治者虽小，务知者大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237061_comment'></div>出入朱墨，钩校精覈，一毫必利于公上，一豆不落于人手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237061_comment'></div>于文无害，其长蒙成，众谓称其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237061_comment'></div>至于沿牒而稽经决狱，弦歌而乘间摄县，嚬呻纤悉，情伪洞晓，盖有补当今、见思异日者甚多焉，故当路数数荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237061_comment'></div>逮终更伊迩，书来告曰：「凡官舍皆刻石题名，创制兹职，肇自我先，子为记之，以贻后政之君子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237061_comment'></div>余窃以古人谨始必书，夫兴废当理则见称，图治宜民则可纪，可纪虽黄绶传不朽，不然，虽千驷无足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237061_comment'></div>矧贤牧伯之首建明，而吾友效官如此，不患湮沦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237061_comment'></div>姑妄书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237061_comment'></div>绍兴六年六月十日，眉山苏籀记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1237061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　朝廷省员，苏籀作书拟上赵鼎，论用士。作品：《拟上赵相书》<div id='poem_1236966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟上赵相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236966")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236966'>恭惟理世之要，澄源拯敝，纤悉举措，罔非大公至正而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236966_comment'></div>伏闻朝论，吏员猥众，缺次极少，率一官而五人共之，一人任职四人待次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236966_comment'></div>仕者无穷，而常员有限，填咽充塞，不可区处，有至十年而后之任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236966_comment'></div>本祈奖拔之多，而贤路迫隘至于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236966_comment'></div>近制，中都官待次者并罢斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236966_comment'></div>详味美意，戒于汎滥，务在精切，此举非不善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236966_comment'></div>前岁修废，除用诸丞，所添不过三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236966_comment'></div>今者概行朝兵府僚属，以次皆黜之，不下七八十人，其閒不容稍留矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236966_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236966_comment'></div>以人物为怀，以宗社为悦，毅然确然，自任休戚而后及此，灼见阁下之心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236966_comment'></div>《传》曰：「治本在得人，得人在审举，审举在核实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236966_comment'></div>古之用人，取之至宽，用之至狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236966_comment'></div>取之宽，故贤者不隔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236966_comment'></div>用之狭，故不肖者无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236966_comment'></div>夫披沙以求金，其始未弃沙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236966_comment'></div>舂糠以取米，其始兼取糠也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236966_comment'></div>终藉陶汰、簸扬之功耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236966_comment'></div>自今公举慎选，官曹之清必矣，士之黜者，谁不曰然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236966_comment'></div>或者以谓舍之则藏，今既舍矣，则宜远举遐引，奉祠宫，从农圃而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236966_comment'></div>其长者以为安义命，坚特操，读书立言，贵于行也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236966_comment'></div>修身正家，以治国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236966_comment'></div>自进之路尚广，长逝山林则过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236966_comment'></div>阁下统理中外，奖擢延引，覆载之内，跂行喙息，皆有赖于庇庥，而士大夫不蒙垂荫，理有不当然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236966_comment'></div>夫一意于退，自薄自弃者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236966_comment'></div>自奋自励者，岂钜其无取乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236966_comment'></div>彼七八十人中，其志意才略尚有人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236966_comment'></div>今夫天下之势，方且倒悬，神州陆沉，未能雪复，夷狄凭陵，腥秽寰宇，此正用才求贤之急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236966_comment'></div>夫负能挟策，自以绝出常流，则悯世忧时，亦谁能默坐而已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236966_comment'></div>亦不容逝去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236966_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236966_comment'></div>才之难也，吾君吾相岂终弃人也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236966_comment'></div>所黜七八十人者，岂将使失其职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236966_comment'></div>夫古之逐客，有复为尊官、成大功名者矣，三黜五去，复被礼遇者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236966_comment'></div>至于鄙夷厌贱，遏绝忽略，则识者不敢以此期阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236966_comment'></div>意者鉴裁称量，丹青造化已素定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236966_comment'></div>唐崔祐甫除吏八百，时无遗才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236966_comment'></div>裴垍荐士三十馀人，朝野翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236966_comment'></div>二子尚能然，是岂足以概论高明乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236966_comment'></div>士之无能、无求、无思、无欲，可以投闲散、群冗士者，莫如籀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236966_comment'></div>罢斥数中，不在有无多少之间，恃阁下之在上，犹复一鸣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236966_comment'></div>亦尝承风旨，辱轸念，自惟身贱迹疏，而有再三之渎，惶悚无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236966_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236966_comment'></div>自待固不忍薄，待阁下亦敢不厚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236966_comment'></div>今天下所谓魁垒豪杰，功业隆重，阁下当轴，实无忝焉，与天下之士共建皇极，固优为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236966_comment'></div>自惟非刘禹锡之才誉而求牛僧孺之知，乏杜牧之谋猷而觊李德裕之用，亦已难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236966_comment'></div>倘尚宽其愚，训其拙，未忘掇拾之意，实以有道贫贱为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236966_comment'></div>若夫流落无归，至于累年，私事也，非敢辄言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236966_comment'></div>经术道义，学于前哲，公论也，其或小用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236966_comment'></div>结发读书，白首不辍，亦尝侧闻长者之风，而窃窥梦奠老人之意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236966_comment'></div>庶几用其道，并其人试之以伎，效之以官，飞一檄，驰一传，裨补尘露，书生之事也，敢不勉焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236966_comment'></div>「吉甫作颂，穆如清风」，平生所慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236966_comment'></div>恭惟今春虏犯淮泗，阁下实为首相，捍患御灾之际，举无遗策，虏以败北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236966_comment'></div>诚愿纪述盛德大业，被之金石，以追配古中兴之佐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236966_comment'></div>狂斐干冒，俯伏俟罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236966_comment'></div>不宣<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236966_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1236966'>「非敢」至「小用」：原错简在前，据右引移补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1236966_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　苏籀以谢克家荐得改秩，作谢表。作品：《改秩牋谢资政》<div id='poem_1236987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>改秩笺谢资政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236987")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236987'>伏念在浚城之旟，进迁命秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236987_comment'></div>上泉山之牍，佩戴揄扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236987_comment'></div>就日望云，入朝法座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236987_comment'></div>跼天蹐地，被奉恩纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236987_comment'></div>高蹈龙津，追回鹢路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236987_comment'></div>知人必当，听众咸孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236987_comment'></div>寡乏何人，祗慄优论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236987_comment'></div>窃以铨管千条之密，钩考五仕之严，抑欺滥与侥浮，慎裁量而澄汰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236987_comment'></div>怵迫之徒，使其安分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236987_comment'></div>规矩之士，岂不稍伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236987_comment'></div>公论夷涂，真贤实绩，假令冒昧，反玷高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236987_comment'></div>如籀者倨僻迂疏，孤羁癯悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236987_comment'></div>承学以诗书为业，捍格未精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236987_comment'></div>吏道以法令为师，黾勉无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236987_comment'></div>二十五年于随牒，十生九死于乱邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236987_comment'></div>陇月河冰，旧游最壮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236987_comment'></div>蛮陬夷落，屏却未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236987_comment'></div>思所以奖王室之图，庶几不忝天下之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236987_comment'></div>祈临机而趋事，顾縻爵而敢辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236987_comment'></div>非抟扶摇，则耕衍沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236987_comment'></div>此盖伏遇侍读大资丈渊源冲邃，器识穹宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236987_comment'></div>洽览羲皇以来，若烛照而数计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236987_comment'></div>尊临岳牧之首，如凤举而鹏鶱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236987_comment'></div>妩媚上前，神用卓绝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236987_comment'></div>雄飞朝右，风旨英华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236987_comment'></div>燮精祲之至和，消戎丑之奸悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236987_comment'></div>亹亹过庭之诱，拳拳跪履之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236987_comment'></div>不倦题评，见顾岂无其本末？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236987_comment'></div>未谐补益，狂狷政赖于甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236987_comment'></div>虚徐进寸之阶，昂耸直寻之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236987_comment'></div>尘埃冠剑，吹拂有待于牛公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236987_comment'></div>嚣噪声歌，减放必资于杨子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236987_comment'></div>幸阿陵之广纳，使品汇之备成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236987_comment'></div>厚义所存，小礼奚用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236987_comment'></div>汗流湜、籍之后，气苏管、乐之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236987_comment'></div>器使不遗，愿究上臣格天之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236987_comment'></div>区别素定，亦使小草因地而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236987_comment'></div>恭惟负鼎之心，实轸纳沟之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236987_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1236987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年12月</a>　十二月辛亥，张守自常州入见，即日除参知政事，苏籀作贺启。作品：《贺张参政启》<div id='poem_1236991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236991")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236991'>伏审上眷旧劳，复还大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236991_comment'></div>命传疾置，罔不佥谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236991_comment'></div>道路欣拜于锋车，搢绅腾咏于纶綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236991_comment'></div>事系国体，喜溢民情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236991_comment'></div>前古建极之君，至精考慎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236991_comment'></div>其相风云感会，霖雨敷施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236991_comment'></div>虽天纵日新之姿，亦人谋弼谐之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236991_comment'></div>恭惟治本，要在得人，核实循名，较修量短，验于已试，柬其真才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236991_comment'></div>莫如孟子之恭王，必曰仁义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236991_comment'></div>亟召穆之而翊亮，同济艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236991_comment'></div>迫促诏音，参陪道论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236991_comment'></div>凡密勿邦家之务，待畴咨国老而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236991_comment'></div>相时会通，若惊受宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236991_comment'></div>伏惟参政相公金玉王度，蓍龟帝谟，望峻乌台，词高鳌禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236991_comment'></div>梗议无隐，砭世之盲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236991_comment'></div>清节无华，干国之蛊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236991_comment'></div>若安世而簪笔持橐，如次公而增秩赐金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236991_comment'></div>以万姓劳苦为忧，以四海焦枯自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236991_comment'></div>著书传道，趋圣域而优长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236991_comment'></div>重席谈经，发睿学之高妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236991_comment'></div>文士宗其题品，武臣赖于抚循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236991_comment'></div>寡悔与尤，当世谁比？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236991_comment'></div>或出暨处，底绩见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236991_comment'></div>数移百六之秋，运际升平之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236991_comment'></div>督励耕战，宽恤闾阎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236991_comment'></div>顿振纲维，善厚风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236991_comment'></div>拯遗黎而迓箪食，宾左衽而系长缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236991_comment'></div>允副渊衷之怀，果慰天下之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236991_comment'></div>霸姜微管，似此得君而成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236991_comment'></div>翊舜命皋，岂曰安民之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236991_comment'></div>籀夙事芙蓉之府，乐逢桃李之蹊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236991_comment'></div>被捃拾躏藉之馀，犯而岂校；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236991_comment'></div>傥湔洗照临之末，公生至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236991_comment'></div>窃惟屏退之踪，岂忘致恭之礼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236991_comment'></div>矜恤孤拙，祗恃仁恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236991_comment'></div>钦想于衷，敷述奚既！</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1236991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　范正国由比部为广东转运使，苏籀作诗送之。作品：《送范比部持节广东》<div id='poem_139867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送范比部持节广东</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139867")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139867'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139867'>羊城使者神仙中，苒苒叱驭凌云踪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139867'>绣袂吾徒强掺执，解手一举南飞鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139867'>君侯烜赫标肉谱，文正烈祖忠宣父。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139867'>典刑付托呼所钟，经国风规俨如故。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139867'>伤时嗟我思古人，遗直茂勋君<span class='inlineComment2'>（粤雅堂本作名）</span>世嗣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139867'>春秋主盟由范氏，不战屈人从范智。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139867'>备尝世故无难易，出入淹回俱掌计。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139867'>世推汲偃似长孺，共怀下惠贤展喜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139867'>鸟言夷面吾氓耳，岂弟公清渠自理。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139867'>声华本实警蛮貊，锋颖天然加峭利。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139867'>转粮遵海爰究度，并按三河应不避。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139867'>追车少日便还朝，首出儒林冠循吏。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139867'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_139867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　代范正国上谢表。作品：《代广东漕谢表》<div id='poem_1236927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代广东漕谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236927")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236927'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236927'>乘轺江右，深愧空餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236927_comment'></div>改辕峤南，再蒙宠寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236927_comment'></div>咨诹原隰，焜耀岭泷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236927_comment'></div>均王泽于敷天，冒海隅之出日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236927_comment'></div>澄清任责，欣慨交并<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236927_comment'></div>伏念臣少学洙泗之滨，缪习六艺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236927_comment'></div>老昧然、桑之妙，岂悟《九章》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236927_comment'></div>黾勉金谷之间，汩没簿书之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236927_comment'></div>循良尚冀于前躅，空疏误玷于显曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236927_comment'></div>倚伏相乘，颠沛失据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236927_comment'></div>吊影舐犊之戚，消冰晞骥之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236927_comment'></div>不欲抗颜于形势之途，乃其私愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236927_comment'></div>荐令悉力于均调之任，休有荣光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236927_comment'></div>仰天造之曲成，顾人微而靡称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236927_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下至仁化育，神智裁成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236927_comment'></div>耀德振兵，柔远能迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236927_comment'></div>讲修旧贯，初解瑟更张之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236927_comment'></div>允迪中兴，有思马斯臧之富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236927_comment'></div>察臣恳悃，素守不移；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236927_comment'></div>怜臣践扬，老当益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236927_comment'></div>收东隅而已晚，付南纪则过优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236927_comment'></div>思终始以酬恩，今绥柔于遐裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236927_comment'></div>殚竭计虑，理财正辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236927_comment'></div>抚循民夷，裕人约己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236927_comment'></div>敦崇礼义，抑绝暴贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236927_comment'></div>爱惜禹阴，尽瘁公家之利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236927_comment'></div>倾就尧日，无惭畿甸之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236927_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1236927_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月</a>　正月癸未，陈与义自翰林学士除参知政事，苏籀作贺启。作品：《贺陈参政启》<div id='poem_1236992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺陈参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236992")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236992'>伏审光奉宸章，进陪国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236992_comment'></div>诞告遐迩，欢欣交通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236992_comment'></div>伏惟庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236992_comment'></div>窃以内修外攘之艰，大劳小康之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236992_comment'></div>惟道德才谞之醇固，所以拯患而致祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236992_comment'></div>惟将相士民之协和，所以同心而造事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236992_comment'></div>忘于斯者，或昧其术；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236992_comment'></div>谋于斯者，或挠其权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236992_comment'></div>大政之几，非贤不乂，必也抱魁垒之质，挟清警之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236992_comment'></div>故侍凝旒，则听纳被知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236992_comment'></div>逮居黄閤，则寅恭竭尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236992_comment'></div>算多而胜，业广惟勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236992_comment'></div>中国倒悬，告猷能解；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236992_comment'></div>生灵沦陷，援手释忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236992_comment'></div>如通闭破结，发越人之药石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236992_comment'></div>若引重致远，辑造父之辔衔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236992_comment'></div>在措置之锱铢，系安危之輗軏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236992_comment'></div>故廊庙虚位，妙柬清忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236992_comment'></div>搢绅公言，莫如执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236992_comment'></div>伏惟参政资禀绝异，规略最优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236992_comment'></div>沈涵仁义之渊，点𪑮诗书之囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236992_comment'></div>典司八玺，宿学儒宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236992_comment'></div>劝讲六经，每舒皇眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236992_comment'></div>夙夜匪懈，密勿赞佑之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236992_comment'></div>讽谏从容，启沃多闻之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236992_comment'></div>韩厥为人之不党，子产临事则慎辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236992_comment'></div>国蓍蔡而世表仪，帝股肱而天笔舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236992_comment'></div>报坚昆而谕渤海，檄巴蜀而射聊城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236992_comment'></div>倚马操觚，袪迷决瞆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236992_comment'></div>尺一有中和之气，方隅识睿圣之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236992_comment'></div>布繁悉化俗之言，播委曲难谕之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236992_comment'></div>陪銮扈跸，造膝虚襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236992_comment'></div>酌古今而处便宜，预图画而补遗阙，允执大柄，光辅明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236992_comment'></div>殆将致主于唐虞，自信许身之稷契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236992_comment'></div>引类而真贤举，励精而治功成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236992_comment'></div>沛其源流，素所蓄积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236992_comment'></div>籀夙叨奖饰，几免牢愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236992_comment'></div>纶綍颁行，喜而不寐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236992_comment'></div>光尘眇末，仰之弥高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236992_comment'></div>绵宇蒙庥，伟哉造物！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236992_comment'></div>馀波所泽，尽出生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236992_comment'></div>素悯枵疏，岂遗贱远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236992_comment'></div>颂咏之切，敷染奚殚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1236992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月</a>　九月丙子，赵鼎复除左仆射兼枢密使，苏籀作贺启。作品：《贺赵相公启》《贺赵丞相再入相启》<div id='poem_1236989' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236989' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236989?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赵相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236989")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236989_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236989'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236989'>伏审宸廷敷号，铉府策勋，首冠冢司，眷隆台辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236989_comment'></div>群公禀承于处决，含生鼓舞于设施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236989_comment'></div>朝廷愈尊，国势增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236989_comment'></div>凡居大芘，何啻小康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236989_comment'></div>窃以国之隆兴，必有命世之佐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236989_comment'></div>士之光显，盖逢知己之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236989_comment'></div>磊落殊常之姿，得于考慎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236989_comment'></div>特达难酬之遇，猗于经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236989_comment'></div>帷幄畴咨，廷臣莫比；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236989_comment'></div>爪牙宣力，庙略居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236989_comment'></div>逮戎丑之攸宁，嘉指踪之成效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236989_comment'></div>眷隆极品之赏，宠褒特异之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236989_comment'></div>恭惟某官兼文武之资，好帝王之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236989_comment'></div>扩持纲之大度，守补衮之小心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236989_comment'></div>白简霜威，尝落奸邪之胆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236989_comment'></div>追车日下，再掌宥密之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236989_comment'></div>副叶虚怀，从容爰立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236989_comment'></div>霖雨未敷于三日，羽檄沓至于百函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236989_comment'></div>制胜安边，恨用休璟之晚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236989_comment'></div>御军却敌，悉皆德裕之裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236989_comment'></div>威令严明，将士奋励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236989_comment'></div>遂使僭盗之类，落吾术数之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236989_comment'></div>解腥秽为乐郊，决赘疣于俄顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236989_comment'></div>方且扶持正论，削庶事之厉阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236989_comment'></div>抚辑黎元，为百年之长虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236989_comment'></div>熟讲全策，以防盛秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236989_comment'></div>富民振兵，寔举措之优裕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236989_comment'></div>治内服外，谅条画之无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236989_comment'></div>以我自守之馀，图厥进取之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236989_comment'></div>符移汴雒，知猘子之不足擒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236989_comment'></div>表饵龙荒，见黠虏之将屈伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236989_comment'></div>允塞中兴之责，捷疾亨泰之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236989_comment'></div>籀仰止门阑，尝辱顾盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236989_comment'></div>恭惟格天之辅，譬如涉海之舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236989_comment'></div>不容一木之或亏，岂有一夫之不获？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236989_comment'></div>尚祈草芥，亦与甄陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236989_comment'></div>钦闻休命之飏，倍切舆情之喜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1236989_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赵丞相再入相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236993")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236993'>伏审被召镇东，来归揆路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236993_comment'></div>注清衷而爰立，采黎庶之公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236993_comment'></div>柬贤允念于前劳，用旧莫先于元老，诞飏孚号，胥庆舆情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236993_comment'></div>窃以协一德而冠群公，维四方而调品汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236993_comment'></div>夙契风云之会，才遏干戈之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236993_comment'></div>道远心勤，务繁日浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236993_comment'></div>效著明于详试，绩靡究于成能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236993_comment'></div>欲尽其施设之方，必假以岁月之久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236993_comment'></div>遽辍调羹之手，岂伸负俎之心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236993_comment'></div>条得失之将然，灼筹画之可倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236993_comment'></div>增庙堂之严邃，还魁柄以弥纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236993_comment'></div>任责丕平，允酬殊遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236993_comment'></div>恭惟仆射相公举尹、望之术，助尧、舜之明，恢恢乎肯綮之间，炳炳乎付授之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236993_comment'></div>燮理精祲，察玉衡之端；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236993_comment'></div>绥靖邦家，无金瓯之缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236993_comment'></div>边实将勇，当朝辟国之召公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236993_comment'></div>民肃吏循，斯晨化俗之杨绾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236993_comment'></div>惟用意之高远，故图画而必成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236993_comment'></div>解中原之倒悬，配前修之奇士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236993_comment'></div>籀自惟疏冗，尝误生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236993_comment'></div>一毫何补于门阑，即日中伤于唇吻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236993_comment'></div>孰谓根茎之弱，亦湔霖雨之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236993_comment'></div>倘一观东閤之英，将稍释衡门之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236993_comment'></div>日者驱策之意，时哉幸会之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236993_comment'></div>竦忭之诚，敷写奚既！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1236993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月</a>　常同除御史中丞，苏籀作贺启。作品：《贺常中丞启》<div id='poem_1236994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺常中丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236994")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236994'>伏审弄印宸严，首膺属任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236994_comment'></div>专席朝右，祗竦观瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236994_comment'></div>胪传邸音，义当赞喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236994_comment'></div>伏惟某官闻见远大，体履醇深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236994_comment'></div>谈王霸施为，究古今要术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236994_comment'></div>寤皇明之思治，奋直谅以输忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236994_comment'></div>隆礼义为堤防，革蠹敝由原本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236994_comment'></div>宽黔黎于疲瘵，葺典章之阙遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236994_comment'></div>沐雨栉风，不愆讲艺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236994_comment'></div>握发吐哺，唯在用贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236994_comment'></div>天地之间，气浩然而不挠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236994_comment'></div>雷霆之下，身独当而弗辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236994_comment'></div>敷文卓诡而契上心，建议精明而定国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236994_comment'></div>赤墀言动，䌷绎倚相之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236994_comment'></div>右掖训词，润色郑侨之博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236994_comment'></div>一麾出守，三节亟还，受釐延问于贾生，扬觯难忘于杜举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236994_comment'></div>初贰秩宗之绵蕝，遂执风宪而纠绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236994_comment'></div>悉协朝佥，岂谷子敢荐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236994_comment'></div>卓然天奖，如裴度召来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236994_comment'></div>方今形势抢攘，夷虏变诈，所贵先胜之计，姑为灭贼之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236994_comment'></div>俟虏衅端，恃有德而获天助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236994_comment'></div>制敌衰毙，虽不战而屈人兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236994_comment'></div>殆将督励惰媮，赞宵旰之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236994_comment'></div>分别忠佞，为月旦之评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236994_comment'></div>切当世大机，绍前修坠绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236994_comment'></div>无我而副公望，许国而弗隐情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236994_comment'></div>人曰康哉，邦其庶矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236994_comment'></div>籀分甘山薮，望绝鼎彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236994_comment'></div>逮夫休命之扬，岂胜不寐之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236994_comment'></div>伫仁贤之燮理，举明主乎升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236994_comment'></div>正始返于风规，知旧与其膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236994_comment'></div>欣颂之至，敷染奚殚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1236994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　在临安。有文。作品：《杂著》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《杂著》共八篇，分别是《媮风》、《民情》、《进取》、《论将》、《刑礼》、《碱裁》、《任将》、《知人》。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年12月</a>　祔徽宗皇帝、显肃皇后灵位于太庙，苏籀表、疏。作品：《徽宗祔庙慰表》《徽宗帝、宁德皇后上仙荐疏》<div id='poem_1236942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗祔庙慰表<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十二年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236942")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236942'>宾仙跸于云天，廓然遐陟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236942_comment'></div>从祖祢于庙室，永言孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236942_comment'></div>凡属臣民，共增摧咽<span class='inlineComment2'>（中慰）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236942_comment'></div>窃以饰终之容典惟备，追远之想望何胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236942_comment'></div>叙宗祧昭穆之彝伦，为礿祠烝尝而作主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236942_comment'></div>所以达睿诚欲报之德，系邦国哀恫之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236942_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下爱钦尽于笃亲，苾芬昭于孝祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236942_comment'></div>致终天罔极之慕，安皇灵如在之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236942_comment'></div>存手泽以感音容，每斋戒而思居处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236942_comment'></div>风木不静，霜庭恻然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236942_comment'></div>愿抑至情，以幸天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236942_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1236942_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗皇帝宁德皇后上仙荐疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237073")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237073'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237073'>伏以日月告凶，天地震裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237073_comment'></div>攀龙罔逮，御骏已遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237073_comment'></div>凡在照临，岂胜摧慕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237073_comment'></div>伏惟太上道君皇帝忧劳二纪，化育万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237073_comment'></div>逮北狩之不还，剧函生之延企。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237073_comment'></div>伏惟宁德皇后坤元柔顺，屯难邅回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237073_comment'></div>法宫未返于椒兰，赠襚遽陈于袆狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237073_comment'></div>爰假大雄之妙力，以资仙驭之神游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237073_comment'></div>伏愿威灵在天，并生兜率；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237073_comment'></div>福祚垂世，宁壹寰瀛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237073_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1237073_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='206f5fe718ee474288104bacc63d1e47_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("206f5fe718ee474288104bacc63d1e47");'><span id='206f5fe718ee474288104bacc63d1e47_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1144')">1141-1144年</a>，51-54岁</div><div id='206f5fe718ee474288104bacc63d1e47' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　苏籀入朝面对论和战。作品：《面对论和战札子》<div id='poem_1236953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>面对论和战劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236953")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236953'>臣闻禹抑洪水，拔万世之患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236953_comment'></div>高宗伐鬼方，三年克之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236953_comment'></div>圣王巍乎建事策勋，盖天辟隆平之路，治人事天，命世膺期，不得不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236953_comment'></div>逮夫中古豪杰之主，唐文皇之讨颉利，汉高帝之赂冒顿，措置惬当，罔非伟绩，亦各斟酌时宜，庙算多得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236953_comment'></div>然严尤谓之无策，未为通论，乃是不知时势而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236953_comment'></div>窃惟陛下日昃焦劳，江、淮、梁、益累年小康，而中原尚梗强虏，坚敌侵掠，凭陵日来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236953_comment'></div>事势诚有间矣，而未集也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236953_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236953_comment'></div>洪水尚可治，鬼方、颉利、冒顿之伦，有为者岂难制哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236953_comment'></div>陛下睿明，今之禹、高宗也，成功何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236953_comment'></div>夫和愈于战，天下虽平，忘战则危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236953_comment'></div>圣德英猷，何特汉唐可比？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236953_comment'></div>其当战也，揆江山夷险之势，持重示弱，养威待衅，然后趋三捷之利，保万全而奋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236953_comment'></div>暂劳永逸，贵谋贱战，以节制辑睦之众，据险乘便，决机取胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236953_comment'></div>近日川陕、顺昌、柘皋殄歼丑类，如举鸿毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236953_comment'></div>夫或驱捕膻秽，或致币穹庐，陛下卜之于天命，参之以人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236953_comment'></div>天诱戎酋之衷，知难而退，翕然更始，厌处中原，思归巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236953_comment'></div>陛下此际熟复长虑，合天下之耳目而察之，岂无最远之见闻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236953_comment'></div>历古今之成败而推之，岂无最长之方略？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236953_comment'></div>时攻而攻，时赂而赂，文皇之雪耻非难，高帝之大度何怯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236953_comment'></div>不废两涂，随事而慎用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236953_comment'></div>战而非穷武拿祸，豺狼之群骇而远遁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236953_comment'></div>赂而非偷安目前，毡毳之性蔼然驯服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236953_comment'></div>深念夫兴王要略，岂不曰修政令、肃纪纲、理财用、洽恩信、精士卒、练将帅、饬守御七者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236953_comment'></div>益加宸心，日新厥猷，励精勤勉，虏必望风夺气，凶悖之心不生，一意慕华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236953_comment'></div>朝廷声实，有以待之，若不获已，以战则克，岂黩于兵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236953_comment'></div>彼既驯矣，以赂则服，奚狃于和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236953_comment'></div>《大雅》称太王待混夷曰：「肆不殄厥愠，亦不陨厥问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236953_comment'></div>混夷駾矣，维其喙矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236953_comment'></div>言虏困剧而卒服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236953_comment'></div>臣窃谓深仁孝悌之感格，英灵神武之变化，长乐必归，侵地即复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236953_comment'></div>道胜德立，息兵措刑，何求而不得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236953_comment'></div>何向而不济耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236953_comment'></div>臣贱远愚陋，不识时机，今日钜论大议，实非敢与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236953_comment'></div>区区事君之义，冒死越职而言之，钦惟睿明裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236953_comment'></div>取进止<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236953_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1236953'>格：原无，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1236953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　在朝。有论事札子。作品：《时务札子》<div id='poem_1236955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>时务劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236955")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236955'>恭惟虑休戚之大，究时用之宜，情有所不堪，功有所难成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236955_comment'></div>不曰如之何，殆将无以为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236955_comment'></div>今夫崇圣道，稽经旨，固已立治本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236955_comment'></div>意者文昭而武未允，志广而谋未竭，天下之公患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236955_comment'></div>考之往牒，惟借汉可以为谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236955_comment'></div>高祖起布衣，器度远大，非若诸生规规诵诗书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236955_comment'></div>又萧、张佐之，济其不逮，履至危，拔至艰，莫不曲当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236955_comment'></div>故先得秦鹿，如约当王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236955_comment'></div>项羽号百万众，盛怒将攻之，当时众寡相绝，诟忿亦人所不堪，子房导之，谢咎自解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236955_comment'></div>酂侯谏以汤武诎伸，乃为顽冒椎钝，忘小恚而得大勇，羽莫能测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236955_comment'></div>及其筑坛以拜淮阴，乃定东向之计，并率五侯之锐以讨羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236955_comment'></div>怀王，君也，羽又弑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236955_comment'></div>然汉义师尝不得志，屡居项氏掌握之中，每以智算折而不屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236955_comment'></div>王陵领兵迓太公，而楚拒绝之，汉复失军于睢水，羽遂止太公、吕后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236955_comment'></div>高祖自此裁一遇楚，小捷京索，即坚垒深堑，不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236955_comment'></div>成皋、脩武之间，惟务逃楚，以亲在其军故然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236955_comment'></div>君父之雠，但分遣淮阴等数将焚储夺地，高祖未尝躬与羽角，意有在也，所以贵智而鄙力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236955_comment'></div>随何片言而下九江，曲逆万镒以间亚父，厥后四方归汉，人心翕若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236955_comment'></div>羽虽剽悍，失援寡助，韩、彭力攻之，遂有鸿沟之割，侯生缓颊，而太公等果归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236955_comment'></div>时谓高祖天授，非人谋，殆不然焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236955_comment'></div>《书》曰：「必有忍，其乃有济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236955_comment'></div>隐忍之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236955_comment'></div>方西伯居羑里七年，闳夭以宝货奇物献纣而后得释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236955_comment'></div>故《诗》称周之克商、成王业曰：「夙夜基命宥密，于缉熙，殚厥心，肆其靖之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236955_comment'></div>文王之答天命，未尝求之，未尝舍之，能忍宥也，能谋密也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236955_comment'></div>及其和洽而光明，尽其心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236955_comment'></div>三代圣王所以肇基王迹，必养锐畏天，以渐制敌人，故集大勋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236955_comment'></div>汉垓下成擒，太公亟归，君父之雠遂雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236955_comment'></div>汉之筹画当矣，暗合于《诗》《书》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236955_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236955_comment'></div>朝廷行大道，隆名教，汉祖所不及，至于隐忍而知天命，卑逊而终不屈，比方三王与汉祖，皆一致耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236955_comment'></div>然今日所欲，未悉谐允如先王者，诚文教有馀，师律未甚竞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236955_comment'></div>使授钺非韩、彭，则虏无所忌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236955_comment'></div>衔命非陈、郦、侯、随，则请求何获？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236955_comment'></div>要当精擢将臣，慎行人之选，不爱金币以结五利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236955_comment'></div>庙堂计虑弥纶，坐以待旦，萧、张功名垂成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236955_comment'></div>若夫留意柬求天下廉耻必胜之将，则黠虏破胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236955_comment'></div>今世知兵者，岂无遗才乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236955_comment'></div>昨者戎心稍驯，贪我赐予，不恃战争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236955_comment'></div>战之赂之，相时而动，不可偏徇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236955_comment'></div>此汉高取太公之策，闳夭出文王之术也，执事者宜熟思之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1236955_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　朝廷拟授苏籀典校秘阁之职，未果授。作品：《拟答馆职谢启》<div id='poem_1236998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟答馆职谢启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236998")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236998'>伏审待对北门，敷陈切务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236998_comment'></div>进直东观，典校秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236998_comment'></div>公言所推，佥听胥穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236998_comment'></div>窃惟隆儒大本，精选抡乐育之途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236998_comment'></div>待士最高，号刊述是正之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236998_comment'></div>广经籍而考阅，得英俊之朋游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236998_comment'></div>皇王之学，并列其间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236998_comment'></div>公辅之储，多从此出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236998_comment'></div>某官升华贤路，擢秀艺林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236998_comment'></div>研精黄卷之言，宜感青藜之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236998_comment'></div>过形简管，深认撝谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236998_comment'></div>获披芬绚之章，欲致酸痟之愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236998_comment'></div>珍藏为幸，玩味何穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236998_comment'></div>裁谢之私，叙言罔既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236998_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1236998_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　苏籀因秦桧提携，转官朝奉郎。作品：《谢转朝奉郎笺》<div id='poem_1236999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转朝奉郎笺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236999")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236999'>右，籀启：准诰转前件官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236999_comment'></div>资品纤微，惠泽沾被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236999_comment'></div>揆劳何取，加秩过优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236999_comment'></div>朝渥难胜，衷情悚慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236999_comment'></div>近者缉熙盛典，光显丕称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236999_comment'></div>备吉蠲之情文，起琢磨之工伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236999_comment'></div>恭惟徽宗皇帝诒谋施于罔极，广声振乎无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236999_comment'></div>如日照临，在帝左右，苍黔所以固结，精祲所以燮和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236999_comment'></div>善继祗承，威灵于赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236999_comment'></div>以为节以壹惠，岂足以飏巨美而阐英猷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236999_comment'></div>加于众名，则可以纪闳图而昭盛绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236999_comment'></div>盖槐府玉堂，妙形容而评拟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236999_comment'></div>鸾台凤阁，俱会议而钦崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236999_comment'></div>颂述《云汉》之章，象牒金椟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236999_comment'></div>昭格神祇之护，宝玺玉函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236999_comment'></div>发册彤庭，揭节命使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236999_comment'></div>于是圭币缛惟馨之荐，庙祐虔至腆之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236999_comment'></div>作民恭先，惟圣纯孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236999_comment'></div>幸尘位著，顾贱有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236999_comment'></div>遭逢至荣，岂期嘉赐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236999_comment'></div>聪察不遗于卑远，责成自有于度程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236999_comment'></div>命日量功，包荒济务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236999_comment'></div>至于熙事之辑，允赖公听之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236999_comment'></div>伏遇太师公相深喻诚明之原，挟持礼乐之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236999_comment'></div>不以三公而易其介，劝歌九叙而俾其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236999_comment'></div>前箸之筹，每先知而应猝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236999_comment'></div>造膝之语，不离道而稽经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236999_comment'></div>优如子产之择能，宽若巨源之多可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236999_comment'></div>励精柬擢，宏溥湛恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236999_comment'></div>品汇自然得其宜，百工安敢爱其力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236999_comment'></div>服冕放佞，乘辂舞《韶》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236999_comment'></div>封博望以柔鬼方，赏叔孙之趋时务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236999_comment'></div>补苴鏬漏，兴造废遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236999_comment'></div>致凤鸟而出《河图》，皆平生之素蕴；<div class='inline'
