id='poem_sentence_33_1236999_comment'></div>殄神奸而拔泗鼎，亦次第而垂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236999_comment'></div>籀滥叨锡予之阶，溢听升平之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236999_comment'></div>童髫耋杖，咸欣睹于降康；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236999_comment'></div>军政国容，顿复仍于旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236999_comment'></div>上眷固尤为卓越，勋略难掩其巍峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236999_comment'></div>念惟睎骥之踪，喻若为山之址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236999_comment'></div>苟听其注，务致思以竭才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236999_comment'></div>必得其官，荷提携而改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236999_comment'></div>无任依向感戢之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1236999_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月</a>　壬午，皇太后自金返，高宗亲迎，苏籀作贺表。作品：《贺东朝归表》<div id='poem_1236948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺东朝归表<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236948")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236948'>格天德至，本自宸扆而刑多方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236948_comment'></div>笃亲诚纯，不忘跬步而还万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236948_comment'></div>奉宝舆之言返，举连环而不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236948_comment'></div>溢绵宇之欢心，巍高世之驯行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236948_comment'></div>慈襟一喜，品汇咸苏<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236948_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下本曾、闵方寸之衷，体勋、华要广之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236948_comment'></div>励勤精力，吁祈请之艰难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236948_comment'></div>菲薄旰宵，慕温凊于遐邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236948_comment'></div>方且显鸿名而正统纪，曷尝忘侍膳而舍寝门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236948_comment'></div>未宣畅于郁堙，久湛详于宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236948_comment'></div>致极兢兢而业业，允谐泄泄与融融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236948_comment'></div>盖人事之无亏，俾天心之保定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236948_comment'></div>顺承颜志，万国悦而养东朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236948_comment'></div>溥博施恩，三表修而怀北顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236948_comment'></div>较劳考事，冠古超今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236948_comment'></div>如汉薄之代来，厥功绝易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236948_comment'></div>若郑姜之颍出，其事罔伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236948_comment'></div>翕如睹大练之光，来归著彤管之炜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236948_comment'></div>臣等幸叨盛际，祇若徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236948_comment'></div>坤载延鸿，殆年长于西母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236948_comment'></div>皇枝繁衍，益天受于太任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236948_comment'></div>臣无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷七。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236948_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1236948'>绍兴十二年：原无，案《宋史》卷三○《高宗纪》七：是年二月，「金主许归梓宫及皇太后」，八月至临安，此与文意合，据补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1236948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　苏籀领工有绩，转朝散郎。作品：《谢转朝散郎牋》<div id='poem_1237000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转朝散郎笺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237000")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237000'>右，籀启：准诰转前件官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237000_comment'></div>俟罪冗僚，庀工陈力，伟中兴仪典之旧，课攸司荣观之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237000_comment'></div>委办落成，计功予爵，涣丝纶之恻怛，陟班叙于峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237000_comment'></div>微夫草木之生，浃此云天之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237000_comment'></div>伛偻祗命，跼蹐衔恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237000_comment'></div>窃以阶太平而礼乐兴，观会通而圣神作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237000_comment'></div>岂干戈倥偬之后，废文物声明之昭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237000_comment'></div>诚习肄更始之秋，副跂耸观瞻之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237000_comment'></div>东观曲台之轶，多得残书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237000_comment'></div>总章衢室之闻，咨访故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237000_comment'></div>诚稽古制今之际，聊息马讲艺于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237000_comment'></div>循枝派而寻根源，酌沿革而求通变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237000_comment'></div>顺遂品汇，统叶天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237000_comment'></div>岂庸末之所知，赖真儒之爰立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237000_comment'></div>鸿惟主上，备雕玉之龙驾，建虹霓之修竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237000_comment'></div>三辰旂旗，前殿正衙之仗卫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237000_comment'></div>五色比象，太室亲祀之文容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237000_comment'></div>翕九奏万舞以祝南山，天日澄朗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237000_comment'></div>制六乐三雍以纳和气，遐迩允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237000_comment'></div>盖叔孙绵蕝要务，则汉高知皇帝之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237000_comment'></div>张纯答诏引经，而光武定禘祫之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237000_comment'></div>昔号嘉会，今固昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237000_comment'></div>典章著明，英髦杂遝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237000_comment'></div>抱图谍铅椠而订议者，殆国侨、向戌之俦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237000_comment'></div>执斲锻橐钥而精新者，必欧冶、工倕之侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237000_comment'></div>裁成悉具，允副责成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237000_comment'></div>殆将比三代而符同，何特超二汉而融赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237000_comment'></div>籀缪督监掌，展究恪恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237000_comment'></div>怀败材伤锦之羞，祇注瓦镕金之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237000_comment'></div>几希庆扁鐻轮之斲，敢萌爵禄徐疾之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237000_comment'></div>幸无苦窳之嫌，各竭精能之伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237000_comment'></div>恃上仁之淘汰，俾下情之奔趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237000_comment'></div>悉皆乐职之常，姑免鄙儒之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237000_comment'></div>近蒙奏最，遂玷恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237000_comment'></div>再惟太师公相禀高明磊落之姿，佐浚哲皇极之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237000_comment'></div>嘉谟猷之凝远，摅美利之无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1237000_comment'></div>大节大劳，冠映前后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1237000_comment'></div>一心一德，致理清宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1237000_comment'></div>从容两社之间，进止弗失尺寸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1237000_comment'></div>仓卒万难之会，酬酢不改色声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1237000_comment'></div>贯穿流略而潜涵，师范群儒之视效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1237000_comment'></div>自得乎度数纪律之表，研精乎载籍根本之元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1237000_comment'></div>发端古文，赞翊洪造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1237000_comment'></div>缉熙办画，和洽光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1237000_comment'></div>搢绅孰不尽乃心，氓庶亦使同其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1237000_comment'></div>念枵琐逖疏之迹，采肤末盲进之勤，假借甄收，庇焘迂拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1237000_comment'></div>籀方且激昂志见，警策事为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1237000_comment'></div>叩閤怀笺，未为报效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1237000_comment'></div>执经授道，久愿依归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1237000_comment'></div>上恃宽洪，恕其臞懦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1237000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年4月</a>　四月丙戌，苏籀上书高宗议补撰《五经正义》，高宗谓“此论甚当”。作品：《初论经解札子》<div id='poem_1236956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初论经解劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236956")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236956'>臣闻圣经贤传，唐虞三代所遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236956_comment'></div>阙里之业，王者乐道尊儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236956_comment'></div>内自九重，化流寰海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236956_comment'></div>金华露门，咨访䌷绎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236956_comment'></div>辟雍东观，群能感奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236956_comment'></div>俾天下品类回心向正，政孚教洽，三代之盛，汉唐之隆，及吾祖宗圣功休烈，六籍之效著矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236956_comment'></div>鸿惟陛下生而知之，孳孳舜善，听朝之隙，横经畴咨，宵旰睿览，研几简编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236956_comment'></div>建立太学，首善之始，崇道辩惑，渥恩养士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236956_comment'></div>臣等遭际作兴，带经负笈，陶沐亭育，绅笏周行，峨弁就列，跂望睟穆之仪，而又昧死轮对轩陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236956_comment'></div>当得言之秋，非有涓尘称塞右文，以谓不足以为士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236956_comment'></div>窃闻永平之岁，期门、羽林肄习名教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236956_comment'></div>贞观之盛，屯营飞骑受书博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236956_comment'></div>臣固驽下，亦知竦慕，狂斐儳说，不揆其愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236956_comment'></div>昔者仲尼删定《系》《彖》，笔削问周史、闻齐《韶》，而《诗》、《书》、《易》《、礼》、《乐》、《春秋》各得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236956_comment'></div>惟举要发端，不详其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236956_comment'></div>非不能详也，以为详之则隘，故略之，使仁智者自求而得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236956_comment'></div>逮夫李斯灭学之后，出于屋壁，既非全经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236956_comment'></div>两汉颛门之流，白首讲贯，受授相传，深不负仲尼之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236956_comment'></div>虎观、石渠，抠衣重席，论难纷纭，开益后人多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236956_comment'></div>唐文皇时，初诏颜师古考究章程，孔颖达撰定义疏，遂为天下定论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236956_comment'></div>此两汉、魏、晋以来千古儒术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236956_comment'></div>夫六经微言妙用，非可易解而遽晓，始学必由传疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236956_comment'></div>近岁兵火，典籍残缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236956_comment'></div>比日诸州刊印稍备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236956_comment'></div>今之诸生所以穷经，舍正义、传注则懵然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236956_comment'></div>此非一代之所私，一家之偏说，一夫之独智，辑合淘汰，千载宇宙之公是非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236956_comment'></div>但汉初儒者，各譊譊师习《诗》、《书》、《春秋》，古文初不甚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236956_comment'></div>《公》、《谷》方炽，《左氏》废锢，故三代遗典乖戾不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236956_comment'></div>唐人因旧承疑，去取粗当，未暇大有发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236956_comment'></div>易数乐律，至今不得其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236956_comment'></div>臣愿陛下特诏名儒学官，既蓄聚唐之义疏，复录近世儒臣以学显者所著讲解，申敕州县，委自守贰，网罗募辑，刊刻抄录，储之太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236956_comment'></div>臣尝思念本朝祖宗以来，名世豪杰之士，体道弥切，经艺疏解愈明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236956_comment'></div>知先儒有未悟者，条目甚夥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236956_comment'></div>本朝之学光矣，非累圣神化不能然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236956_comment'></div>意者商较评品，假以岁年，加秩给费，纂而成编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236956_comment'></div>古人有「集传」、「集解」之号，补唐之《正义》阙遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236956_comment'></div>凡说皆通则并存之，疑者阙之，不妄凿焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236956_comment'></div>庶几孔氏之旧，祖宗右文，实赖陛下为之统纪，甚盛举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236956_comment'></div>其于设科取士，考信万方，究析道真，扶翊名教，使天下后世涤耳刿目，伏膺不忒，实文治之伟迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236956_comment'></div>臣不胜犬马昧死越职上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236956_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1236956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年4月</a>　上书论收用勇武谋略之人。作品：《论收用武略之士札子》<div id='poem_1236957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论收用武略之士劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236957")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236957'>臣恭惟陛下仁圣慈武，驾驭积贤之符，天人显相，故能服强敌，安土宇，四方乂宁，右文兴化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236957_comment'></div>士生斯辰，操觚挟翰者罔不竞劝，咸以无文为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236957_comment'></div>步趋先后，圆冠方履，溢于中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236957_comment'></div>丕平极治，礼乐具备，寖隆盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236957_comment'></div>臣愚窃见近世干戈之际，武力常恨不振，今虽平康，岂遽弛焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236957_comment'></div>恭惟本朝艺祖之武，太宗之文，列圣重其光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236957_comment'></div>所课试区别，尽天下之才，致太平，防患难，文武二柄，未尝偏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236957_comment'></div>天生五材，缺一不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236957_comment'></div>《书》曰：「帝德广运，乃武乃文」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236957_comment'></div>今之识擢武士，不若用文士之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236957_comment'></div>天下之事，莫难于用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236957_comment'></div>中国文明冠带之俗，士闲习于辞艺，不足者武也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236957_comment'></div>盗贼蛮獠之儆，何日无之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236957_comment'></div>今三府有桉琐之吏，外台有馈运之臣，皆所以振兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236957_comment'></div>英奇鸷果，倜傥厌难之才，或不肯由场屋，诚别有以笼罩之，亦多途矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236957_comment'></div>古人有言曰：「物有不求，未有无物之岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236957_comment'></div>士有不用，未有无士之时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236957_comment'></div>万一江海飘沦，往而弗返，异域之人，尚或招来之以为我用，况在吾邦者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236957_comment'></div>凡修政当修之于可修之时，今国家闲暇，理宜致意，一旦仓猝乃求，恐非豫备之策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236957_comment'></div>昔汉高帝总揽天下英杰，而叹曰：「安得猛士兮守四方」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236957_comment'></div>此盖帝王之度，不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236957_comment'></div>登坛受钺，非太平事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236957_comment'></div>旌擢观省，储蓄优遇，亦欲补夫戎阃兽符乘障被羽之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236957_comment'></div>今之宿将，例各休老，后辈威名著者几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236957_comment'></div>勇智可用之辈偶至，失于甄录；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236957_comment'></div>或沉埋军中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236957_comment'></div>嫉于骄将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236957_comment'></div>或汩于贱远，无以自达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236957_comment'></div>或触犯文法，武人常理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236957_comment'></div>宽以容之，索之而出，养之而成，其可已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236957_comment'></div>夫斯民豢于太平之乐，游娱饮博，心志恬嬉，军中投石超距之气索矣，可无猛烈之士倡率之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236957_comment'></div>膏粱华屋之性习，至若冲霜雪，冒炎埃，饥渴驱驰，趋死不悔，惟山泽辛苦之士有以为焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236957_comment'></div>万夫之望，殆此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236957_comment'></div>今之军伍既无出战捕虏可赏，科举粗收策略弓马之名，此外莫若明诏迩缀公卿与戎帅、统督、监司，岁荐所知武勇杰出之人，朝廷置籍甄品，时加召擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236957_comment'></div>绝出伦类如祖宗时郭进、李汉超，削平之后曹玮、李允则、种世衡之流，奇略高才，不易得矣，古人未能远过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236957_comment'></div>《书》曰「载采采」，历言其事状也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236957_comment'></div>《诗》曰「南有嘉鱼，烝然罩罩」，言勤取之必获也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236957_comment'></div>庶几复得如此之流，守边临敌，永不乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236957_comment'></div>臣无任私忧过计、拳拳越职上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236957_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1236957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年4月</a>　有诗留别赵令穰及姪子十七秀才。作品：《留别赵大年并姪十七秀才》<div id='poem_139749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留别赵大年并侄十七秀才<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139749")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139749'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139749'>晋公宾佐选，英毅冠朝端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139749'>三日拂冠剑，一时增羽翰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139749'>世家存器质，国论伫图难。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139749'>从此抛经卷，青毡拜近官。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139749'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139749_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_139748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139748?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139748'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139748'>君年有馀富，我老渐来侵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139748'>莽苍麇鼯野，峙停鸾鹄音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139748'>藜羹秉觚牍，筚路向山林。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139748'>商略古人意，孜孜不患深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年7月</a>　与苏简、苏策游龙井。作品：《甲子岁七夕与伯业、伯衍游龙井，聰老出示次韵边校理诗卷，奉同雅趣一首，借用嚬字》<div id='poem_139811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲子岁七夕与伯业伯衍游龙井聪老出示次韵边校理诗卷奉同雅趣一首借用嚬字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139811")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139811'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139811'>道隐祖风邈，讷斋重葺新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139811'>猊巘下兽魅，神泓跃鳍鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139811'>缁郎踵教律，梵夹画金银。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139811'>几岸风篁帻，屡钩崖峭绅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139811'>颂诗传正眼，击节富其人。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139811'>汉沔曾沦碣，长康工写神。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139811'>思茇在封植，春萝容抗尘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139811'>韡萼秀多襈，茶瓜经几巡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139811'>休休墨儒行，汲汲宰官身。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139811'>欠伸白氎褥，翻倒明玑囷。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139811'>䔲褐岚烟染，心脾草树亲。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139811'>怜君深锻炼，公鉴褒老嚬。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139811'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_139811_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年7月</a>　次韵龙井僧人所示苏籍、程寄庵诗。作品：《龙井僧全示寄庵枢密程公累篇季文弟新什求余继其末一首》<div id='poem_139815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙井僧全示寄庵枢密程公累篇季文弟新什求余继其末一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139815")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139815'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139815'>程苏中兴什，同庵有后前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139815'>前朝沙门首，辨净超卓然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139815'>耆宿失闻聪，饫参馀小全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139815'>龙泓风篁巘，荏苒二十年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139815'>缁俦几换易，岩崿岂变迁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139815'>亭亭百岁杉，泠泠九渊泉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139815'>梵音扰龙性，玄解忘鱼筌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139815'>有客辇瑰诡，无情施缯钱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139815'>佛法伫隆兴，般若须人传。<div id='poem_sentence_8_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_139815'>更令观刹丽，但俾子孙贤。<div id='poem_sentence_9_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_139815'>三空正觉路，一喻实相圆。<div id='poem_sentence_10_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_139815'>不替人天师，重新演教禅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_139815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_139815'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_139815_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　苏籀八弟赴桂林干办买马事，苏籀有诗送行，以“德刑两寄”、“日闢神州”为说。作品：《送都属八舍人桂林买马一首》<div id='poem_139868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送都属八舍弟桂林买马一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139868")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_139868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139868'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139868'>夷德贪婪汉财贿，莫惜金多能使鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139868'>喷玉难拘伏波式，上驷超摇献天子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139868'>子今叱驭湘南裔，桂岭下下复高高，鸟惊兽骇征人喟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139868'>当官官事从容理，思马斯臧由此始。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139868'>电尾风騣未平齿，绝壑踔山如历块。<div id='poem_sentence_4_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_139868'>执驱效牵髯校尉，槽枥经由书殿最。<div id='poem_sentence_5_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_139868'>谢公总统修戎备，二柄德刑兼两寄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_139868'>不矜吾党愈推能，宵旰潜心活国计。<div id='poem_sentence_7_139868_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_139868'>杂沓英豪乘虎骑，日辟神州一百里。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_139868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　苏籀罢京官，有诗。作品：《解罢京局一首》<div id='poem_139773' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139773' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139773?labeling=true' target='_blank'>解罢京局一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139773")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139773_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139773'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139773'>运水担柴力分遭，挟持泥古小儒劳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139773'>浙潮屹起岷峨上，越巘遮蟠江海滔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139773'>一叶鸥湍寻婺女，半生瓢泛信鱼舠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139773'>曩时瓜步从容侣，好糁藜羹待共轑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139773'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139773_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='200a1722ba754a5a9a853e25f53454a4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("200a1722ba754a5a9a853e25f53454a4");'><span id='200a1722ba754a5a9a853e25f53454a4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1159')">1158-1159年</a>，68-69岁</div><div id='200a1722ba754a5a9a853e25f53454a4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年2月</a>　二月丙申，陈诚之自同知枢密院事除知枢密院事，苏籀作书。作品：《牋陈知院》<div id='poem_1237024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺陈知院</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237024")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237024'>伏以赵武长弭兵之聘会，信重春秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237024_comment'></div>孙宏魁亲策之甲科，厌服髦俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237024_comment'></div>摅真才而称职，创贤业而竞时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237024_comment'></div>岳岳吁谟，堂堂伟绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237024_comment'></div>该四科乎阙里，联二八于虞廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237024_comment'></div>若鸢飞鱼跃之穹卑，无逃昭察；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237024_comment'></div>被桂郁兰芬之薰染，孰不欣陪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237024_comment'></div>致景山学海之徒，皆希颜慕蔺之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237024_comment'></div>仰跂墙仞，瞻系声华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237024_comment'></div>傥择其区区之图，亦犹用九九之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237024_comment'></div>比义与道，相求不间夫显严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237024_comment'></div>畴曩甄评，流品衷怀于诱掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237024_comment'></div>罄拳鞠之戴属，蕴悃款之忱忠，激昂之姿，谢绝何可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237024_comment'></div>听歌飏于鸿美，俾宣吐于刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237024_comment'></div>或者其淟陋狂狷，乐附于宽明博大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237024_comment'></div>亟蒙冒于英重，未悉屏于幽遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237024_comment'></div>大冶大钧，熟测裁成之运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237024_comment'></div>小夫小智，岂无一篑之堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237024_comment'></div>恭惟枢密相公本兴王之道，蹑先哲之踪，懿醇禀天，沈机建事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237024_comment'></div>讨邺侯之坟籍，草曼倩之简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237024_comment'></div>志大弥纶，酬九重之亲遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237024_comment'></div>识优讲画，协同德而赞襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237024_comment'></div>天骄重第一之人，世议誉知十之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237024_comment'></div>云间阔步，尘外清标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237024_comment'></div>仁宅理窟以渊源，心匠智囊其警拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237024_comment'></div>帷幄言词密勿，樽俎资略研几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237024_comment'></div>岂特文儒所宗，可谓柄臣之杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237024_comment'></div>忠规雅算，胜气雄风，将相之所倚毗，勋阀必将久大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237024_comment'></div>籀枵虚羸惫，朴野龙钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237024_comment'></div>投耒延陵之皋，敛板巨源之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237024_comment'></div>峨弁已成乎俗韵，曳裾来叩于德闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237024_comment'></div>当代之龙津在兹，借势之鸿毛欲起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237024_comment'></div>盖矜愚诲短，实祈高位之慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237024_comment'></div>求善度材，是谓上臣之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237024_comment'></div>顾铅驽之无取，或桑榆之可收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237024_comment'></div>顾观东閤之宾，庶荷晚涂之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1237024_comment'></div>钦戴成颂，敷述汗颜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1237024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年2月</a>　二月乙巳，王纶自工部除同知枢密院事，苏籀作贺启。作品：《贺王枢密启》<div id='poem_1237028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺王枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237028")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237028'>伏审荣膺中诏，进任西枢，凡预晤游，概有光幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237028_comment'></div>窃以中兴开廓贤路，体貌迩僚，变化鹏鲲，驾驭龙虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237028_comment'></div>骋麟骥于大路，翔鸾鸿于紫霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237028_comment'></div>嘉注奋庸之俊髦，咨诹考慎之详谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237028_comment'></div>殚一心以体国，申公议而得君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237028_comment'></div>启沃智辩之哲谋，揆揣几微之图虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237028_comment'></div>赞赞夙夜之忠笃，明明覈实之圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237028_comment'></div>恭惟枢密相公清警昭融，冲裕高特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237028_comment'></div>学推绅笏，道著岩廊，蕴拔萃之姿，副异常之奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237028_comment'></div>睿慈柬向，儒效辑成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237028_comment'></div>倚马仙掖之赞书，批凤淮南之视草；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237028_comment'></div>密勿兼官于起部，清切儤直于右垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237028_comment'></div>裁定朝章，演润国纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237028_comment'></div>金銮密旨，蔚瑞世之典彝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237028_comment'></div>玉清讨论，信代天之喉舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237028_comment'></div>委紫枢提著述之柄，任黄阁主文艺之盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237028_comment'></div>奏篇机鉴于帝谟，封章缉熙于王度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237028_comment'></div>斗杓掌武，无竞惟人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237028_comment'></div>鼎饪用和，非贤弗乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237028_comment'></div>正始之闻博备，太平之基愈隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237028_comment'></div>越石偶遭于晏婴，淳髡遂服乎邹忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237028_comment'></div>筋骨翱、愈，源本轲、雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237028_comment'></div>揄扬甄藻以英明，咀噍经济之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237028_comment'></div>珍策重计，懿画肤功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237028_comment'></div>师律将符，韬钤熟讲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237028_comment'></div>官箴士范，衡石精明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237028_comment'></div>详味渥恩，允旌盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237028_comment'></div>籀罢更川峡之戍，即安琳馆之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237028_comment'></div>近传好音，下风惊喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237028_comment'></div>附词林之根蒂，托钧量之帡幪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237028_comment'></div>缪陈截截之言，难写依依之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1237028_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　上书，论取士优《春秋三传》作品：《论取士专优春秋三传札子》<div id='poem_1236958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论取士专优春秋三传劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236958")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236958'>臣昧死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236958_comment'></div>恭惟本朝以诗赋、经义造士，庶几《虞书》「飏言」之举，于斯得人，祖宗朝甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236958_comment'></div>迩日海内诸生穷计圣籍，该洽道艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236958_comment'></div>义疏名家，群士慕向，罔不遵周孔之轨躅，纂阙里之旨趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236958_comment'></div>《易》、《诗》、《书》及二《礼》，先王谟猷，贯穿详备，课有厥程，惟《春秋》一经，前此废绝不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236958_comment'></div>陛下稽古睿明，注意经传，致令学者讨仿脩习，今既举行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236958_comment'></div>二百四十二年文字，五家浩博，以其久遭摈弃，其说孤寂，罕为人所讲授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236958_comment'></div>仅有治者，终恐芜翳，有识之士咨嗟叹息！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236958_comment'></div>此书笔削乃文王之文，褒贬则周公之法，礼义大宗，伯王通典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236958_comment'></div>考周之所以王，有邦家者守经事而欲知其宜，更变礼而欲知其权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236958_comment'></div>是非劝戒，系天下表仪绳准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236958_comment'></div>别嫌疑、定犹豫，至断妙用，世所希闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236958_comment'></div>传业者优柔浸渍，积久转解，实不易领会也，古之君子穷此学，白首不辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236958_comment'></div>惟经之体要，固天下国家本务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236958_comment'></div>丘明受经仲尼，厥为附《传》，非私意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236958_comment'></div>前代称左氏古学所载，䌷绎三代礼乐，上纪牺、炎、唐、虞、禹、汤、周、孔遗轶，齐晋伯主，尊奖王室，舍此何据焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236958_comment'></div>又公、谷二儒传经子夏，二《传》乃孔徒遗旨典则，非后世所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236958_comment'></div>西汉贾谊、贾嘉相与纂继此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236958_comment'></div>光武中兴，立《左氏》博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236958_comment'></div>唐文皇早岁受麟经之谊，晋代杜预宗趣渊源，大贤所业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236958_comment'></div>夫治《春秋》之学，如贾及杜，皆名世伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236958_comment'></div>臣愿陛下明诏中外有司，场屋诗赋策论，命题措意，或用《春秋》三《传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236958_comment'></div>礼闱取人，特优此孔经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236958_comment'></div>分数不妨以声律定去留，柬求精悉杰俊知类通达者，置在博学师儒之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236958_comment'></div>如谊、预才谟，飞声迈烈，未必乏其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236958_comment'></div>俾琐琐懵学虽欲夸世，亦不斥而自屏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236958_comment'></div>臣愚乌足以究其闳奥，极其高坚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236958_comment'></div>不胜恳恳披写之诚，所有越职，不敢逃罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236958_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1236958_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年1月</a>　正月丙辰朔，皇太后八十寿辰，高宗诣慈宁殿行庆寿礼，苏籀上贺表。作品：《慈宁庆八十贺表》<div id='poem_1236951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慈宁庆八十贺表<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十九正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236951")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236951'>母仪慈懿，帝孝遵承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236951_comment'></div>慕孳孳之色难，躬显显之爱立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236951_comment'></div>协气流乎闱壸，要道光于华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236951_comment'></div>稽前古之姜、任，继今朝之高、向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236951_comment'></div>王化辅毗之燮理，椒屋兰闺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236951_comment'></div>坤元博载以无疆，龙舆宝玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236951_comment'></div>于皇万斯之纪，肇登八十之龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236951_comment'></div>三灵之溥命咸宜，九有之欢心一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236951_comment'></div>甲子环匝，幅员雍熙<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236951_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下体古训于韦编，运嘉猷于掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236951_comment'></div>德之所覃者大，文之所加者深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236951_comment'></div>宏休难罄于揄扬，尽美兼全于仁孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236951_comment'></div>臣萤蚁至眇，愿增缀《南陔》雅章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236951_comment'></div>绅笏合并，庆无量西竺遐寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236951_comment'></div>尧时舜旦，兽舞樵讴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236951_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1236951_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年7月</a>　七月丁亥，贺允中自吏部侍郎除参知政事，苏籀作贺书。作品：《牋贺参政》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年9月</a>　九月陈康伯、汤思退为左、右仆射，苏籀作贺书。作品：《上汤丞相书》《牋陈仆射》<div id='poem_1236970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上汤丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236970")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236970'>月日，籀谨斋沐裁书，献于昭文仆射相公阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236970_comment'></div>窃惟方今天下之势，大小纲纪，斟酌调维，庙堂邃深，道周术远，算数精审，干邦槐棘之彦，命世佐时之机，凡常庶官不足议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236970_comment'></div>仆就义忠公之诚、奕世补报之心，弗以荣贱闲剧易其介，徒以忧虑私叹激其衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236970_comment'></div>屑屑孜孜，邀祈控诉，愤悱拳拳，所愿瞻依者天下大老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236970_comment'></div>伏惟阁下稽古致时，应半千之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236970_comment'></div>攀云附翼，励盖世之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236970_comment'></div>秉人文师表，蕴智辩裁成，冠一时而绥庶邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236970_comment'></div>谦而加之以求善无厌，健以至于宣勤不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236970_comment'></div>顷日小夫不自分限，轻千里而扫行马之门闼，趋宥府之严屏，抠衣鸱堂，鞠躬望履，瑟僩令仪，自然休质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236970_comment'></div>乃蒙抑损穹崇，诲诱卑品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236970_comment'></div>钦景风之穆，戴冬日之温，想宗庙之美，觌百官之富，高大远密，岂容隐度？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236970_comment'></div>强记默识，秀伟绝伦，信可谓君子之宗盟，士林之根蒂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236970_comment'></div>此时不敢以刍言触闻贵听，私意拔耸慕爱，吁，已久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236970_comment'></div>主上枚卜，首简左辅魁柄，道协时来，陛隆堂高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236970_comment'></div>阁下从容予夺，六事百司罔不风从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236970_comment'></div>画一建明，鲜不奉为律令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236970_comment'></div>内有精思起草之亭，外辟钦贤翘材之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236970_comment'></div>庶政准程，公道皂白，指踪武干，范模文场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236970_comment'></div>政理赫焉如日正中，勋绩浩乎如川方至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236970_comment'></div>百度无滞，九功可歌，不淹岁月而谐允矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236970_comment'></div>方且兴复汴雒，恢廓中原，有成岂待三载，天下孰不倾心延颈而俟也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236970_comment'></div>于皇当阳，圣造求理之锐，万方注赖之切，捍患拔艰，畴咨良哲，必务疾速以副之，决断而答之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236970_comment'></div>敕天稽众之吁谟，广士博选之至要，不可以不汲汲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236970_comment'></div>天下之形声，虽娄、旷不能周览遍闻，分治而岂无遗忧，汎应而岂无遗使？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236970_comment'></div>惟明鉴大度，虚中诹索，访问援引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236970_comment'></div>人之好我，弗疑弗猜，无怠无斁，悉厥胸腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236970_comment'></div>俾来者虚徐，区别以崇其资略，甄升以收其器能，此纳揆之叙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236970_comment'></div>贤者必表，良者必进，此天下公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236970_comment'></div>夫哲谋肃乂，公实要切之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236970_comment'></div>智囊心匠，长国家者之所贪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236970_comment'></div>山不让土，故极其高；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236970_comment'></div>海不择流，以极其深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236970_comment'></div>天官地祇，有神物主之，非徒然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236970_comment'></div>且如多士之中，随、管经济，韩、白韬钤，威、文节制，龚、黄风化，游、夏文学，然、桑心计，赵、张钩距，或各遐阻，不能自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236970_comment'></div>纲目所加，裘领既振，非所虑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236970_comment'></div>昔燕昭厚币以聘郭隗，遂致乐毅、邹衍、剧辛三杰，凡所欲果得，所求果成，燕以之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236970_comment'></div>盖似善斯举，真善必来矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236970_comment'></div>似才斯拔，真才即至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236970_comment'></div>先王吁俊无方，重使一夫不被，以此功利遍物，举措适当，其可数计乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236970_comment'></div>夫未发之机，藏伏之符，必有能辨之人，瞻前顾后，左摩右揣，诹度之加详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236970_comment'></div>晋赵武举管库之士七十家，唐崔祐甫除吏八百，吾邦何为而不可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236970_comment'></div>仆琐琐龊龊，滥从下大夫之缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236970_comment'></div>自视聱牙寡合，冒进谒于吾大老之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236970_comment'></div>惟是承前人义，自幼缪纂所学，造夫小者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236970_comment'></div>近者幸蒙不拒其庸劣，赐之进前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236970_comment'></div>他日曚昧瞽说，因事尘献自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236970_comment'></div>昔者贾谊五十八篇，陆贽之文百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236970_comment'></div>二公究丘旦壸奥，系华夏休戚，后学之龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236970_comment'></div>致时资治，窒隙拾遗，诚在夫勉励稽覈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236970_comment'></div>又顷岁蒙睿训，擢丞奉常，以其志尚有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236970_comment'></div>区区所尚，心志确固，纶綍既出，必有所取，诚不敢少隳其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236970_comment'></div>先祖遗训曰：「士而无益于世，谓之苟生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236970_comment'></div>窃诵斯言，未尝弭忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236970_comment'></div>恭惟阁下宣慈博大，包蓄庶僚，肤末不才，万冀无鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236970_comment'></div>干渎大钧，战慄死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236970_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1236970_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺陈仆射</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237030")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237030'>伏审光奉册书，进跻宰席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237030_comment'></div>显近详试，协赞虔恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237030_comment'></div>盖心膂坚而股肱良，由陛廉远而堂皇峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237030_comment'></div>覆金甄之褒表，加玉铉之利亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237030_comment'></div>先志定于当阳，洽言佥于首正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237030_comment'></div>造膝吁谟之湛审，爰立庆会之非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237030_comment'></div>概有识知，符同竦贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237030_comment'></div>恭惟本朝虚伫以图赞邦治理，褒锡于□瑞世真贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237030_comment'></div>忠智揆策而执权，睿文前席而向纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237030_comment'></div>上下相须而相济，圣彦相值而相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237030_comment'></div>不紊乎枢轴纪纲之条，密勿乎章程课覈之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237030_comment'></div>坐论对时之务，柄揭援拯之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237030_comment'></div>苏海内之倒悬，次第六奇秘计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237030_comment'></div>削中原之左衽，雍容九合肤功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237030_comment'></div>料敌伐谋，应机全仗异士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237030_comment'></div>攀云附翼，同寅莫匪钜才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237030_comment'></div>生民将乐于华胥，羽卫伫归于洛汴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237030_comment'></div>持衡尺熙乎帝载，俨端委代于天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237030_comment'></div>致主愈谐，庇人弥夥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237030_comment'></div>伏惟集贤仆射相公毓粹元精，禀灵神岳，间出挺生于拔萃，渊懿自得乎时中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237030_comment'></div>光明显融，调一新美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237030_comment'></div>该典籍理世之具，纂庙朝循道之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237030_comment'></div>兼四科而有光，论万机而至悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237030_comment'></div>可以应无穷之资略，故允出益办之弥纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237030_comment'></div>谐弼裁成，风采号令，等魏弱公之学识，切李文饶之虑图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237030_comment'></div>潜心王体之缉熙，尽节国是而翊亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237030_comment'></div>优优措置之标的，矫矫决果之蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1237030_comment'></div>同舆辀车，若左右手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1237030_comment'></div>接士藻鉴，故应任耇而迩英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1237030_comment'></div>及物恩波，何胜数计而周度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1237030_comment'></div>钩致俊伟，备患折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1237030_comment'></div>驯扰遐荒，櫜弓却马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1237030_comment'></div>宁壹太平之业，运用文武而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1237030_comment'></div>鄙庸俯伏于下风，仁杰宜在于高位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1237030_comment'></div>跂闻宠陟，稍欲激昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1237030_comment'></div>想广博之甄评，宣自公之元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1237030_comment'></div>道义不隔于富贵，旱旸借润于滂霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1237030_comment'></div>大度高风，窥较岂易？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1237030_comment'></div>古心奇韵，取予无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1237030_comment'></div>驰神闬闳，引脰符照，倾颂之素，敷叙曷殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1237030_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　眉山族人二十八郎应试下第，苏籀作诗送归。作品：《送苏念八郎下第西归梁益》<div id='poem_139733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送苏念八郎下第西归梁益</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_139733")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_139733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_139733'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139733'>金昌亭下泊舟舻，木马关西赵郡苏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139733'>建邺鱼飧武昌水，延陵皋壤霸王都。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139733'>吾髯轩轶登楼赋，汝器切磨清庙瑚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_139733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_139733'>刷羽三馀鸿鹄举，亨衢甲乙看先驱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_139733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_139733'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_139733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　在临安。有诗。作品：《疏懒》《王季海求父朝议挽词二首》<br /></div>

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　至绍兴府任参议官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　春，正月丁未朔，高宗御大殿初行大朝会礼，苏籀上贺表。作品：《贺元会表》<div id='poem_1236949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺元会表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236949")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236949'>伏以垂象施教，大一统于王正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236949_comment'></div>凝冕当阳，举盛仪于元朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236949_comment'></div>稽详周典，采摭汉儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236949_comment'></div>夷夏来同，天人昭格<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236949_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下体元正大，建极中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236949_comment'></div>曩者每多外御之虞，是以未遑正宁之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236949_comment'></div>裁成补救，肇自睿图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236949_comment'></div>和洽光辉，允谓儒效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236949_comment'></div>向明而治，谨始授时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236949_comment'></div>设九宾之胪传，受四海之图籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236949_comment'></div>万汇待发生之庆，十行布宽大之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236949_comment'></div>物备礼隆，发声明于度数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236949_comment'></div>化孚泽浃，正班爵而纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236949_comment'></div>臣夙滥寘行，坐縻外补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236949_comment'></div>想簪绅之表著，望云日以神驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236949_comment'></div>承明宣政之庭，固尝俯伏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236949_comment'></div>衢室合宫之事，殆无复过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236949_comment'></div>嘉与苍黔，同兹鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236949_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1236949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　苏籀以王次翁离任荐己，作书谢之。作品：《牋交代王中丞》《贺王中丞启》<div id='poem_1237020' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237020' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237020?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺交代王宗丞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237020")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237020_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237020'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237020'>伏念联镳接武，参朝会于都门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237020_comment'></div>歛板趋风，赴官期于闽峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237020_comment'></div>画图莫逆，邑里素交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237020_comment'></div>岂意暌携，复叨更代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237020_comment'></div>强宝婺衰慵之迹，登稽山佐谋之司，蹈袭风规，咨度职守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237020_comment'></div>伏惟交代参谋宗丞历落青云之职具，高标黄阁之渊源，羽仪天朝，润色家学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237020_comment'></div>挟保邦之懋术，怀赞世之令图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237020_comment'></div>翕然远迩之见珍，所到衣冠之竦慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237020_comment'></div>如石投水，若玉在山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237020_comment'></div>著鞭遄迈于华涂，入幕误留于外镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237020_comment'></div>自今加秩命之数，超腾于伯仲之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237020_comment'></div>籀久荷矜庥，多承友益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237020_comment'></div>方幸促席而倾展，傥容弭盖而周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237020_comment'></div>会觌之欣，颂咏罔既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1237020_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺王中丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236997")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236997'>伏审显膺休命，擢领南司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236997_comment'></div>席绝百僚，副清衷之重委；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236997_comment'></div>胪传万口，诚圣上之知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236997_comment'></div>凡在听观，莫不钦竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236997_comment'></div>恭惟帝王立本建中之道，朝廷褒直尽下之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236997_comment'></div>揆策于无眚之途，置器于永宁之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236997_comment'></div>致君子小人咸适其分，使庶工群品各竭厥能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236997_comment'></div>宽恤疲羸，抵排邪枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236997_comment'></div>屈人兵于不战，消祸衅于未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236997_comment'></div>老成仪刑，师表动静，虚伫咨访之益，允若忧勤之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236997_comment'></div>百志惟熙，万问必理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236997_comment'></div>伏惟中丞阁下有专通新一之学，极切磨餍饫之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236997_comment'></div>析蜀执戟之元文，究鲁感麟之旨趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236997_comment'></div>澄清揽辔，民誉攸归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236997_comment'></div>模范贤关，士风丕格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236997_comment'></div>不枉己以阿徇，惟信道而全醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236997_comment'></div>告老投闲，穷而不愠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236997_comment'></div>弼违救失，辩且难当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236997_comment'></div>初无爵禄之心，宁复得丧之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236997_comment'></div>丘樊恬佚，甘独乐于无何；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236997_comment'></div>轩冕傥来，蹈中庸而克合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236997_comment'></div>迁陟二史，超历三台，减仪休之圃蔬，仍平津之布被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236997_comment'></div>词章藻鉴，宜典掌于文盟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236997_comment'></div>诚正威风，妙弥纶于国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236997_comment'></div>显显大节，郁郁高谟，积著忠劳，殆登疑弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236997_comment'></div>然不鄙蓬蒿而徙眷，罔憎筦库以移交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236997_comment'></div>笑常情之猥卑，见达人之大观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236997_comment'></div>朴遫小吏，偃伏下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236997_comment'></div>曾何毫末之裨，每借江湖之润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236997_comment'></div>叨尘选取，出自称知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236997_comment'></div>误玷周行，方依奖诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236997_comment'></div>抠衣坐末，或偶合于小言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236997_comment'></div>仰首朝端，真难逢之嘉会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236997_comment'></div>不愿执鞭而求富，幸观极笔以谈王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236997_comment'></div>欣戴之私，敷颂难悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1236997_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　翟参议有书相贺，苏籀作启答之。作品：《回翟参议启》<div id='poem_1237021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回翟参议启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237021")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237021'>伏念暌违星纪，羁游随牒之踪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237021_comment'></div>谟画日畿，同舍为僚之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237021_comment'></div>浙湍遄驶，齐舫将临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237021_comment'></div>宠贶滕缄，记存拊念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237021_comment'></div>咨诹幕府，参论咸推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237021_comment'></div>伏惟参议学士德门承则，艺苑老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237021_comment'></div>允膺慎柬之除，竦听殊常之擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237021_comment'></div>交游慕乐，方将薰习于芝兰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237021_comment'></div>将吏辑谐，密烦部勒于韬略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237021_comment'></div>遵海一时之善士，在邦三益之良朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237021_comment'></div>获际高贤，岂为小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237021_comment'></div>颂咏之恳，敷染何穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237021_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1237021_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　曹机宜有书相贺，苏籀作启答之。作品：《答曹机宜启》<div id='poem_1237022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答曹机宜启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237022")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237022'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237022'>伏承泥封青竹，重问相存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237022_comment'></div>油幕红莲，行将临屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237022_comment'></div>东道戎机之密，上贤咨度之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237022_comment'></div>焕炳懿词，竦侧嘉惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237022_comment'></div>嘘呵衰钝，激发枵芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237022_comment'></div>伏惟机宜学士嶷嶷柬僚，席勋门之济美；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237022_comment'></div>潭潭大镇，簉宾位之阙员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237022_comment'></div>晓畅军咨，光被朝委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237022_comment'></div>设招贤之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1237022", 1237022, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>连榻</span>，侍致胜之良筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237022_comment'></div>联翩奏报以精详，裁證揣摩之警敏，声猷期远，知烛益隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237022_comment'></div>擢杞梓之卿材，登瑚琏之国器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237022_comment'></div>克家有裕，显拜攸宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237022_comment'></div>籀仰椒兰异芬，愧蒹葭缪倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237022_comment'></div>连舆并席，琢磨益友之陪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237022_comment'></div>会弁挥犀，磊落德星之聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237022_comment'></div>过逢无间，鄙吝自消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237022_comment'></div>咏味之诚，敷述曷究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1237022_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　薛弼为福建安抚使，苏籀作牋。作品：《牋薛帅》<div id='poem_1237001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺薛帅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237001")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237001'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237001'>伏念亲仰楷模，曩日朝右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237001_comment'></div>屡觌轩驭，趋诣门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237001_comment'></div>圭璋宜瑞于宸廷，符节每翔于外镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237001_comment'></div>蹉跎冗吏，遵禀下尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237001_comment'></div>庥大府而承流，簉小邦之倅乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237001_comment'></div>属尔更代之始，唐突典记之曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237001_comment'></div>夤缘恃旧而冒闻，寖露狂斐而无避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237001_comment'></div>伏惟某官英概特立，几识挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237001_comment'></div>文武兼资，负澄清济物之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237001_comment'></div>中外迭晋，有倜傥曜世之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237001_comment'></div>牧害马而伏驯，俾乱丝之条理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237001_comment'></div>才艺第一，当冠从臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237001_comment'></div>政术绝优，久淹侯社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237001_comment'></div>近者海邦骚动，以资略而任分忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237001_comment'></div>军阃咨诹，膺统督而奠要剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237001_comment'></div>金珂画角，殄蜂蚁于立谈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237001_comment'></div>羽檄捷书，剿蛇鼠于薰灌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237001_comment'></div>八州调护，三方悉平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237001_comment'></div>信庙堂之知人，寤冕旒之念绩，即隆名器，以答勋勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237001_comment'></div>稠叠褒嘉，殊常眷瞩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237001_comment'></div>方且析介圭而遄觐，穿豹尾之清班，被卓尔之殊恩，赞郁乎之文治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237001_comment'></div>籀贪藉辉荫，乐奉教条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237001_comment'></div>祈方隅永逸之规，觊幕府从长之画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237001_comment'></div>衷情向往，竿牍莫陈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1237001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　辛酉，高宗亲耕藉田，苏籀作贺表。作品：《代贺亲耕藉田表》<div id='poem_1236950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺亲耕耤田表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236950")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236950'>省耕千亩之甸，亲御三推之仪，断揉斯勤，齐祓与祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236950_comment'></div>恻怛宸旨，溥率域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236950_comment'></div>荣观日新，圣风云靡<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236950_comment'></div>窃以衣食王业之要，思文后稷之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236950_comment'></div>皇极建而五福敷，烝人粒而万邦乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236950_comment'></div>曩昔艰难之际，扰徙安业之农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236950_comment'></div>故敦奉为寰宇先，盖未祈而造物相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236950_comment'></div>会通典礼，底豫神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236950_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下，存信去兵，纳民轨物，躬行舜禹之急务，力致宗庙之洁丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236950_comment'></div>兴起弥文，笃纂前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236950_comment'></div>诞降嘉种，至治馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236950_comment'></div>如坻如京，以孝以享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236950_comment'></div>近弼硕彦，调燮富民之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236950_comment'></div>列郡循良，申严力穑之课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236950_comment'></div>户户乐生而劝善，人人举趾而授时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236950_comment'></div>天瑞地符，家给国阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236950_comment'></div>臣究宣德意，眇汉仪之六条；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236950_comment'></div>遵禀化原，迈唐贤之八计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236950_comment'></div>万耦于耜，九土载芟，偕生逊畔之心，咸革惰游之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236950_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1236950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月</a>　有奏札。作品：《务农札子》<div id='poem_1236954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>务农劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236954")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236954'>臣闻王政之先，务农为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236954_comment'></div>观周公《豳风》所陈，后稷以来，田畯耜馌，斧斨蚕桑，重穋涤场，玄黄绩褐，想见先王爱利厚生之叙，慨然稼穑艰难、小人之咨者，《思文》之粒烝民，底于道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236954_comment'></div>古之治财者非一孔，笼货算缗，运米敛积，甚勤且裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236954_comment'></div>而周公所陈，渊源深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236954_comment'></div>珠玉泉货，寒不可衣，饥不可食，有补饥寒而至重者，粟帛也，二者不充，则它财无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236954_comment'></div>盖禾不天降，非民力不生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236954_comment'></div>缣不地涌，非民工不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236954_comment'></div>今陛下帑藏出于租税，每岁禄廪军宾以百万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236954_comment'></div>五年之蓄，九年之备，殆其可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236954_comment'></div>自昔承平，诸路之赋常不能自给，素所仰者，东南数十郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236954_comment'></div>今淮南往往为斥堠之郊，罕复种植，赋入惟恃二浙而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236954_comment'></div>吴地海陵之仓，天下莫及，税稻再熟，贡绵八蚕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236954_comment'></div>方今缣绮之美不下齐鲁，又增以鹾镪笼榷之盛，夫复何加？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236954_comment'></div>白丁红女，终身丝谷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236954_comment'></div>伍符尺籍，尽力边疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236954_comment'></div>行阵者无暇播穑，南亩者甘心馈饷，二者互相养卫，田夫必亿兆于甲士，犁牛必百倍于战马，而后济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236954_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236954_comment'></div>孰与温饱天下而富强邦国，非农也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236954_comment'></div>四民之最苦辛，三务之最劳剧，苟宽裕其生生之业，则士商工及末务者亦不匮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236954_comment'></div>臣窃惟先圣有敦本兴王之要道，田里之安，恃贤守令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236954_comment'></div>亦不必其躬行阡陌以为劝课，惟科敛正辞，恻怛务实，使民养生送死无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236954_comment'></div>人心悦则阴阳和，阴阳和而天下平，于是风雨时若，耕织咸遂，殆其庶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236954_comment'></div>太公言宽民之目曰：「利之而勿害，成之而勿败，生之而勿杀，与之而勿夺，乐之而勿苦，喜之而勿怒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236954_comment'></div>夫如是，地无遗利，家有羡馀，县官岂在加赋侵牟而后足用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236954_comment'></div>闾阎困乏，则邦本不固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236954_comment'></div>姑令有司量入为出，出纳之间，不失钦慎，岁计时办，裁抑浮冗，累岁均省，必致京坻之丰，山岳之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236954_comment'></div>带甲百万，陈锡周洽，篚实盈溢，民有蓄藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236954_comment'></div>谷缣虽钜万，不以为家赀数，虽公私咸有九年之积可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236954_comment'></div>礼义益敦，风化益厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236954_comment'></div>陛下待遇守令，赏罚以其勤惰于民，才否必由民之谤誉，谁敢不尽力哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236954_comment'></div>尝闻汉人推衍盐铁条目之说至数十万言，亦是裨益邦家之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236954_comment'></div>臣谓习读诗书，敦本而末茂矣，儒家仁富，与霸道固异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236954_comment'></div>臣不胜区区，越职昧死以闻，伏惟圣明裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236954_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1236954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年5月</a>　五月丙寅，高宗生日，百官上寿于紫宸殿，苏籀作疏文。作品：《天申圣节疏》<div id='poem_1237072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天申圣节疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237072")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237072'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237072'>千龄圣瑞，运叶亨嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237072_comment'></div>四海乐推，道隆康济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237072_comment'></div>虔假三乘之妙，鸿延万寿之祺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237072_comment'></div>凡庶同词，普天善祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237072_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下乾健不息，离明正中，仁增益高，施博弥溥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237072_comment'></div>受天之禄，如川方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237072_comment'></div>雪复神州，绥靖华夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237072_comment'></div>永御无疆之历，固安不拔之基。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1237072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1146')">1145-1146年</a>　在绍兴。有跋文。作品：《跋任氏东坡诗及所书黄门记》《跋般若心经后》<div id='poem_1237047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋任氏东坡诗及所书黄门记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237047")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237047'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237047'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237047_comment'></div>二祖道德之范，见于笔墨，传示来世，不容拟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237047_comment'></div>观其述二大夫乐贤之意，炳然著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237047_comment'></div>辨书真赝，仆粗能焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237047_comment'></div>古人谓辞之不可已，故黾勉而题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237047_comment'></div>是岁九月丙辰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1237047_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋般若心经后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十六年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237048")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237048'>佛告舍利佛般若第一义谛，无心而成正觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237048_comment'></div>初祖国师颂释，益晓然，即群迷为圣智，照大闇为光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237048_comment'></div>众生勤念本源自性，由此致悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237048_comment'></div>颍川元辅意珠融通，斋心所书，虔奉《般若》，志愿笃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237048_comment'></div>以梵夹示余，欲彼此同證善果，不容无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237048_comment'></div>绍兴丙寅岁首夏中休日，眉山苏籀题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1237048_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　书黄庭坚、秦观、晁补之三人《长短句新集》题跋。作品：《书三学士<长短句新集>后》<div id='poem_1237049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书三学士长短句新集后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237049")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237049'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237049'>予晚生，希仰前修，汇汲与能，耳目屡接典刑故老，喜幸如获麟凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237049_comment'></div>餍于昏懵不知而作者，论文拊卷，每每兴叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237049_comment'></div>顾念九原莫作，述者有迹可传，不忍置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237049_comment'></div>曩日正始群贤在朝，黄、秦、晁三公骞翔台阁，追想其奏篇大廷，垂绅文陛，据梧挥犀，石渠、东观，质据辨析，泯然邈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237049_comment'></div>所馀著书，名章大论，炜煌照世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237049_comment'></div>其樽俎折冲，款昵名胜，高酬妍倡，以使酒寓意，融金石、感鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237049_comment'></div>咸韶虽隐，《阳春白雪》犹将彷佛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237049_comment'></div>其风流雅尚之最，吾人所欲珍辑，寔天下奇韵嘉闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237049_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237049_comment'></div>东阿《豆萁》之敏，子敬《蚕种》之墨，渊明《閒情》之赋，三公度曲，与此何远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237049_comment'></div>尝窃评之：黄太史纤秾精稳，体趣天出，简切流美，能中之能，投弃锜斧，有佩玉之雍容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237049_comment'></div>秦校理落尽畦畛，天心月胁，逸格超绝，妙中之妙，议者谓前无伦而后无继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237049_comment'></div>晁南宫平处言近文缓，高处新规胜致，朱弦三叹，斐丽音旨，自成一种姿致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237049_comment'></div>概考其才识，皆内重而外物轻，淳至旷达，学无所遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237049_comment'></div>水镜万象，谢遣势利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237049_comment'></div>湔祓陈俚，发为新雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237049_comment'></div>有谓寓言，罕能名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237049_comment'></div>三公同明相照，并驾而驰，声称彰灼于天下，斯文经纬乎一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237049_comment'></div>淟涊萎敝、剽裂无稽之徒熄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237049_comment'></div>吾侪鲰生，讽咏喁噞，刿目娱心，痼文字之癖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237049_comment'></div>昔谢安石中年伤于悲欢，与亲友别，作数日恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237049_comment'></div>王右军曰：「正赖丝竹陶写耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237049_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237049_comment'></div>吉日良宵，宾主酣饫，笙簧嘈杂，使旷世纤阿之伦，求语意之相类，穷音调之抑扬，上激青云，荡泄吾辈胸怀，所谓陶写也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237049_comment'></div>杨恽「耳热乌乌」，梁鸿《五噫》狂歌，亦茫渺耳，乌能逮此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1237049_comment'></div>或曰：「耳非夔、牙，安知幻妙之音」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1237049_comment'></div>答曰：三公之词，非专玩而独鉴者，实四海九州有识之士共焉，故予言而不僭越耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1237049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在绍兴。有文。作品：《迎吴郎中启》《回发解举人启》<div id='poem_1237002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎吴郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237002")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237002'>伏审明纶妙擢，廉按详刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237002_comment'></div>观览风俗之宜，布宣诏令之意，凝霜被节，甘泽随车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237002_comment'></div>凡在庇庥，咸怀钦跂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237002_comment'></div>伏惟提刑中大郎中体履穹懿，持操渊澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237002_comment'></div>发远韵于朱弦，洒清飙于兰雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237002_comment'></div>国梁栋而民仪准，《诗》老成而《易》丈人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237002_comment'></div>棠阴遗爱于东山，驿乘全临于闽部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237002_comment'></div>要涂粉省，显除星列于台中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237002_comment'></div>直指绣衣，威望震雄于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237002_comment'></div>俨范会之端委，致绿林之惊奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237002_comment'></div>入境抗旌，远迩胥悦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237002_comment'></div>出教属邑，民吏肃雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237002_comment'></div>蟠错识评，喻若秋荼之密；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237002_comment'></div>游刃辩画，温然冬日之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237002_comment'></div>清节不群，庙堂翕予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237002_comment'></div>召期非远，宸扆柬能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237002_comment'></div>遄讲道而横经，峻持橐而簪笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237002_comment'></div>籀尘劳冗吏，漂寓衰踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237002_comment'></div>引领使尘，先景星而快睹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237002_comment'></div>依归民誉，仰高山之诚勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237002_comment'></div>欣慕之深，造次罔述<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷一三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237002_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1237002'>东：原缺，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1237002_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回发解举人谢启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237003")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237003'>伏审秋闱遴选，擢芳廉秀之林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237003_comment'></div>贡籍能书，驰骛青冥之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237003_comment'></div>有司乐育，乡党推贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237003_comment'></div>枉沐笺题，过垂宠诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237003_comment'></div>伏惟解元先辈研六籍之魁士，奋一上于英躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237003_comment'></div>唾手云衢，仙桂空于月窟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237003_comment'></div>荣观玉笋，风雷化于春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237003_comment'></div>劝驾及期，公堂受遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237003_comment'></div>颂咏之恳，敷述奚殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237003_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1237003_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f3f199e4d6db4d4192c8eb36a27842f6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f3f199e4d6db4d4192c8eb36a27842f6");'><span id='f3f199e4d6db4d4192c8eb36a27842f6_link'
