href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　苏籀移通判衢州，有致知府张舍人书。作品：《衢州张舍人启》<div id='poem_1237004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州张舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237004")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237004'>伏念近者解龟新命，易倅大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237004_comment'></div>值中和乐职之秋，属右移更代之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237004_comment'></div>愿附青云之素，敢陪皂盖之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237004_comment'></div>天幸适然，官途优调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237004_comment'></div>伏遇知府舍人待制文盟艺苑，人瑞国华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237004_comment'></div>早副眷求，极当年之柬倚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237004_comment'></div>分忧重委，付陪辅之屏藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237004_comment'></div>奉计虽许于三年，伟业且抟于九万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237004_comment'></div>高嶷忠肃，悉振起乎懦媮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237004_comment'></div>公大懿醇，不苟沽于名誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237004_comment'></div>钤键惟谨，薤水兴谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237004_comment'></div>优柔贵胜之薮渊，敦崇礼义于防范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237004_comment'></div>籀飘萍流寓，弹铗归来，依投吏道之宗师，仰止词林之根蒂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237004_comment'></div>所祈寡陋，尚幸烛微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237004_comment'></div>向慕之诚，敷染曷既<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷一三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237004_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1237004'>早：原缺，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1237004_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　在衢州，致前任林通判书。作品：《衢州交代林通判启》<div id='poem_1237005' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237005' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237005?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州交代林通判启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237005")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237005_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237005'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237005'>伏念昔陪朝籍，并趋位著之联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237005_comment'></div>恳避换州，祇践仁明之躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237005_comment'></div>自惟尘迹，每获云庥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237005_comment'></div>伏遇交代通判寺丞冠冕朝伦，圭璋民表，修饰治绩，竦振能声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237005_comment'></div>英妙贰州，孰出高能之右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237005_comment'></div>代移更戍，敢咨旧政之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237005_comment'></div>驰耸清规，欣趋幸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237005_comment'></div>扬剑津之糠秕，实赖同尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237005_comment'></div>袭柯山之芝兰，自兹借润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237005_comment'></div>愿交之恳，染翰曷殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1237005_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　苏籀谒庙，有祭文。作品：《谒庙文》<div id='poem_1237069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237069")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237069'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237069'>籀奉朝命，贰州治中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237069_comment'></div>视事之初，虔谒祠下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237069_comment'></div>惭其菲荐，冀达忱诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237069_comment'></div>惟恃聪直，罔不庇鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237069_comment'></div>庶几学道及物，魔障永除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237069_comment'></div>私门咸宁，灵蚃攸赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237069_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1237069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年11月</a>　敷文阁直学士赵不弃自临安移知绍兴府，苏籀作文。作品：《牋赵敷文》<div id='poem_1237019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺赵敷文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237019")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237019'>伏念尘冒朝抡，升陪镇幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237019_comment'></div>骤跻官局，祗竦轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237019_comment'></div>尝偕部吏于计台，复俾咨谋于宾佐，顾省枵闇，但益兢营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237019_comment'></div>清冷慢闲之具员，矜烛宁存之攸庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237019_comment'></div>伏惟知府安抚敷文风绩开济，资略凝和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237019_comment'></div>实德施为，金声玉振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237019_comment'></div>思谟献纳，绣口锦心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237019_comment'></div>平时魏雒之阃旄，广内宸奎之隶职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237019_comment'></div>赫寅车而问俗，允宗望以维翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237019_comment'></div>著劳输挽于日畿，腾价浩穰于天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237019_comment'></div>前后渊衷之柬，崇隆物望之孚，卒乘辑和，吏民信惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237019_comment'></div>素承眷瞩之遇，遂擢回翔之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237019_comment'></div>治声径达于九重，朝宁遄追于三节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237019_comment'></div>超持橐之选，正书殿之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237019_comment'></div>籀流落羁伧，侵寻晚迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237019_comment'></div>矫首桑枌之邈，介怀釜庾之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237019_comment'></div>力任职之罔隳，愿事贤之良幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237019_comment'></div>欣属之切，敷染曷宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1237019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年9月</a>　俞俟知绍兴府，苏籀作书。作品：《牋俞帅》<div id='poem_1237012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺俞帅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237012")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237012'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237012'>恭审寿咨文陛，均秩东藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237012_comment'></div>巍峨节制之尊，雄毅抚绥之略，声腾族望，欢溢搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237012_comment'></div>矧叨庇于属城，寔素承于风旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237012_comment'></div>恭惟某官元龟先识，隆栋宏材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237012_comment'></div>道契千龄，雅被宸扆之注；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237012_comment'></div>志存一节，夙扬康济之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237012_comment'></div>辍内朝清切之班，体中制丁宁之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237012_comment'></div>顷居辇毂，著浩穰弹压之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237012_comment'></div>旋总藩维，妙宣布中和之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237012_comment'></div>适交留籥之近，益高分陕之釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237012_comment'></div>惟会计之名邦，控东南之要地，必资全德，尽护列城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237012_comment'></div>阅礼乐而敦诗书，寅车元老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237012_comment'></div>兼文武而储将相，两府上公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237012_comment'></div>籀夙荷恩知，欣闻大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237012_comment'></div>敢图幸会，获备官僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237012_comment'></div>负韊前驱，阻趋瞻于棨戟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237012_comment'></div>寓书拜问，但仰托于云天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237012_comment'></div>欣颂之私，敷陈罔既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1237012_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　迎衢州新知府章氏，作启。作品：《迎衢州知府章郎中》<div id='poem_1237006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎衢州知府章郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237006")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237006'>伏审诏恩成命，授委休嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237006_comment'></div>畿辅殿邦，清选英重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237006_comment'></div>地接行朝之次舍，民孚邻境之甘棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237006_comment'></div>持节斯来，柅车允治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237006_comment'></div>伏惟知府郎中蚤鶱翔于廷右，久佚乐于侯封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237006_comment'></div>冠门阀于云霄，俨朝绅之领袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237006_comment'></div>粉闱回首，启台阁之荣涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237006_comment'></div>金节按澄，肃峤泷之憬俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237006_comment'></div>根艺学于敏识，裕风力于繁难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237006_comment'></div>详谛通方，警拔适当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237006_comment'></div>功名显宠，方且鼎来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237006_comment'></div>岳镇藩隅，匪稽峻陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237006_comment'></div>籀稔聆华闻，尝叩铃斋，既周旋于惠慈，又贬枉于音诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237006_comment'></div>不意抗尘之迹，缪叨别乘之荣，照瞩所因，参陪良幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237006_comment'></div>颂咏之切，攀述罔殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1237006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在衢州通判任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　在衢州。有文。作品：《跋伯时二马图》《书王维<辋川图>后》《回江少卿启》《婺州钱龙图》《迎吴中大》《牋吴尚书》《徐漕启》《牋周尚书》《谢高市舶启》《迎贺曹漕启》《贺提举游郎中》<div id='poem_1237050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋伯时二马图<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十一年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237050")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237050'>先祖黄门喜顾、陆、王、韩遗迹，龙眠集三马见贻，效之者三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237050_comment'></div>其风仪雄杰，皆可任双钺，三槐所驭，殆天厩之龙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237050_comment'></div>兵火后，粉绘羽化，惟丝字赓唱在椟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237050_comment'></div>今观此髣髴间，感旧屡慨而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237050_comment'></div>绍兴辛未秋孟，苏籀跋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1237050_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237007?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回江少卿启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237007")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237007'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237007'>伏念引嫌避地，换镇监州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237007_comment'></div>邦国不空，众倚贤侯为重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237007_comment'></div>狱市所寄，分安俗吏之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237007_comment'></div>九棘移书，五云拜贶，辉华蔀室，喜动蓬心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237007_comment'></div>伏惟宫使中大少卿炎汉子真之才华，西晋稚川之襟趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237007_comment'></div>资清秩峻，羽仪平陟于天京；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237007_comment'></div>礼备乐纯，剑履周旋于郊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237007_comment'></div>天将降任，身享寿康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237007_comment'></div>谱牒前闻，继起葳蕤于贤业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237007_comment'></div>搢绅推予，声华籍甚于班联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237007_comment'></div>琳馆湛研，丹台密迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237007_comment'></div>籀臞儒自哂，晚宦思归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237007_comment'></div>布气嘘枯，曩祈受诀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237007_comment'></div>建言发瞆，敢望灵方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237007_comment'></div>丐闻霄壤之始元，无碍窔奥之荧爝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1237007_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺婺州钱龙图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237008")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237008'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237008'>伏审光膺选倚，荣奉蕃宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237008_comment'></div>冠内阁之宠名，专辅邦之重镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237008_comment'></div>辍耳目之杰，殿股肱之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237008_comment'></div>偃伏英风，翘竦硕望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237008_comment'></div>恭惟知府龙图大中有毗翊奋起之绩，得功名显达之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237008_comment'></div>天授众才，世承丕德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237008_comment'></div>焕文华而外发，励公实以衷强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237008_comment'></div>进自结于睿聪，退仰酬于柬任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237008_comment'></div>裕民足国，无非远图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237008_comment'></div>宣化承流，更观共理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237008_comment'></div>跋兹宝婺，祐我台躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237008_comment'></div>赏心坐啸于新亭，游刃发硎于馀地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237008_comment'></div>柅车未几，舆诵弥佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237008_comment'></div>必奉玺书，将膺冕服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237008_comment'></div>籀旧族衰裔，薄宦孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237008_comment'></div>曩贯籍于剑南，今侨寓于浙左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237008_comment'></div>仰高平夙，幸恭梓以焉穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237008_comment'></div>府贰拘縻，从贺宾而独阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237008_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1237008_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237011' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237011?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎吴中大启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237011")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237011'>伏审昨被诏除，近釐符守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237011_comment'></div>任优旧德，荣屈雅才，凡百为僚，允出幸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237011_comment'></div>伏惟知府中大公清良弼，方重嘉谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237011_comment'></div>文采风流，蚤作藩桓之贵客；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237011_comment'></div>咨诹策画，屡当帷幄之折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237011_comment'></div>历试烦难，愈新闻望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237011_comment'></div>覃布美怀于封部，润饰文儒于教条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237011_comment'></div>矧夫剑百鍊而缮藏，自能应手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237011_comment'></div>骥千金而增价，何必问途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237011_comment'></div>器博省台，抱本朝之雅意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237011_comment'></div>能高惠养，察里落之嚬呻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237011_comment'></div>不鄙小邦，稍恢馀刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237011_comment'></div>籀趋风关陕，假盖荆襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237011_comment'></div>倒指计两星之终，飞书陈二天之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237011_comment'></div>慕前修之牧相，甘棠匪遥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237011_comment'></div>恃畴夙之陪游，蒹葭缪倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237011_comment'></div>愿际和同之美，允为鲁钝之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237011_comment'></div>钦咏之衷，敷述奚既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1237011_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺吴尚书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237009")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237009'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237009'>伏审光膺诏命，再莅雄藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237009_comment'></div>棠郊争跂于仪刑，绛帐乐从于辩画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237009_comment'></div>以常伯之夙望，副旧德之精求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237009_comment'></div>好音布腾，惠风翕若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237009_comment'></div>伏惟某官慈仁无扰，柔辑警明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237009_comment'></div>勤恤素闻于天聪，爱惠久洽于民誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237009_comment'></div>端靖而密，温温法从之宗工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237009_comment'></div>鸿博而文，嶷嶷儒林之先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237009_comment'></div>雅韵常优于厚俗，耆哲乃宜于牧人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237009_comment'></div>盖源远而流清，由形直而影正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237009_comment'></div>方且来宣美意，班宽大之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237009_comment'></div>感奋猷为，歌中和之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237009_comment'></div>寖结深知于黄屋，岂淹挥翰于紫宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237009_comment'></div>虎符一麾，召擢伊迩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237009_comment'></div>鹏程九万，资略难量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237009_comment'></div>籀侨籍治城，特纡顾盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237009_comment'></div>其为抃怿，实逾等伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237009_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1237009_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>示徐漕启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1236984")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236984'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236984'>伏以命秩日边，假羽翰而干进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236984_comment'></div>论评月旦，辱謦欬而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236984_comment'></div>堂室高坚，岂易钻仰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236984_comment'></div>门目浩博，靡或不收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236984_comment'></div>惟糺按黜陟之间，有办治公清之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236984_comment'></div>悉取髦彦，奚顾循常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236984_comment'></div>籀自媒包羞，冒渎贻诮，足将前而退却，口欲说而嗫嚅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236984_comment'></div>免于谴弹，为惠已甚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236984_comment'></div>尘于观听，负愧实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236984_comment'></div>黾勉衷情，曲折布露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236984_comment'></div>五仕委命，七稔书劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236984_comment'></div>忧患乘陵，岁月二纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236984_comment'></div>兵戈迁徙，道里百程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236984_comment'></div>大丧其家，栖托无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236984_comment'></div>熊落于槛，攀援奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236984_comment'></div>世方须才，时属多事，愿翊皇舆乎正路，仍拯生类于穷途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236984_comment'></div>事国激昂之心，孤愤曷已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236984_comment'></div>陈力衰贱之际，守局胡为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236984_comment'></div>冀高位之仁人，拔孤迹于要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236984_comment'></div>尚古人之不苟禄，幸君子之弗遐遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236984_comment'></div>庶曰非愚，尝试甄宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236984_comment'></div>伏惟某官廓度量于河海，铄风采于云烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236984_comment'></div>致主忧民，奉法循理，并用周臣之五善，尽遵汉诏之六条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236984_comment'></div>望隆蕃宣，誉振岳牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236984_comment'></div>儒显当代，宜冠从班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236984_comment'></div>课最诸州，即归朝右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236984_comment'></div>妙郊、岛为馀事，纂班、左之遗芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236984_comment'></div>题品则林宗、子将，知识则鲍叔、罕虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236984_comment'></div>铢称寸度，不失毫分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236984_comment'></div>弦急韦柔，悉承旨趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236984_comment'></div>再念籀少也狂简，便慕相如之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236984_comment'></div>老矣不才，窃附子臧之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236984_comment'></div>求而后值，喜同时之有若人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236984_comment'></div>漫不知非，推等列之多美士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236984_comment'></div>铨选冗琐，难以发其器能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236984_comment'></div>民政设施，粗可崇其术业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236984_comment'></div>保持无吝，补报是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236984_comment'></div>称于天下曰己知，游扬令闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236984_comment'></div>登于王朝而引达，果决当仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1236984_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237010?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺周尚书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237010")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237010_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237010'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237010'>伏审光膺褒诏，宠畀近藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237010_comment'></div>东浙虚股肱之邦，中台辍喉舌之老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237010_comment'></div>搢绅遵承而翕若，吏民豫附以讴谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237010_comment'></div>遐竦车尘，驰想旌棨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237010_comment'></div>伏惟某官窥古今之奥，适时务之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237010_comment'></div>超冠素云之曹，寤柬隆赫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237010_comment'></div>摄空清鉴之长，注倚精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237010_comment'></div>爵秩逢年而九迁，才具一日而千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237010_comment'></div>委重文昌之枢要，望邻公衮之民瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237010_comment'></div>究宣周变之能，加崇牧伯之柄，俞音甚渥，召节俯颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237010_comment'></div>籀听郑履于朝端，尝获亲近；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237010_comment'></div>买龚犊于部内，实赖惠慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237010_comment'></div>仰存诲之夤缘，形庇庥之僭冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237010_comment'></div>其为欣幸，殆逾等伦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1237010_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢高市舶启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237013")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237013'>伏念肃旄钺之高门，夙侍先府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237013_comment'></div>迓霜台之叱驭，欣耀皇华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237013_comment'></div>获佐藩条于海隅，遵奉约束于部内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237013_comment'></div>仰睎云荫，延颈日畿，祗服威尊，寖露狂斐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237013_comment'></div>想望伊迩，候问敢稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237013_comment'></div>伏惟某官详雅博通，高明独胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237013_comment'></div>名行兼著，可谓克家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237013_comment'></div>义利咸和，所祈足国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237013_comment'></div>莳兰玉于阶闼，作杞梓于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237013_comment'></div>究观拔擢之新，行听旌酬之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237013_comment'></div>赆琛角齿，骈蕃充牣于载输；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237013_comment'></div>蛮獠贾胡，竭蹶趋承于表饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237013_comment'></div>公储积珍贝之夥，属郡殚驽蹇之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237013_comment'></div>虽不及物而享多仪，盖知取予而获其宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237013_comment'></div>籀希功展效，缮性虑才，敢不尽心，祈于成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237013_comment'></div>缉熙勤恪，稍纡旷瘝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237013_comment'></div>无任归向宗仰之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1237013_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237014?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎贺曹漕启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237014")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237014'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237014'>伏审宠被俞诏，召擢计台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237014_comment'></div>亲柬渊衷，阶廷无右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237014_comment'></div>澄清畿辅，耳目任颛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237014_comment'></div>邸音骤誊，封境钦肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237014_comment'></div>大庇宗瞩，佥论允怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237014_comment'></div>伏惟都运大卿智术兼人，风采名世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237014_comment'></div>藉甚华腴之规范，声驰烜赫之闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237014_comment'></div>早卿月以扬辉，荐侯藩而称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237014_comment'></div>人门并美，诚第一流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237014_comment'></div>资略俱高，省察六事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237014_comment'></div>高选剧任，督课租庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237014_comment'></div>居止止以凝祥，治优优乎投刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237014_comment'></div>阜民体国，蔚循拊之文移；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237014_comment'></div>博古知今，妙飞挽之纤悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237014_comment'></div>方且进思毗副乎文石之陛，洞澈均敛乎善最之筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237014_comment'></div>惠恤周流，莫非岂弟之赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237014_comment'></div>盈虚调一，必极大受之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237014_comment'></div>卓卓忠劳，巍巍奖拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237014_comment'></div>籀莫窥墙仞，详谛风裁，冒尊府之威棱，具小夫之敝牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237014_comment'></div>庆颂之臆，敷述奚殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1237014_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1237015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺提举游郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237015")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237015'>伏审朝抡柬委，使指擢贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237015_comment'></div>叱驭都门，扬舲浙浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237015_comment'></div>旌节光华乎境部，符移鼓动于属城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237015_comment'></div>辱在馀庥，倍增系慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237015_comment'></div>恭惟提举郎中学术渊懿，资禀清醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237015_comment'></div>达邦克家，所履甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237015_comment'></div>丛剧颛任，乐职飞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237015_comment'></div>閤府倚其酌斟，便殿闻斯献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237015_comment'></div>骛青霄之径路，储卿月之平迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237015_comment'></div>澄揽事重于他司，管榷权尊于迩日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237015_comment'></div>课绩赫奕，诹度敏详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237015_comment'></div>蕴柔嘉弓冶之世修，宣临遣丝纶之诏意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237015_comment'></div>伫膺大受，岂云小知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237015_comment'></div>籀毗赞铢分，夙承顾接，体仁人求瘼之画，效鲰生荐藻之衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1237015_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　迎衢州新任知府吴某。作品：《迎吴大中启》<div id='poem_1237002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迎吴郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237002")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237002'>伏审明纶妙擢，廉按详刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237002_comment'></div>观览风俗之宜，布宣诏令之意，凝霜被节，甘泽随车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237002_comment'></div>凡在庇庥，咸怀钦跂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237002_comment'></div>伏惟提刑中大郎中体履穹懿，持操渊澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237002_comment'></div>发远韵于朱弦，洒清飙于兰雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237002_comment'></div>国梁栋而民仪准，《诗》老成而《易》丈人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237002_comment'></div>棠阴遗爱于东山，驿乘全临于闽部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237002_comment'></div>要涂粉省，显除星列于台中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237002_comment'></div>直指绣衣，威望震雄于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237002_comment'></div>俨范会之端委，致绿林之惊奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237002_comment'></div>入境抗旌，远迩胥悦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237002_comment'></div>出教属邑，民吏肃雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237002_comment'></div>蟠错识评，喻若秋荼之密；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237002_comment'></div>游刃辩画，温然冬日之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237002_comment'></div>清节不群，庙堂翕予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237002_comment'></div>召期非远，宸扆柬能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237002_comment'></div>遄讲道而横经，峻持橐而簪笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237002_comment'></div>籀尘劳冗吏，漂寓衰踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237002_comment'></div>引领使尘，先景星而快睹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237002_comment'></div>依归民誉，仰高山之诚勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237002_comment'></div>欣慕之深，造次罔述<span class='inlineComment2'>（《双溪集》卷一三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237002_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1237002'>东：原缺，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1237002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年2月</a>　春雪，作诗。作品：《壬申春雪一绝》<div id='poem_139586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_139586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/139586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬申春雪一绝</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_139586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_139586'>长天顿改楚云容，初夕依微后搅空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_139586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_139586'>点缀柳条纷若絮，未妨梅蕊衒芳丛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_139586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_139586'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_139586_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　婺州新守赵到任，苏籀作书。作品：《牋婺守赵殿撰》<div id='poem_1237017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺婺守赵殿撰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237017")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237017'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237017'>窃以壤地相邻，闽、浙贰邦之幸会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237017_comment'></div>桑枌依赖，龚、黄统理之攸宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237017_comment'></div>宝婺奥区，兽符重镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237017_comment'></div>屏翰陪辅，撰述枫宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237017_comment'></div>英英秘殿之迩联，显显雄藩之妙柬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237017_comment'></div>股肱谋帅，莫如已试之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237017_comment'></div>宗属维城，所赖分忧之切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237017_comment'></div>宽柔侨寓，允属仁慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237017_comment'></div>伏惟知府殿撰朝望颙卬，天枝标的，温文足学，美政殊称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237017_comment'></div>爱棠前荫以重临，衒裤诧襦而来莫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237017_comment'></div>倚成取办，儒雅裕然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237017_comment'></div>摩拊惠来，德泽滂被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237017_comment'></div>佳誉腾溢于乡校，英声速达于明光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237017_comment'></div>诺凤尾以疏恩，持荷橐而非晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237017_comment'></div>清涂寖启，伟绩弥隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237017_comment'></div>籀郑重承庥，阔疏望履，缄题捧辱，琼玖非珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237017_comment'></div>绛帐溪堂，愿辈侪朋而请益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237017_comment'></div>板扉蔀屋，已分恬妥于私庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237017_comment'></div>恳咏之诚，敷述奚既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1237017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年3月</a>　三月丙辰，曹泳知绍兴府，苏籀作牋。作品：《牋绍兴曹帅》<div id='poem_1237018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237018?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺绍兴曹帅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237018")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237018'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237018'>伏念珍仰达尊，恪倾依于雄屏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237018_comment'></div>呻呼么末，不虚附于青云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237018_comment'></div>竦庆高牙，拜笺东镇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237018_comment'></div>羁栖侨籍，待次属州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237018_comment'></div>未遑诣前，方此潜退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237018_comment'></div>抱寸诚之恳激，缄渺邈以荐闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237018_comment'></div>贱疵渎尊，尪孱借势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237018_comment'></div>伏幸忠恕，未赐谴诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237018_comment'></div>恭惟知府安抚敷文展干邦器能，挺王臣才节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237018_comment'></div>台阁钦崇乎章奏，兵民信惮其纲条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237018_comment'></div>显绩天开，压伏诸镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237018_comment'></div>权机先范，素负英猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237018_comment'></div>孜孜抚循，汲汲理化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237018_comment'></div>四明报政，九牧飏声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237018_comment'></div>宜居浩剧之司，实藉颖脱之手，朝论注瞩，柬擢眷优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237018_comment'></div>今时魏雒之藩翰，畴夙丞疑之符阃，倚遇卓绝，恩华迈伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237018_comment'></div>允副佥谐，保釐丕柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237018_comment'></div>琐琐舞雩之子，拳拳溉扫之童，埏陶洪钧，牛马下走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1237018_comment'></div>沐科别而人材长育，不外索而帷幄宽宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1237018_comment'></div>挽引资阶，跂望甄品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1237018_comment'></div>倘辱提携之旧，倍增报塞之衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1237018_comment'></div>一诺千金，阖门万感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1237018_comment'></div>恃闽浙之旧吏，攀桃李之成蹊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1237018_comment'></div>伫伸野谋，更祈佳惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1237018_comment'></div>冒浼之眚，惭汗无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1237018_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年3月</a>　在衢州。有文。作品：《牋赵敷文》<div id='poem_1237019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>笺赵敷文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237019")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237019'>伏念尘冒朝抡，升陪镇幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237019_comment'></div>骤跻官局，祗竦轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237019_comment'></div>尝偕部吏于计台，复俾咨谋于宾佐，顾省枵闇，但益兢营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237019_comment'></div>清冷慢闲之具员，矜烛宁存之攸庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237019_comment'></div>伏惟知府安抚敷文风绩开济，资略凝和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237019_comment'></div>实德施为，金声玉振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1237019_comment'></div>思谟献纳，绣口锦心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1237019_comment'></div>平时魏雒之阃旄，广内宸奎之隶职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1237019_comment'></div>赫寅车而问俗，允宗望以维翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1237019_comment'></div>著劳输挽于日畿，腾价浩穰于天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1237019_comment'></div>前后渊衷之柬，崇隆物望之孚，卒乘辑和，吏民信惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1237019_comment'></div>素承眷瞩之遇，遂擢回翔之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1237019_comment'></div>治声径达于九重，朝宁遄追于三节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1237019_comment'></div>超持橐之选，正书殿之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1237019_comment'></div>籀流落羁伧，侵寻晚迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1237019_comment'></div>矫首桑枌之邈，介怀釜庾之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1237019_comment'></div>力任职之罔隳，愿事贤之良幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1237019_comment'></div>欣属之切，敷染曷宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1237019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　苏籀离任辞衢州，告别诸庙。作品：《衢州辞诸庙文》<div id='poem_1237070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1237070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1237070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州辞诸庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31344, "宋", "苏籀", "poem_title_1237070")'>苏籀</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1237070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1237070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1237070'>避亲改命，暂贰本邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1237070_comment'></div>柅车剧暑，荏苒小春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1237070_comment'></div>聪直鉴庇，首末宁谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1237070_comment'></div>解印奉辞，敢伸虔荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1237070_comment'></div>归诚之恳，伏惟尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1237070_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1237070_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
